FILE: BaseStandardAI.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;

/**
 * Base class for standard AI behavior patterns.
 * Provides common goal registration patterns shared across all species.
 * 
 * Species-specific AI classes can extend this or use its static methods.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: NEW
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8
 */
public class BaseStandardAI {
    
    /**
     * Registers standard AI goals using configuration parameters.
     * This is the basic mob behavior pattern shared across all species.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register goals for
     * @param aiGoals The AI goals configuration from JSON
     */
    public static void registerStandardGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        registerMovementAndMeleeGoals(entity, aiGoals);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerStandardTargetingGoals(entity);
    }

    /**
     * Shared movement and melee attack registration for standard xenomorph AI patterns.
     */
    public static void registerMovementAndMeleeGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerStandardMovementGoals(entity, aiGoals);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerMeleeAttackGoal(entity, 2, aiGoals.meleeAttackSpeed, false);
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers defensive AI goals with modified speeds.
     * Used by defensive entities (like humans) that are more cautious.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register goals for
     * @param aiGoals The AI goals configuration from JSON
     * @param defensiveSpeedMultiplier The multiplier for defensive speed (e.g., 0.8 for slower)
     */
    public static void registerDefensiveGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals, double defensiveSpeedMultiplier) {
        // Register standard movement goals with defensive speed modifications
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerFloatGoal(entity, 1);
        
        // Defensive melee attack - slower, more cautious
        double defensiveAttackSpeed = aiGoals.meleeAttackSpeed * defensiveSpeedMultiplier;
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerMeleeAttackGoal(entity, 2, defensiveAttackSpeed, false);
        
        // Cautious movement - slower, stays near safety
        double defensiveStrollSpeed = aiGoals.strollSpeed * (defensiveSpeedMultiplier * 0.75); // Even slower for movement
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerStrollGoal(entity, 3, defensiveStrollSpeed);
        
        // Standard look range
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerLookAtPlayerGoal(entity, 4, aiGoals.lookAtPlayerRange);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerRandomLookAroundGoal(entity, 5);
        
        // Defensive targeting - only attack when threatened
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerStandardTargetingGoals(entity);
    }
    
    // Private constructor to prevent instantiation
    private BaseStandardAI() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("BaseStandardAI is a utility class and cannot be instantiated");
    }
}

FILE: CommonGoalRegistrar.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.FloatGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.LookAtPlayerGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.MeleeAttackGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.RandomLookAroundGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.RandomStrollGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.WaterAvoidingRandomStrollGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.target.HurtByTargetGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.target.NearestAttackableTargetGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;

/**
 * Utility class for registering common AI goals across all species.
 * Centralizes common goal registration logic to eliminate DRY violations.
 * 
 * This is a generic version that works with any PathfinderMob, not species-specific.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: NEW
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8
 */
public class CommonGoalRegistrar {
    
    /**
     * Registers FloatGoal with specified priority.
     * DRY: Centralizes FloatGoal registration used across all species.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register the goal for
     * @param priority The priority for this goal
     */
    public static void registerFloatGoal(PathfinderMob entity, int priority) {
        entity.goalSelector.addGoal(priority, new FloatGoal(entity));
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers WaterAvoidingRandomStrollGoal with specified priority and speed.
     * DRY: Centralizes stroll goal registration used across all species.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register the goal for
     * @param priority The priority for this goal
     * @param strollSpeed The speed multiplier for strolling
     */
    public static void registerStrollGoal(PathfinderMob entity, int priority, double strollSpeed) {
        entity.goalSelector.addGoal(priority, new WaterAvoidingRandomStrollGoal(entity, strollSpeed));
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers RandomStrollGoal with specified priority, speed, and interval.
     * DRY: Centralizes RandomStrollGoal registration (used when interval control is needed).
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register the goal for
     * @param priority The priority for this goal
     * @param strollSpeed The speed multiplier for strolling
     * @param strollInterval The interval in ticks between stroll attempts
     */
    public static void registerRandomStrollGoal(PathfinderMob entity, int priority, double strollSpeed, int strollInterval) {
        entity.goalSelector.addGoal(priority, new RandomStrollGoal(entity, strollSpeed, strollInterval));
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers LookAtPlayerGoal with specified priority and range.
     * DRY: Centralizes look-at-player goal registration used across all species.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register the goal for
     * @param priority The priority for this goal
     * @param lookRange The range at which to look at players
     */
    public static void registerLookAtPlayerGoal(PathfinderMob entity, int priority, float lookRange) {
        entity.goalSelector.addGoal(priority, new LookAtPlayerGoal(entity, Player.class, lookRange));
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers RandomLookAroundGoal with specified priority.
     * DRY: Centralizes random look-around goal registration used across all species.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register the goal for
     * @param priority The priority for this goal
     */
    public static void registerRandomLookAroundGoal(PathfinderMob entity, int priority) {
        entity.goalSelector.addGoal(priority, new RandomLookAroundGoal(entity));
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers MeleeAttackGoal with specified priority and speed.
     * DRY: Centralizes melee attack goal registration used across all species.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register the goal for
     * @param priority The priority for this goal
     * @param attackSpeed The speed multiplier for attacks
     * @param followTarget Whether to follow the target
     */
    public static void registerMeleeAttackGoal(PathfinderMob entity, int priority, double attackSpeed, boolean followTarget) {
        entity.goalSelector.addGoal(priority, new MeleeAttackGoal(entity, attackSpeed, followTarget));
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers HurtByTargetGoal with specified priority.
     * DRY: Centralizes hurt-by-target goal registration used across all species.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register the goal for
     * @param priority The priority for this goal
     */
    public static void registerHurtByTargetGoal(PathfinderMob entity, int priority) {
        entity.targetSelector.addGoal(priority, new HurtByTargetGoal(entity));
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers NearestAttackableTargetGoal for Player with specified priority.
     * DRY: Centralizes player targeting goal registration used across all species.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register the goal for
     * @param priority The priority for this goal
     * @param checkSight Whether to check line of sight
     */
    public static void registerPlayerTargetGoal(PathfinderMob entity, int priority, boolean checkSight) {
        entity.targetSelector.addGoal(priority, new NearestAttackableTargetGoal<>(entity, Player.class, checkSight));
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers standard movement goals (Float, Stroll, Look).
     * DRY: Centralizes common movement goal pattern used across all species.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register goals for
     * @param aiGoals The AI goals configuration
     */
    public static void registerStandardMovementGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        registerFloatGoal(entity, 1);
        registerStrollGoal(entity, 3, aiGoals.strollSpeed);
        registerLookAtPlayerGoal(entity, 4, aiGoals.lookAtPlayerRange);
        registerRandomLookAroundGoal(entity, 5);
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers standard targeting goals (HurtByTarget, Player).
     * DRY: Centralizes common targeting goal pattern used across all species.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register goals for
     */
    public static void registerStandardTargetingGoals(PathfinderMob entity) {
        registerHurtByTargetGoal(entity, 1);
        registerPlayerTargetGoal(entity, 2, true);
    }
    
    // Private constructor to prevent instantiation
    private CommonGoalRegistrar() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("CommonGoalRegistrar is a utility class and cannot be instantiated");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;

/**
 * Interface for goal registration across all species.
 * Provides a common abstraction for registering AI goals without depending
 * on specific species implementations.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: WIRE-DEFER — no implementors yet; reserved for composition-based goal registration.
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8
 */
public interface GoalRegistry {
    
    /**
     * Registers AI goals for an entity based on its entity type.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register goals for
     * @param entityType The entity type
     */
    void registerGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityType entityType);
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.monster.Monster;

/**
 * Level-0 hook for human goal registration (wired from level_3 at bootstrap).
 */
public final class HumanGoalRegistration {

    private static Consumer<Monster> registrar;

    private HumanGoalRegistration() {
    }

    public static void init(Consumer<Monster> implementation) {
        registrar = Objects.requireNonNull(implementation, "human goal registrar");
    }

    public static void registerGoals(Monster entity) {
        Objects.requireNonNull(registrar, "HumanGoalRegistration not initialized").accept(entity);
    }
}

FILE: NestBuildingGoal.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai;

import java.util.EnumSet;
import java.util.Objects;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.Goal;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.QueenNestProgress;

/**
 * Goal wrapper for nest building — delegates tick/canUse to {@link QueenNestProgress}.
 */
public final class NestBuildingGoal extends Goal {

    private final QueenNestProgress nestProgress;

    public NestBuildingGoal(@Nonnull QueenNestProgress nestProgress) {
        this.nestProgress = nestProgress;
        this.setFlags(Objects.requireNonNull(EnumSet.of(Flag.MOVE, Flag.LOOK)));
    }

    @Override
    public boolean canUse() {
        return !nestProgress.isNestComplete();
    }

    @Override
    public boolean canContinueToUse() {
        return !nestProgress.isNestComplete();
    }

    @Override
    public void tick() {
        nestProgress.tick();
    }

    @Override
    public boolean requiresUpdateEveryTick() {
        return true;
    }
}

FILE: XenomorphTargetRegistry.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Predicate;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.target.NearestAttackableTargetGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.monster.Monster;

/**
 * Registry for xenomorph entity types that humans should target.
 * L3-only: uses {@link NearestAttackableTargetGoal} and {@link Monster} goal registration.
 * Any future target-type catalog (domain keys) may live L0/L2; registration stays here.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: NEW
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8
 */
public class XenomorphTargetRegistry {
    
    /**
     * Interface for registering xenomorph entity targets.
     * Allows species-specific implementations to provide target classes.
     */
    public interface XenomorphTargetProvider {
        /**
         * Gets the class of xenomorph entities to target.
         * 
         * @return The entity class to target
         */
        @Nonnull
        Class<? extends LivingEntity> getTargetClass();
        
        /**
         * Gets the priority for this target goal.
         * Lower numbers = higher priority.
         * 
         * @return The priority
         */
        int getPriority();
    }
    
    private static final List<XenomorphTargetProvider> TARGET_PROVIDERS = new ArrayList<>();
    
    /**
     * Registers a xenomorph target provider.
     * 
     * @param provider The target provider
     */
    public static void registerTarget(@Nonnull XenomorphTargetProvider provider) {
        TARGET_PROVIDERS.add(Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "xenomorph target provider"));
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers all xenomorph target goals for a human entity.
     * 
     * @param human The human entity to register targets for
     */
    public static void registerXenomorphTargets(@Nonnull Monster human) {
        for (XenomorphTargetProvider provider : TARGET_PROVIDERS) {
            human.targetSelector.addGoal(
                provider.getPriority(),
                new NearestAttackableTargetGoal<>(human, provider.getTargetClass(), true));
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers all xenomorph target goals for a human entity with a filter predicate.
     * 
     * @param human The human entity to register targets for
     * @param filter The filter predicate for targeting
     */
    public static void registerXenomorphTargets(
            @Nonnull Monster human,
            @Nonnull Predicate<LivingEntity> filter) {
        for (XenomorphTargetProvider provider : TARGET_PROVIDERS) {
            human.targetSelector.addGoal(
                provider.getPriority(),
                new NearestAttackableTargetGoal<>(human, provider.getTargetClass(), true, filter));
        }
    }
}

FILE: BaseModBlock.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks;

import java.util.Objects;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.level.BlockGetter;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.Block;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.SoundType;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;
import net.minecraft.world.level.material.MapColor;
import net.minecraft.world.level.material.PushReaction;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.shapes.CollisionContext;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.shapes.Shapes;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.shapes.VoxelShape;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;

/**
 * Common base class for all mod blocks (both lab equipment and xenomorph blocks).
 * Provides shared functionality and eliminates code duplication.
 * 
 * This class implements the DRY principle by centralizing:
 * - Common block properties handling (shape, collision, lifecycle)
 * - Standardized logging for block lifecycle events
 * - Common abstract methods that subclasses must implement
 * - Common override methods that subclasses can customize
 * 
 * Subclasses (BaseLabBlock, BaseXenomorphBlock) extend this to provide
 * block-type-specific property creation methods.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public abstract class BaseModBlock extends Block {
    
    /**
     * Constructs a BaseModBlock with the specified properties.
     * 
     * @param properties The block properties
     */
    protected BaseModBlock(Properties properties) {
        super(properties);
        ModLogger.debug("Initialized " + getClass().getSimpleName());
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the shape for this block.
     * Subclasses must implement this to define the block's collision shape.
     * 
     * @return The VoxelShape for this block
     */
    protected abstract VoxelShape getBlockShape();
    
    /**
     * Creates a full-block VoxelShape (16x16x16).
     * Helper method for consistency when blocks need a full block shape.
     * 
     * @return A full-block VoxelShape
     */
    protected static VoxelShape createFullBlockShape() {
        return Shapes.block();
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the sound type for this block.
     * Subclasses can override this for different sound characteristics.
     * 
     * @return The SoundType for this block
     */
    public SoundType getSoundType() {
        return SoundType.STONE; // Default sound type
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the push reaction for this block.
     * Subclasses can override this for different piston behavior.
     * 
     * @return The PushReaction for this block
     */
    protected PushReaction getPushReaction() {
        return PushReaction.NORMAL;
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the light level for this block.
     * Subclasses can override this for light-emitting blocks.
     * 
     * @param state The block state
     * @return The light level (0-15)
     */
    protected int getLightLevel(@Nonnull BlockState state) {
        return 0; // No light emission by default
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the map color for this block.
     * Subclasses can override this for different colors.
     * 
     * @return The MapColor for this block
     */
    @Nonnull
    protected MapColor getMapColor() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(MapColor.STONE);
    }
    
    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public VoxelShape getShape(@Nonnull BlockState state, @Nonnull BlockGetter level, @Nonnull BlockPos pos, @Nonnull CollisionContext context) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(getBlockShape());
    }
    
    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public VoxelShape getCollisionShape(@Nonnull BlockState state, @Nonnull BlockGetter level, @Nonnull BlockPos pos, @Nonnull CollisionContext context) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(getBlockShape());
    }
    
    /**
     * Called when the block is placed in the world.
     * Provides logging for block placement events.
     * 
     * @param state The block state
     * @param level The level where the block was placed
     * @param pos The position where the block was placed
     * @param oldState The previous block state
     * @param isMoving Whether the block is moving
     */
    @Override
    public void onPlace(@Nonnull BlockState state, @Nonnull Level level, @Nonnull BlockPos pos, @Nonnull BlockState oldState, boolean isMoving) {
        super.onPlace(state, level, pos, oldState, isMoving);
        if (!level.isClientSide) {
            ModLogger.debug("Placed " + getClass().getSimpleName() + " at " + pos);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Called when the block is removed from the world.
     * Provides logging for block removal events.
     * 
     * @param state The block state
     * @param level The level where the block was removed
     * @param pos The position where the block was removed
     * @param newState The new block state
     * @param isMoving Whether the block is moving
     */
    @Override
    public void onRemove(@Nonnull BlockState state, @Nonnull Level level, @Nonnull BlockPos pos, @Nonnull BlockState newState, boolean isMoving) {
        super.onRemove(state, level, pos, newState, isMoving);
        if (!level.isClientSide) {
            ModLogger.debug("Removed " + getClass().getSimpleName() + " at " + pos);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the display name for this block type.
     * Used in logging and debugging.
     * 
     * @return The display name of this block type
     */
    protected String getBlockTypeName() {
        return getClass().getSimpleName();
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntityType;

/**
 * Null-safe helpers for {@link BlockEntityType} registration.
 */
public final class BlockEntityTypeHelper {

    private BlockEntityTypeHelper() {
    }

    /**
     * Builds a custom block entity type without a datafixer schema.
     * NeoForge/Vanilla registration passes null for the datafixer type at runtime.
     */
    @Nonnull
    @SuppressWarnings("null") // Mod block entities have no datafixer schema; null is valid at runtime.
    public static <T extends BlockEntity> BlockEntityType<T> buildWithoutDatafixer(
            @Nonnull BlockEntityType.Builder<T> builder) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(builder.build(null));
    }
}

FILE: SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks.specimen_pod;

import java.util.function.BiFunction;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntityTicker;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

/**
 * Registration hooks wired from L5 block-entity registration (breaks L1 upward imports).
 */
public final class SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration {

    private static BiFunction<BlockPos, BlockState, BlockEntity> factory;
    private static BlockEntityTicker<BlockEntity> serverTicker;

    private SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration() {
    }

    public static void register(
            BiFunction<BlockPos, BlockState, BlockEntity> entityFactory,
            BlockEntityTicker<BlockEntity> ticker) {
        factory = entityFactory;
        serverTicker = ticker;
    }

    public static BlockEntity create(BlockPos pos, BlockState state) {
        if (factory == null) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration not initialized");
        }
        return factory.apply(pos, state);
    }

    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    public static <T extends BlockEntity> BlockEntityTicker<T> serverTicker() {
        BlockEntityTicker<BlockEntity> ticker = serverTicker;
        return ticker == null ? null : (BlockEntityTicker<T>) ticker;
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.bootstrap;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.neoforged.bus.api.IEventBus;

/**
 * Reflection bridge from L0 {@link WeylandYutaniCore} to composition-tier bootstraps.
 */
public final class ModBootstrapHooks {

    private static final String MOD_REGISTRATION_BOOTSTRAP =
            "com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_12.lifecycle.ModRegistrationBootstrap";

    private ModBootstrapHooks() {
    }

    public static void onModConstruct(@Nonnull IEventBus modEventBus) {
        invokeStatic(MOD_REGISTRATION_BOOTSTRAP, "register", modEventBus);
    }

    private static void invokeStatic(String className, String methodName, IEventBus modEventBus) {
        try {
            Class<?> bootstrap = Class.forName(className);
            bootstrap.getMethod(methodName, IEventBus.class).invoke(null, modEventBus);
        } catch (ReflectiveOperationException e) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to invoke " + className + "#" + methodName, e);
        }
    }
}

FILE: BaseXenomorphTransformation.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.function.Function;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.transformation.TransformationConstants;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;

/**
 * Minecraft-bound xenomorph transformation utility.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 */
public class BaseXenomorphTransformation {

    public static <S extends LivingEntity, T extends LivingEntity> boolean transform(
            @Nonnull S sourceEntity,
            @Nonnull EntityType<T> targetType,
            @Nonnull String transformationName,
            @Nonnull Function<EntityType<T>, T> entityCreator) {
        return transformEntity(sourceEntity, targetType, transformationName, entityCreator) != null;
    }

    @Nullable
    public static <S extends LivingEntity, T extends LivingEntity> T transformEntity(
            @Nonnull S sourceEntity,
            @Nonnull EntityType<T> targetType,
            @Nonnull String transformationName) {
        return transformEntity(sourceEntity, targetType, transformationName, type -> type.create(sourceEntity.level()));
    }

    @Nullable
    public static <S extends LivingEntity, T extends LivingEntity> T transformEntity(
            @Nonnull S sourceEntity,
            @Nonnull EntityType<T> targetType,
            @Nonnull String transformationName,
            @Nonnull Function<EntityType<T>, T> entityCreator) {
        Level level = sourceEntity.level();

        if (level.isClientSide()) {
            return null;
        }

        ModLogger.info(transformationName, "Transforming...");

        try {
            BlockPos originalPos = sourceEntity.blockPosition();
            T targetEntity = entityCreator.apply(targetType);
            if (targetEntity == null) {
                return null;
            }

            targetEntity.moveTo(
                    originalPos.getX() + TransformationConstants.ENTITY_POSITION_OFFSET,
                    originalPos.getY(),
                    originalPos.getZ() + TransformationConstants.ENTITY_POSITION_OFFSET,
                    sourceEntity.getYRot(),
                    sourceEntity.getXRot()
            );

            targetEntity.setHealth(sourceEntity.getHealth());
            sourceEntity.remove(Entity.RemovalReason.DISCARDED);
            level.addFreshEntity(targetEntity);

            ModLogger.info(transformationName, "Successfully transformed");
            return targetEntity;

        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error(transformationName, "Failed: " + e.getMessage());
            return null;
        }
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.WorldRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

/**
 * Minecraft-side conversions between domain boundary DTOs and NeoForge types.
 */
public final class BoundaryRefs {

    private BoundaryRefs() {
    }

    public static BlockPosRef from(BlockPos pos) {
        return new BlockPosRef(pos.getX(), pos.getY(), pos.getZ());
    }

    public static BlockPos toBlockPos(BlockPosRef ref) {
        return new BlockPos(ref.x(), ref.y(), ref.z());
    }

    public static WorldRef worldFrom(Level level) {
        return new WorldRef(level.dimension().location().toString());
    }

    public static LivingEntityRef entityFrom(LivingEntity entity) {
        String dimension = "overworld";
        if (entity.level() instanceof ServerLevel server) {
            dimension = server.dimension().location().toString();
        }
        return new LivingEntityRef(entity.getUUID(), new WorldRef(dimension));
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Objects;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.core.registries.BuiltInRegistries;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * Resolves vanilla-style entity registry names for host/config lookup.
 */
public final class EntityRegistryNames {

    private EntityRegistryNames() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("EntityRegistryNames is a utility class");
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static String getEntityName(@Nullable LivingEntity entity) {
        if (entity == null || !entity.isAlive() || entity.isRemoved()) {
            return "";
        }
        ResourceLocation id = BuiltInRegistries.ENTITY_TYPE.getKey(Objects.requireNonNull(entity.getType()));
        return Objects.requireNonNull(id != null ? id.getPath() : entity.getType().toString());
    }
}

FILE: MinecraftResourceLoader.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import com.google.gson.JsonObject;
import com.google.gson.JsonParser;
import java.io.InputStreamReader;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.server.packs.resources.Resource;
import net.minecraft.server.packs.resources.ResourceManager;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.io.ResourceLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;

/**
 * L3 boundary adapter: {@link ResourceLoader} backed by Minecraft {@link ResourceManager}.
 */
public class MinecraftResourceLoader implements ResourceLoader {

    private final ResourceManager resourceManager;

    public MinecraftResourceLoader(@Nonnull ResourceManager resourceManager) {
        this.resourceManager = resourceManager;
    }

    @Override
    @Nullable
    public JsonObject loadJson(String resourcePath, Class<?> contextClass) {
        try {
            ResourceLocation resourceLocation = Objects.requireNonNull(
                    ResourceLocation.parse(Objects.requireNonNull(resourcePath)));
            Optional<Resource> resourceOpt = resourceManager.getResource(resourceLocation);

            if (resourceOpt.isEmpty()) {
                ModLogger.debug("MinecraftResourceLoader",
                        String.format("Resource not found: %s", resourcePath));
                return null;
            }

            try (InputStreamReader reader = new InputStreamReader(resourceOpt.get().open())) {
                return JsonParser.parseReader(reader).getAsJsonObject();
            }
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("MinecraftResourceLoader",
                    String.format("Failed to load JSON from %s: %s", resourcePath, e.getMessage()), e);
            return null;
        }
    }

    @Override
    public boolean resourceExists(String resourcePath, Class<?> contextClass) {
        try {
            ResourceLocation resourceLocation = Objects.requireNonNull(
                    ResourceLocation.parse(Objects.requireNonNull(resourcePath)));
            return resourceManager.getResource(resourceLocation).isPresent();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return false;
        }
    }

    @Nonnull
    public ResourceManager getResourceManager() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(resourceManager);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Objects;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.core.Holder;
import net.minecraft.core.registries.BuiltInRegistries;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffect;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;

/**
 * Resolves mod mob effects by registry id without importing minecraft-layer init holders.
 */
public final class ModEffectRegistry {

    private ModEffectRegistry() {
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static Holder<MobEffect> facehuggerAttachment() {
        return resolve("facehugger_attachment");
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static Holder<MobEffect> facehuggerImplantation() {
        return resolve("facehugger_implantation");
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static Holder<MobEffect> gestation() {
        return resolve("gestation");
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static Holder<MobEffect> hostInfection() {
        return resolve("host_infection");
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static Holder<MobEffect> suffocation() {
        return resolve("suffocation");
    }

    @Nonnull
    private static Holder<MobEffect> resolve(@Nonnull String path) {
        MobEffect effect = Objects.requireNonNull(
                BuiltInRegistries.MOB_EFFECT.get(
                        ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath(ModContext.MOD_ID, path)));
        return Objects.requireNonNull(BuiltInRegistries.MOB_EFFECT.wrapAsHolder(effect));
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeAttachmentStateAdapter.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.parasite.AttachmentState;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_2.lifecycle.AttachmentStatePort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.parasite.FacehuggerAttachmentEntity;

/**
 * NeoForge binding for {@link AttachmentStatePort} via {@link FacehuggerAttachmentEntity}.
 */
public final class NeoForgeAttachmentStateAdapter implements AttachmentStatePort {

    private final MinecraftServer server;

    public NeoForgeAttachmentStateAdapter(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        this.server = server;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean supports(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        return resolve(entity) != null;
    }

    @Override
    public AttachmentState getState(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        return require(entity).getAttachmentState();
    }

    @Override
    public void setState(LivingEntityRef entity, AttachmentState state) {
        require(entity).setAttachmentState(state);
    }

    @Override
    public int getTicks(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        return require(entity).getAttachmentTicks();
    }

    @Override
    public void setTicks(LivingEntityRef entity, int ticks) {
        require(entity).setAttachmentTicks(ticks);
    }

    @Override
    public LivingEntityRef getTarget(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        return require(entity).getAttachmentTarget();
    }

    @Override
    public void setTarget(LivingEntityRef entity, LivingEntityRef target) {
        require(entity).setAttachmentTarget(target);
    }

    @Nonnull
    private FacehuggerAttachmentEntity require(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        FacehuggerAttachmentEntity contract = resolve(entity);
        if (contract == null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Entity does not support attachment state: " + entity);
        }
        return contract;
    }

    private FacehuggerAttachmentEntity resolve(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        LivingEntity living = resolveEntity(entity).orElse(null);
        if (living instanceof FacehuggerAttachmentEntity attachment) {
            return attachment;
        }
        return null;
    }

    private Optional<LivingEntity> resolveEntity(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, ref.world())
                .flatMap(serverLevel -> {
                    var entity = serverLevel.getEntity(Objects.requireNonNull(ref.entityId()));
                    if (entity instanceof LivingEntity living) {
                        return Optional.of(living);
                    }
                    return Optional.empty();
                });
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.targeting.TargetingConditions;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_2.ai.CombatThreatQueryPort;

/**
 * L3 adapter: vanilla combat targeting scan via {@link TargetingConditions#forCombat()}.
 */
public final class NeoForgeCombatThreatAdapter implements CombatThreatQueryPort {

  private NeoForgeCombatThreatAdapter() {}

  @Nullable
  public static LivingEntity findNearestThreat(@Nonnull PathfinderMob entity, double radius) {
    if (entity.level() == null) {
      return null;
    }

    return entity.level().getNearestEntity(
        Objects.requireNonNull(entity.level().getEntitiesOfClass(
            LivingEntity.class, Objects.requireNonNull(entity.getBoundingBox().inflate(radius)))),
        Objects.requireNonNull(TargetingConditions.forCombat().range(radius)),
        entity,
        entity.getX(),
        entity.getY(),
        entity.getZ());
  }

  public static boolean hasThreatsNearby(@Nonnull PathfinderMob entity, double radius) {
    return findNearestThreat(entity, radius) != null;
  }

  @Override
  public Optional<LivingEntityRef> findNearestCombatThreat(LivingEntityRef observer, double radius) {
    // Port path reserved for BoundaryServices wiring; goals use PathfinderMob overloads above.
    return Optional.empty();
  }
}

FILE: NeoForgeEffectApplicationAdapter.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.core.Holder;
import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffect;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffectInstance;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffects;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.effects.DomainEffectKey;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.effects.EffectApplyOptions;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.effects.StandardMobEffectKey;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_2.effects.EffectApplicationPort;

public final class NeoForgeEffectApplicationAdapter implements EffectApplicationPort {

    private final MinecraftServer server;

    public NeoForgeEffectApplicationAdapter(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        this.server = server;
    }

    @Override
    public void apply(LivingEntityRef target, DomainEffectKey key, int durationTicks, int amplifier, EffectApplyOptions options) {
        resolve(target).ifPresent(living -> {
            Holder<MobEffect> effect = resolveDomainEffect(key);
            living.addEffect(new MobEffectInstance(effect, durationTicks, amplifier,
                    options.ambient(), options.showParticles(), options.showIcon()));
        });
    }

    @Override
    public void applyStandard(LivingEntityRef target, StandardMobEffectKey key, int durationTicks, int amplifier, EffectApplyOptions options) {
        resolve(target).ifPresent(living -> {
            Holder<MobEffect> effect = resolveStandardEffect(key);
            living.addEffect(new MobEffectInstance(effect, durationTicks, amplifier,
                    options.ambient(), options.showParticles(), options.showIcon()));
        });
    }

    @Override
    public void remove(LivingEntityRef target, DomainEffectKey key) {
        resolve(target).ifPresent(living -> {
            Holder<MobEffect> effect = resolveDomainEffect(key);
            living.removeEffect(effect);
        });
    }

    @Override
    public void removeStandard(LivingEntityRef target, StandardMobEffectKey key) {
        resolve(target).ifPresent(living -> {
            Holder<MobEffect> effect = resolveStandardEffect(key);
            living.removeEffect(effect);
        });
    }

    @Override
    public boolean hasEffect(LivingEntityRef target, DomainEffectKey key) {
        return resolve(target)
                .map(living -> {
                    Holder<MobEffect> effect = resolveDomainEffect(key);
                    return living.hasEffect(effect);
                })
                .orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean hasStandardEffect(LivingEntityRef target, StandardMobEffectKey key) {
        return resolve(target)
                .map(living -> {
                    Holder<MobEffect> effect = resolveStandardEffect(key);
                    return living.hasEffect(effect);
                })
                .orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public int getRemainingDuration(LivingEntityRef target, DomainEffectKey key) {
        return resolve(target)
                .map(living -> {
                    Holder<MobEffect> effect = resolveDomainEffect(key);
                    MobEffectInstance instance = living.getEffect(effect);
                    return instance != null ? instance.getDuration() : 0;
                })
                .orElse(0);
    }

    private Optional<LivingEntity> resolve(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        if (ref == null) {
            return Optional.empty();
        }
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, ref.world())
                .flatMap(level -> {
                    var entity = level.getEntity(Objects.requireNonNull(ref.entityId()));
                    if (entity instanceof LivingEntity living) {
                        return Optional.of(living);
                    }
                    return Optional.empty();
                });
    }

    @Nonnull
    private static Holder<MobEffect> resolveDomainEffect(DomainEffectKey key) {
        return switch (key) {
            case FACEHUGGER_ATTACHMENT -> ModEffectRegistry.facehuggerAttachment();
            case FACEHUGGER_IMPLANTATION -> ModEffectRegistry.facehuggerImplantation();
            case GESTATION -> ModEffectRegistry.gestation();
            case HOST_INFECTION -> ModEffectRegistry.hostInfection();
            case SUFFOCATION -> ModEffectRegistry.suffocation();
        };
    }

    @Nonnull
    private static Holder<MobEffect> resolveStandardEffect(StandardMobEffectKey key) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(switch (key) {
            case BLINDNESS -> MobEffects.BLINDNESS;
            case SLOWNESS -> MobEffects.MOVEMENT_SLOWDOWN;
            case WEAKNESS -> MobEffects.WEAKNESS;
            case HUNGER -> MobEffects.HUNGER;
            case POISON -> MobEffects.POISON;
            case DIG_SLOWDOWN -> MobEffects.DIG_SLOWDOWN;
            case SLOW_FALLING -> MobEffects.SLOW_FALLING;
            case LEVITATION -> MobEffects.LEVITATION;
        });
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeEntityQueryAdapter.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.core.registries.BuiltInRegistries;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.animal.Animal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.npc.AbstractVillager;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.entity.EntityKind;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.parasite.AttachmentState;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_2.entity.EntityQueryPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.parasite.FacehuggerAttachmentEntity;

public final class NeoForgeEntityQueryAdapter implements EntityQueryPort {

    private final MinecraftServer server;

    public NeoForgeEntityQueryAdapter(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        this.server = server;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isValid(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref)
                .map(entity -> entity.isAlive() && !entity.isRemoved())
                .orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isClientSide(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref)
                .map(entity -> entity.level().isClientSide())
                .orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public Optional<String> encodeId(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref).map(entity -> {
            @Nullable ResourceLocation id = BuiltInRegistries.ENTITY_TYPE.getKey(Objects.requireNonNull(entity.getType()));
            return id != null ? id.toString() : entity.getType().toString();
        });
    }

    @Override
    public EntityKind classify(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref)
                .map(entity -> classifyEntity(entity))
                .orElse(EntityKind.OTHER);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isPlayer(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref).map(entity -> entity instanceof Player).orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public String typeDescriptionId(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref)
                .map(entity -> entity.getType().getDescriptionId())
                .orElse("");
    }

    @Override
    public int countAttachedFacehuggers(LivingEntityRef host) {
        LivingEntity living = resolve(host).orElse(null);
        if (living == null || !living.isAlive() || living.isRemoved() || living.level() == null) {
            return 0;
        }

        int count = 0;
        for (LivingEntity entity : living.level().getEntitiesOfClass(
                LivingEntity.class, Objects.requireNonNull(living.getBoundingBox().inflate(0.5)))) {
            if (!(entity instanceof FacehuggerAttachmentEntity facehugger)) {
                continue;
            }
            AttachmentState state = facehugger.getAttachmentState();
            LivingEntityRef target = facehugger.getAttachmentTarget();
            if (target != null && target.equals(host) && !facehugger.isSpent()
                    && (state == AttachmentState.ATTACHING || state == AttachmentState.ATTACHED)) {
                count++;
            }
        }
        return count;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isAlive(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref).map(entity -> entity.isAlive()).orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isRemoved(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref).map(entity -> entity.isRemoved()).orElse(true);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isCreativePlayer(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref)
                .filter(entity -> entity instanceof Player)
                .map(entity -> (Player) entity)
                .map(player -> player.getAbilities().instabuild)
                .orElse(false);
    }

    private static EntityKind classifyEntity(LivingEntity entity) {
        @Nullable ResourceLocation id = BuiltInRegistries.ENTITY_TYPE.getKey(Objects.requireNonNull(entity.getType()));
        if (id != null && "weylandyutani".equals(id.getNamespace())) {
            return EntityKind.MOD_XENOMORPH;
        }
        if (entity instanceof Player) {
            return EntityKind.PLAYER;
        }
        if (entity instanceof AbstractVillager) {
            return EntityKind.VILLAGER;
        }
        if (entity instanceof Animal) {
            return EntityKind.ANIMAL;
        }
        return EntityKind.OTHER;
    }

    private Optional<LivingEntity> resolve(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        if (ref == null) {
            return Optional.empty();
        }
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, ref.world())
                .flatMap(level -> {
                    var entity = level.getEntity(Objects.requireNonNull(ref.entityId()));
                    if (entity instanceof LivingEntity living) {
                        return Optional.of(living);
                    }
                    return Optional.empty();
                });
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeEntitySpawnAdapter.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.spawn.SpawnContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_2.spawn.EntitySpawnPort;

/**
 * L0 boundary: resolves {@code EntityInit} holders via FQN (no L4 import).
 *
 * <p>NDE escape hatch: {@link #resolveType} calls
 * {@code com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init.EntityInitRefs} by fully qualified name
 * so this adapter stays at {@code level_0} without importing {@code level_3} {@code EntityInit}.
 * Do not replace with a compile-time import unless the adapter tier is raised to {@code level_3}+.
 */
public final class NeoForgeEntitySpawnAdapter implements EntitySpawnPort {

    private final MinecraftServer server;

    public NeoForgeEntitySpawnAdapter(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        this.server = server;
    }

    @Override
    @Nullable
    public LivingEntityRef spawnXenomorph(SpawnContext context, XenomorphType type) {
        EntityType<? extends Mob> entityType = resolveType(type);
        if (entityType == null) {
            return null;
        }
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, context.world())
                .map(level -> {
                    Mob mob = entityType.create(Objects.requireNonNull(level));
                    if (mob == null) {
                        return null;
                    }
                    mob.moveTo(context.x(), context.y(), context.z(), context.yRot(), context.xRot());
                    mob.setYHeadRot(context.headYaw());
                    level.addFreshEntity(mob);
                    return BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(mob);
                })
                .orElse(null);
    }

    @Override
    @Nullable
    public LivingEntityRef transformXenomorph(LivingEntityRef source, XenomorphType targetType) {
        EntityType<? extends Mob> entityType = resolveType(targetType);
        if (entityType == null || source == null) {
            return null;
        }
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, source.world())
                .flatMap(level -> {
                    if (!(level.getEntity(Objects.requireNonNull(source.entityId())) instanceof LivingEntity living)) {
                        return Optional.<LivingEntityRef>empty();
                    }
                    EntityType<? extends LivingEntity> livingType =
                            (EntityType<? extends LivingEntity>) entityType;
                    LivingEntity transformed = BaseXenomorphTransformation.transformEntity(
                            living, livingType, "TransformTo" + targetType);
                    return transformed != null
                            ? Optional.of(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(transformed))
                            : Optional.empty();
                })
                .orElse(null);
    }

    @Nullable
    private static EntityType<? extends Mob> resolveType(XenomorphType type) {
        String fieldName = switch (type) {
            case OVOMORPH -> "OVOMORPH";
            case FACEHUGGER -> "FACEHUGGER";
            case CHESTBURSTER -> "CHESTBURSTER";
            case GROWTH -> "GROWTH";
            case DRONE -> "DRONE";
            case PRAETOR -> "PRAETOR";
            case QUEEN -> "QUEEN";
            case HUMAN -> "HUMAN";
        };
        try {
            return com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init.EntityInitRefs.mobType(fieldName);
        } catch (IllegalStateException e) {
            return null;
        }
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeEscapeNavigationAdapter.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

/**
 * L3 adapter: issues escape navigation via entity pathfinding (no teleportation).
 */
public final class NeoForgeEscapeNavigationAdapter {

    private static final double ESCAPE_DISTANCE_MULTIPLIER = 3.0;
    private static final double ESCAPE_SPEED_MULTIPLIER = 1.0;

    private NeoForgeEscapeNavigationAdapter() {}

    public static void attemptEscape(PathfinderMob entity, Level level) {
        double randomX = (level.random.nextDouble() - 0.5) * 2.0;
        double randomZ = (level.random.nextDouble() - 0.5) * 2.0;

        entity.getNavigation().moveTo(
                entity.getX() + randomX * ESCAPE_DISTANCE_MULTIPLIER,
                entity.getY(),
                entity.getZ() + randomZ * ESCAPE_DISTANCE_MULTIPLIER,
                ESCAPE_SPEED_MULTIPLIER);

        ModLogger.debug("NeoForgeEscapeNavigationAdapter", "Attempting to walk to safety (no teleportation)");
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeLevelResolver.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.WorldRef;

import net.minecraft.core.registries.Registries;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceKey;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

public final class NeoForgeLevelResolver {

    private NeoForgeLevelResolver() {}

    public static Optional<ServerLevel> resolve(@Nullable MinecraftServer server, @Nullable WorldRef worldRef) {
        if (server == null || worldRef == null) {
            return Optional.empty();
        }
        ResourceLocation dimensionId = Objects.requireNonNull(
                ResourceLocation.parse(Objects.requireNonNull(worldRef.dimensionKey())));
        Level level = server.getLevel(Objects.requireNonNull(
                ResourceKey.create(
                        Objects.requireNonNull(Registries.DIMENSION),
                        dimensionId)));
        if (level instanceof ServerLevel serverLevel) {
            return Optional.of(serverLevel);
        }
        return Optional.empty();
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeMaturationStateAdapter.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.parasite.MaturationTimed;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_2.lifecycle.MaturationStatePort;

/**
 * NeoForge binding for {@link MaturationStatePort} via {@link MaturationTimed} entities.
 */
public final class NeoForgeMaturationStateAdapter implements MaturationStatePort {

    private final MinecraftServer server;

    public NeoForgeMaturationStateAdapter(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        this.server = server;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean supports(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        return resolveEntity(entity).map(living -> living instanceof MaturationTimed).orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public int getMaturationTimer(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        return requireTimed(entity).getMaturationTimer();
    }

    @Override
    public void setMaturationTimer(LivingEntityRef entity, int timer) {
        requireTimed(entity).setMaturationTimer(timer);
    }

    @Nonnull
    private MaturationTimed requireTimed(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        LivingEntity living = resolveEntity(entity)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalArgumentException("Entity not found: " + entity));
        if (!(living instanceof MaturationTimed timed)) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Entity does not implement MaturationTimed: " + entity);
        }
        return timed;
    }

    private Optional<LivingEntity> resolveEntity(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, ref.world())
                .flatMap(serverLevel -> {
                    var entity = serverLevel.getEntity(Objects.requireNonNull(ref.entityId()));
                    if (entity instanceof LivingEntity living) {
                        return Optional.of(living);
                    }
                    return Optional.empty();
                });
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeStuckInBlocksProbe.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.AABB;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;

/**
 * L3 probe: detects entity collision with occluding blocks via bounding-box samples.
 */
public final class NeoForgeStuckInBlocksProbe {

    private NeoForgeStuckInBlocksProbe() {}

    public static boolean isStuckInBlocks(@Nonnull PathfinderMob entity, @Nonnull Level level) {
        AABB boundingBox = entity.getBoundingBox();
        BlockPos[] checkPoints = {
            new BlockPos((int) boundingBox.minX, (int) boundingBox.minY, (int) boundingBox.minZ),
            new BlockPos((int) boundingBox.maxX, (int) boundingBox.minY, (int) boundingBox.minZ),
            new BlockPos((int) boundingBox.minX, (int) boundingBox.maxY, (int) boundingBox.minZ),
            new BlockPos((int) boundingBox.maxX, (int) boundingBox.maxY, (int) boundingBox.minZ),
            new BlockPos((int) boundingBox.minX, (int) boundingBox.minY, (int) boundingBox.maxZ),
            new BlockPos((int) boundingBox.maxX, (int) boundingBox.minY, (int) boundingBox.maxZ),
            new BlockPos((int) boundingBox.minX, (int) boundingBox.maxY, (int) boundingBox.maxZ),
            new BlockPos((int) boundingBox.maxX, (int) boundingBox.maxY, (int) boundingBox.maxZ),
            new BlockPos(
                    (int) ((boundingBox.minX + boundingBox.maxX) / 2),
                    (int) ((boundingBox.minY + boundingBox.maxY) / 2),
                    (int) ((boundingBox.minZ + boundingBox.maxZ) / 2))
        };

        for (BlockPos checkPos : checkPoints) {
            BlockState block = level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(checkPos));
            if (!block.isAir() && block.canOcclude()) {
                if (entity.tickCount % 100 == 0) {
                    ModLogger.debug("NeoForgeStuckInBlocksProbe", "Entity stuck in block at: " + checkPos);
                }
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

FILE: NestBlockScanHelper.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.Block;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.queen.NestStructureFeatures;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.queen.NestStructureScanOffsets;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.nest.NestStructureProgressPolicy;

/**
 * MC block-scan helpers for nest structure detection.
 * Offsets and scoring live in domain; this file only probes {@link Level} blocks.
 */
public final class NestBlockScanHelper {

    private NestBlockScanHelper() {
    }

    public static boolean hasNestBlocksNearby(
            @Nonnull Level level,
            @Nonnull BlockPos pos,
            @Nonnull Block resinBlock,
            @Nonnull Block spinyBlock,
            @Nonnull Block cocoonBlock,
            int scanRadius) {
        if (level.getBlockState(pos).getBlock() == resinBlock) {
            return true;
        }
        for (int[] offset : NestStructureScanOffsets.horizontalSquareOffsets(scanRadius)) {
            BlockPos checkPos = pos.offset(offset[0], 0, offset[1]);
            BlockState state = level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(checkPos));
            Block block = state.getBlock();
            if (block == resinBlock || block == spinyBlock || block == cocoonBlock) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    public static int detectNestProgress(
            @Nonnull Level level,
            @Nonnull BlockPos centerPos,
            @Nonnull Block resinBlock,
            @Nonnull Block spinyBlock,
            int scanRadius) {
        boolean hasFoundation = anyMatch(level, centerPos,
                NestStructureScanOffsets.foundationRingOffsets(scanRadius), 0, resinBlock);
        boolean hasWalls = hasFoundation
                && anyMatch(level, centerPos, NestStructureScanOffsets.wallPerimeterOffsets(scanRadius), 1, resinBlock);
        boolean hasDecorations = hasWalls
                && anyMatch(level, centerPos, NestStructureScanOffsets.horizontalSquareOffsets(scanRadius), 1, spinyBlock);
        boolean hasCenterResin = hasDecorations
                && level.getBlockState(centerPos).getBlock() == resinBlock;

        return NestStructureProgressPolicy.score(
                new NestStructureFeatures(hasFoundation, hasWalls, hasDecorations, hasCenterResin));
    }

    private static boolean anyMatch(
            @Nonnull Level level,
            @Nonnull BlockPos center,
            int[][] offsets,
            int relativeY,
            @Nonnull Block expected) {
        for (int[] offset : offsets) {
            if (level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(
                    center.offset(offset[0], relativeY, offset[1]))).getBlock() == expected) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

FILE: CreativeTabHelper.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.client;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceKey;
import net.minecraft.world.item.Item;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.event.BuildCreativeModeTabContentsEvent;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredHolder;

/**
 * Centralized utility for creative tab registration.
 * Consolidates duplicate creative tab registration patterns.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * This utility consolidates creative tab registration following DRY principles.
 * Reduces boilerplate in WeylandYutaniClient.
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class CreativeTabHelper {
    
    /**
     * Adds an item to a creative tab if the holder is bound.
     * Consolidates the repetitive if-bound check pattern.
     * 
     * @param event The creative tab contents event
     * @param currentTabKey The current tab key from the event (for comparison)
     * @param targetTabKey The target tab key to add to
     * @param itemHolder The deferred holder for the item
     */
    public static void addItemToTab(
            @Nonnull BuildCreativeModeTabContentsEvent event,
            @Nonnull ResourceKey<?> currentTabKey,
            @Nonnull ResourceKey<?> targetTabKey,
            @Nonnull DeferredHolder<Item, ? extends Item> itemHolder) {
        
        if (currentTabKey == targetTabKey && itemHolder.isBound()) {
            event.accept(Objects.requireNonNull(itemHolder.get()));
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Adds multiple items to a creative tab.
     * Convenience method for adding multiple items at once.
     * Uses List instead of varargs to avoid @SafeVarargs annotation.
     * 
     * @param event The creative tab contents event
     * @param currentTabKey The current tab key from the event (for comparison)
     * @param targetTabKey The target tab key to add to
     * @param itemHolders The deferred holders for the items
     */
    public static void addItemsToTab(
            @Nonnull BuildCreativeModeTabContentsEvent event,
            @Nonnull ResourceKey<?> currentTabKey,
            @Nonnull ResourceKey<?> targetTabKey,
            @Nonnull List<DeferredHolder<Item, ? extends Item>> itemHolders) {
        
        if (currentTabKey == targetTabKey) {
            for (DeferredHolder<Item, ? extends Item> itemHolder : itemHolders) {
                if (itemHolder.isBound()) {
                    event.accept(Objects.requireNonNull(itemHolder.get()));
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

FILE: FeatureFlagHelper.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.config;

import java.util.Objects;

import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.world.flag.FeatureFlag;
import net.minecraft.world.flag.FeatureFlagSet;
import net.minecraft.world.level.LevelReader;

/**
 * Helper utility for checking if feature flags are enabled.
 * Provides convenient methods for feature flag validation.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class FeatureFlagHelper {
    
    /**
     * Checks if a feature flag is enabled in the given level.
     * Generic method that consolidates duplicate feature flag checking logic.
     * 
     * @param level The level reader to check enabled features from
     * @param flag The feature flag to check
     * @return True if the feature flag is enabled, false otherwise
     */
    public static boolean isFeatureEnabled(@Nullable LevelReader level, @Nullable FeatureFlag flag) {
        if (level == null || flag == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        FeatureFlagSet enabledFeatures = level.enabledFeatures();
        FeatureFlagSet requiredFeatures = Objects.requireNonNull(FeatureFlagSet.of(flag));
        return requiredFeatures.isSubsetOf(Objects.requireNonNull(enabledFeatures));
    }
    
    /**
     * Checks if the Growth entity feature is enabled in the given level.
     * Convenience method that delegates to the generic isFeatureEnabled method.
     * 
     * @param level The level reader to check enabled features from
     * @return True if Growth feature is enabled, false otherwise
     */
    public static boolean isGrowthEnabled(@Nullable LevelReader level) {
        return isFeatureEnabled(level, ModFeatureFlags.EXPERIMENTAL_GROWTH);
    }
    
    /**
     * Checks if the Praetor entity feature is enabled in the given level.
     * Convenience method that delegates to the generic isFeatureEnabled method.
     * 
     * @param level The level reader to check enabled features from
     * @return True if Praetor feature is enabled, false otherwise
     */
    public static boolean isPraetorEnabled(@Nullable LevelReader level) {
        return isFeatureEnabled(level, ModFeatureFlags.EXPERIMENTAL_PRAETOR);
    }
    
    /**
     * Checks if the experimental expansions feature is enabled in the given level.
     * Convenience method that delegates to the generic isFeatureEnabled method.
     * 
     * @param level The level reader to check enabled features from
     * @return True if expansions feature is enabled, false otherwise
     */
    public static boolean isExpansionsEnabled(@Nullable LevelReader level) {
        return isFeatureEnabled(level, ModFeatureFlags.EXPERIMENTAL_EXPANSIONS);
    }
    
    /**
     * Private constructor to prevent instantiation.
     */
    private FeatureFlagHelper() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Utility class cannot be instantiated");
    }
}

FILE: ModFeatureFlags.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.config;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.core.Registry;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.world.flag.FeatureFlag;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;

/**
 * Utility class for managing feature flags.
 * Provides centralized access to all feature flags used by the mod.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class ModFeatureFlags {
    
    /**
     * Feature flag for experimental Growth entity.
     * Growth entities will only be available when this flag is enabled.
     */
    @Nullable
    public static FeatureFlag EXPERIMENTAL_GROWTH = null;
    
    /**
     * Feature flag for experimental Praetor entity.
     * Praetor entities will only be available when this flag is enabled.
     */
    @Nullable
    public static FeatureFlag EXPERIMENTAL_PRAETOR = null;
    
    /**
     * Feature flag for experimental expansion content.
     * Includes Priority 3-5 content: Mob-Based Xenomorphs, Alien: Earth, Cyborg/Android.
     */
    @Nullable
    public static FeatureFlag EXPERIMENTAL_EXPANSIONS = null;
    
    
    /**
     * Initializes feature flags from a registry.
     * This method should be called during RegisterEvent for FEATURE_FLAG registry.
     * 
     * @param registry The feature flag registry
     */
    public static void initialize(@Nullable Registry<FeatureFlag> registry) {
        if (registry == null) {
            ModLogger.warn("ModFeatureFlags", "⚠️ Feature flag registry is null");
            return;
        }
        
        try {
            EXPERIMENTAL_GROWTH = getFlag(registry, "experimental_growth");
            EXPERIMENTAL_PRAETOR = getFlag(registry, "experimental_praetor");
            EXPERIMENTAL_EXPANSIONS = getFlag(registry, "experimental_expansions");
            
            ModLogger.info("ModFeatureFlags", "✅ Feature flags initialized");
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("ModFeatureFlags", "Failed to initialize feature flags", e);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Retrieves a feature flag from the registry.
     * 
     * @param registry The feature flag registry
     * @param flagName The name of the flag (without namespace)
     * @return The feature flag, or null if not found
     */
    @Nullable
    private static FeatureFlag getFlag(@Nonnull Registry<FeatureFlag> registry, @Nonnull String flagName) {
        try {
            ResourceLocation flagId = ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath(ModContext.MOD_ID, flagName);
            FeatureFlag flag = registry.get(flagId);
            
            if (flag == null) {
                ModLogger.warn("ModFeatureFlags", "⚠️ Feature flag not found: " + flagId);
            } else {
                ModLogger.debug("ModFeatureFlags", "✅ Feature flag loaded: " + flagId);
            }
            
            return flag;
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("ModFeatureFlags", "Failed to retrieve feature flag: " + flagName, e);
            return null;
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Private constructor to prevent instantiation.
     */
    private ModFeatureFlags() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Utility class cannot be instantiated");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.config;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;

import net.minecraft.sounds.SoundEvent;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Helper class for applying sound parameters from JSON configuration.
 * This replaces hardcoded sound values with data-driven configuration.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class SoundHelper {
    
    /**
     * Plays a step sound using configuration from JSON.
     * Gracefully skips if sound is not registered (null check).
     * 
     * @param entity The entity playing the sound
     * @param xenomorphType The xenomorph type to get configuration for
     * @param soundEvent The sound event to play
     */
    public static void playStepSound(Mob entity, XenomorphType xenomorphType, SoundEvent soundEvent) {
        if (soundEvent == null) {
            return; // Gracefully skip if sound not registered
        }
        
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);
        
        if (config.soundParameters != null) {
            entity.playSound(soundEvent, config.soundParameters.stepVolume, config.soundParameters.stepPitch);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Plays an ambient sound using configuration from JSON.
     * Gracefully skips if sound is not registered (null check).
     * 
     * @param entity The entity playing the sound
     * @param xenomorphType The xenomorph type to get configuration for
     * @param soundEvent The sound event to play
     */
    public static void playAmbientSound(Mob entity, XenomorphType xenomorphType, SoundEvent soundEvent) {
        if (soundEvent == null) {
            return; // Gracefully skip if sound not registered
        }
        
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);
        
        if (config.soundParameters != null) {
            entity.playSound(soundEvent, config.soundParameters.ambientVolume, config.soundParameters.ambientPitch);
        }
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.entity;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;

/**
 * Centralized utility for calculating cardinal and intercardinal directions.
 * Provides common direction calculation functionality following DRY principles.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class DirectionHelper {
    
    /**
     * Gets the cardinal or intercardinal direction from one entity to another.
     * Returns directions like "North", "Northeast", "East", etc.
     * 
     * @param from The source entity
     * @param to The target entity
     * @return The direction string (North, Northeast, East, Southeast, South, Southwest, West, Northwest, or Unknown)
     */
    public static String getCardinalDirection(Entity from, Entity to) {
        if (from == null || to == null) {
            return "Unknown";
        }
        
        double deltaX = to.getX() - from.getX();
        double deltaZ = to.getZ() - from.getZ();
        
        // Calculate angle in degrees (0-360)
        double angle = Math.atan2(deltaZ, deltaX) * 180.0 / Math.PI;
        angle = (angle + 360) % 360; // Normalize to 0-360
        
        // Map angle to cardinal/intercardinal directions
        if (angle >= 337.5 || angle < 22.5) return "North";
        if (angle >= 22.5 && angle < 67.5) return "Northeast";
        if (angle >= 67.5 && angle < 112.5) return "East";
        if (angle >= 112.5 && angle < 157.5) return "Southeast";
        if (angle >= 157.5 && angle < 202.5) return "South";
        if (angle >= 202.5 && angle < 247.5) return "Southwest";
        if (angle >= 247.5 && angle < 292.5) return "West";
        if (angle >= 292.5 && angle < 337.5) return "Northwest";
        
        return "Unknown";
    }
}
