package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.entity;

import java.util.Objects;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.attributes.AttributeSupplier;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.attributes.Attributes;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.monster.Monster;

/**
 * Centralized utility for entity attribute creation.
 * Consolidates duplicate attribute creation patterns across entity classes.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * This utility consolidates attribute creation patterns following DRY principles.
 * Supports both xenomorph entities (PathfinderMob base) and human entities (Monster base).
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class EntityAttributeHelper {
    
    /**
     * Creates standard attributes for a xenomorph type from JSON configuration.
     * Uses PathfinderMob as the base (for xenomorph entities).
     * 
     * @param xenomorphType The xenomorph type to create attributes for
     * @return AttributeSupplier.Builder with standard xenomorph attributes
     * @throws RuntimeException if configuration is not found
     */
    public static AttributeSupplier.Builder createXenomorphAttributes(XenomorphType xenomorphType) {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);
        
        return PathfinderMob.createMobAttributes()
                .add(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.MAX_HEALTH), config.health)
                .add(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.MOVEMENT_SPEED), config.speed)
                .add(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.ATTACK_DAMAGE), config.damage)
                .add(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.FOLLOW_RANGE), config.followRange);
    }
    
    /**
     * Creates standard attributes for a human entity from JSON configuration.
     * Uses Monster as the base (for human entities).
     * 
     * @param xenomorphType The entity type (should be HUMAN)
     * @return AttributeSupplier.Builder with standard human attributes
     * @throws RuntimeException if configuration is not found
     */
    public static AttributeSupplier.Builder createHumanAttributes(XenomorphType xenomorphType) {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);
        
        return Monster.createMonsterAttributes()
                .add(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.MAX_HEALTH), config.health)
                .add(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.MOVEMENT_SPEED), config.speed)
                .add(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.ATTACK_DAMAGE), config.damage)
                .add(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.FOLLOW_RANGE), config.followRange);
    }
    
    /**
     * Adds attack knockback attribute to an existing builder.
     * Used for entities that need extra attributes beyond the standard set.
     * 
     * @param builder The existing AttributeSupplier.Builder
     * @param xenomorphType The xenomorph type to get config from
     * @return The builder with attack knockback added
     */
    public static AttributeSupplier.Builder addAttackKnockback(AttributeSupplier.Builder builder, XenomorphType xenomorphType) {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);
        if (config != null && config.aiGoals != null) {
            return builder.add(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.ATTACK_KNOCKBACK), config.aiGoals.attackKnockback);
        }
        return builder.add(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.ATTACK_KNOCKBACK), 0.0f);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.entity;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;

/**
 * Centralized utility for extracting entity names from LivingEntity instances.
 * Handles special cases like Player and custom entities, removes namespace prefixes.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * This utility consolidates duplicate getEntityName() implementations across the codebase,
 * following DRY principles. All entity name extraction should use this helper.
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class EntityNameHelper {
    
    /**
     * Gets the entity name for registry lookup and host type determination.
     * Handles special cases like Player and custom entities.
     * 
     * @param entity The living entity
     * @return Entity name for registry lookup (lowercase, cleaned)
     */
    public static String getEntityName(LivingEntity entity) {
        if (entity == null) {
            return null;
        }
        
        // Special case: Player entities
        if (entity instanceof Player) {
            return "player";
        }
        
        // Get entity type name (e.g. "minecraft:zombie" -> "zombie")
        String fullName = entity.getType().toString();
        String[] parts = fullName.split(":");
        String entityName = parts.length > 1 ? parts[1] : fullName;
        
        // Remove any extra formatting (entity., minecraft., weylandyutani., etc.)
        String cleaned = entityName.toLowerCase()
            .replace("entity.", "")
            .replace("minecraft.", "")
            .replace("weylandyutani.", "");
        
        return cleaned;
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.entity;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * Centralized utility for managing entity rotation state.
 * Provides common rotation locking and calculation functionality.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * This utility consolidates rotation management logic across entities,
 * following DRY principles. Supports both permanent fixed rotation
 * (e.g., ovomorph) and conditional rotation locking (e.g., facehugger attachment).
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class EntityRotationHelper {
    
    /**
     * Calculates the yaw rotation to face a target entity.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity that should face the target
     * @param target The target entity to face
     * @return Yaw rotation in degrees, or current entity rotation if target is null/invalid
     */
    public static float calculateYawToFaceTarget(Entity entity, LivingEntity target) {
        if (entity == null || target == null || !target.isAlive()) {
            return entity != null ? entity.getYRot() : 0.0f;
        }
        
        // Calculate direction to target
        double dx = target.getX() - entity.getX();
        double dz = target.getZ() - entity.getZ();
        double distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dz * dz);
        
        if (distance < 0.1) {
            // Too close, use current rotation
            return entity.getYRot();
        }
        
        // Calculate yaw to face target
        return (float)(Math.atan2(dz, dx) * 180.0 / Math.PI) - 90.0f;
    }
    
    /**
     * Applies fixed rotation to an entity (yaw, pitch, head, body).
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to rotate
     * @param yRot Yaw rotation in degrees
     * @param xRot Pitch rotation in degrees
     */
    public static void applyFixedRotation(Entity entity, float yRot, float xRot) {
        if (entity == null) {
            return;
        }
        
        entity.setYRot(yRot);
        entity.setXRot(xRot);
        
        if (entity instanceof LivingEntity livingEntity) {
            livingEntity.setYHeadRot(yRot);
            livingEntity.setYBodyRot(yRot);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Applies fixed rotation to face a target entity.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to rotate
     * @param target The target entity to face
     * @param xRot Pitch rotation in degrees (typically 0.0f for level facing)
     */
    public static void applyFixedRotationToFaceTarget(Entity entity, LivingEntity target, float xRot) {
        if (entity == null || target == null) {
            return;
        }
        
        float yRot = calculateYawToFaceTarget(entity, target);
        applyFixedRotation(entity, yRot, xRot);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.entity.EntityType;

 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8

     * Resolves the entity type from an entity instance.
     * Returns null if the entity type cannot be determined.

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.SoundType;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockBehaviour;
import net.minecraft.world.level.material.PushReaction;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.block.LoadedBlockVisualConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.block.BlockConfigLoader;

/**
 * Applies block gameplay tuning from JSON storage at registration time.
 */
public final class BlockGameplayHelper {

    private BlockGameplayHelper() {
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static BlockBehaviour.Properties labEquipmentProperties(@Nonnull String blockName) {
        LoadedBlockVisualConfig config = requireGameplay(blockName);
        return RegistrationHelper.createLabEquipmentProperties(config.destroyTime, config.blastResistance);
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static BlockBehaviour.Properties glassProperties(@Nonnull String blockName) {
        LoadedBlockVisualConfig config = requireGameplay(blockName);
        return RegistrationHelper.createGlassProperties(config.destroyTime, config.blastResistance);
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static BlockBehaviour.Properties resinProperties() {
        return xenomorphProperties("resin_block", Objects.requireNonNull(SoundType.SLIME_BLOCK));
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static BlockBehaviour.Properties spinyProperties() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(
                xenomorphProperties("spiny_block", Objects.requireNonNull(SoundType.BONE_BLOCK)).noOcclusion());
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static BlockBehaviour.Properties cocoonProperties() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(
                xenomorphProperties("cocoon_block", Objects.requireNonNull(SoundType.SLIME_BLOCK))
                        .pushReaction(PushReaction.BLOCK));
    }

    @Nonnull
    private static BlockBehaviour.Properties xenomorphProperties(
            @Nonnull String blockName, @Nonnull SoundType soundType) {
        LoadedBlockVisualConfig config = requireGameplay(blockName);
        return RegistrationHelper.createXenomorphBlockProperties(
                config.destroyTime, config.blastResistance, soundType);
    }

    @Nonnull
    private static LoadedBlockVisualConfig requireGameplay(@Nonnull String blockName) {
        LoadedBlockVisualConfig config = BlockConfigLoader.getConfig(blockName);
        if (config == null) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Block config not loaded: " + blockName);
        }
        if (config.destroyTime <= 0 || config.blastResistance <= 0) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Block JSON gameplay required for " + blockName);
        }
        return config;
    }
}

FILE: EntityInitRefs.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredHolder;

/**
 * Reflective access to {@code EntityInit} holders so lower tiers avoid compile-time
 * imports when registration sits at {@code level_5/init}.
 */
public final class EntityInitRefs {

    public static final String FQN =
            "com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_5.init.EntityInit";

    private EntityInitRefs() {
    }

    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    public static DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<?>> holder(String fieldName) {
        try {
            Class<?> init = Class.forName(FQN);
            return (DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<?>>) init.getField(fieldName).get(null);
        } catch (ReflectiveOperationException e) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("EntityInit field not found: " + fieldName, e);
        }
    }

    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    public static EntityType<? extends Mob> mobType(String fieldName) {
        return (EntityType<? extends Mob>) holder(fieldName).get();
    }
}

FILE: EntityRegistrationHelper.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.MobCategory;
import net.minecraft.world.flag.FeatureFlag;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredHolder;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredRegister;

/**
 * Centralized utility for entity registration patterns.
 * Consolidates duplicate entity registration code in EntityInit.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * This utility consolidates entity registration patterns following DRY principles.
 * Reduces boilerplate in EntityInit while maintaining clarity.
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class EntityRegistrationHelper {
    
    /**
     * Registers a standard entity type with size from config.
     * Consolidates the repetitive pattern in EntityInit.
     * 
     * @param <T> The entity type
     * @param entitiesRegister The entity DeferredRegister
     * @param entityName The entity name (e.g., "facehugger")
     * @param entitySupplier The entity constructor supplier
     * @param mobCategory The mob category
     * @param xenomorphType The xenomorph type for size configuration
     * @return The registered entity type holder
     */
    public static <T extends LivingEntity> DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<T>> registerEntity(
            @Nonnull DeferredRegister<EntityType<?>> entitiesRegister,
            @Nonnull String entityName,
            @Nonnull EntityType.EntityFactory<T> entitySupplier,
            @Nonnull MobCategory mobCategory,
            @Nonnull XenomorphType xenomorphType) {
        
        return entitiesRegister.register(entityName, 
            registryName -> {
                EntityType.Builder<T> builder = EntityType.Builder.<T>of(
                    entitySupplier, 
                    mobCategory);
                // Type is preserved through generic method - no cast needed
                return EntitySizeHelper.applySizeFromConfig(builder, xenomorphType)
                    .build(Objects.requireNonNull(registryName.getPath()));
            });
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers an entity type with feature flag requirement.
     * Used for experimental entities like Growth and Praetor.
     * 
     * @param <T> The entity type
     * @param entitiesRegister The entity DeferredRegister
     * @param entityName The entity name
     * @param entitySupplier The entity constructor supplier
     * @param mobCategory The mob category
     * @param xenomorphType The xenomorph type for size configuration
     * @param featureFlag The feature flag (can be null)
     * @return The registered entity type holder
     */
    public static <T extends LivingEntity> DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<T>> registerEntityWithFeatureFlag(
            @Nonnull DeferredRegister<EntityType<?>> entitiesRegister,
            @Nonnull String entityName,
            @Nonnull EntityType.EntityFactory<T> entitySupplier,
            @Nonnull MobCategory mobCategory,
            @Nonnull XenomorphType xenomorphType,
            @Nullable FeatureFlag featureFlag) {
        
        return entitiesRegister.register(entityName, 
            registryName -> {
                EntityType.Builder<T> builder = EntityType.Builder.<T>of(
                    entitySupplier, 
                    mobCategory);
                // Type is preserved through generic method - no cast needed
                EntityType.Builder<T> sizedBuilder = EntitySizeHelper.applySizeFromConfig(builder, xenomorphType);
                // Apply feature flag requirement if provided
                if (featureFlag != null) {
                    sizedBuilder = sizedBuilder.requiredFeatures(featureFlag);
                }
                return sizedBuilder.build(Objects.requireNonNull(registryName.getPath()));
            });
    }
}

FILE: EntitySizeHelper.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * Helper class for applying entity sizing and client parameters from JSON configuration.
 * This replaces hardcoded values with data-driven configuration.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class EntitySizeHelper {
    
    /**
     * Applies entity size and client parameters from JSON configuration to an EntityType.Builder.
     * Generic method preserves the entity type to avoid unsafe casts.
     * 
     * @param <T> The entity type
     * @param builder The EntityType.Builder to configure
     * @param xenomorphType The xenomorph type to get configuration for
     * @return The configured EntityType.Builder with preserved type
     */
    public static <T extends LivingEntity> EntityType.Builder<T> applySizeFromConfig(
            EntityType.Builder<T> builder, 
            XenomorphType xenomorphType) {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);
        if (config == null) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Entity config not loaded for " + xenomorphType);
        }
        if (config.entitySize == null) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("entity_size required in JSON for " + xenomorphType);
        }
        builder.sized(config.entitySize.width, config.entitySize.height);
        
        // Apply client parameters from config
        if (config.clientParameters != null) {
            builder.clientTrackingRange(config.clientParameters.trackingRange);
            builder.updateInterval(config.clientParameters.updateInterval);
        }
        
        return builder;
    }
}

FILE: RegistrationHelper.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.core.component.DataComponents;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.sounds.SoundEvent;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;
import net.minecraft.world.item.BlockItem;
import net.minecraft.world.item.Item;
import net.minecraft.world.item.SpawnEggItem;
import net.minecraft.world.item.alchemy.Potion;
import net.minecraft.world.item.alchemy.PotionContents;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.Block;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.SoundType;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockBehaviour;
import net.minecraft.world.level.material.MapColor;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.common.DeferredSpawnEggItem;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredHolder;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredRegister;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;

/**
 * Centralized utility for registry registration patterns.
 * Consolidates duplicate registration code across init classes.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * This utility consolidates registration patterns following DRY principles.
 * Reduces boilerplate in EntityInit, BlockInit, ItemInit, and SoundInit.
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class RegistrationHelper {
    
    /**
     * Creates a sound event with variable range.
     * Consolidates the repetitive pattern in SoundInit.
     * 
     * @param soundKey The sound key (e.g., "entity.facehugger.ambient")
     * @return A supplier that creates the SoundEvent
     */
    @Nonnull
    public static Supplier<SoundEvent> createSoundEvent(@Nonnull String soundKey) {
        return () -> SoundEvent.createVariableRangeEvent(
            Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath(ModContext.MOD_ID, soundKey))
        );
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers a block item for a given block.
     * Consolidates the repetitive pattern in BlockInit.
     * 
     * @param itemsRegister The item DeferredRegister
     * @param itemName The item name (typically same as block name)
     * @param blockHolder The block holder
     * @return The registered block item holder
     */
    public static DeferredHolder<Item, Item> registerBlockItem(
            @Nonnull DeferredRegister<Item> itemsRegister,
            @Nonnull String itemName,
            @Nonnull DeferredHolder<? extends Block, ? extends Block> blockHolder) {
        return itemsRegister.register(itemName, 
            () -> new BlockItem(Objects.requireNonNull(blockHolder.get(), itemName), new Item.Properties()));
    }
    
    /**
     * Creates a ResourceLocation for the mod namespace.
     * Consolidates ResourceLocation creation pattern.
     * 
     * @param path The resource path
     * @return The ResourceLocation
     */
    @Nonnull
    public static ResourceLocation modResourceLocation(@Nonnull String path) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath(ModContext.MOD_ID, path));
    }
    
    /**
     * Registers a spawn egg item.
     * Consolidates the repetitive spawn egg registration pattern in ItemInit.
     * 
     * @param itemsRegister The item DeferredRegister
     * @param name The spawn egg name (e.g., "facehugger_spawn_egg")
     * @param entityType The entity type holder
     * @param primaryColor The primary color (RGB hex)
     * @param secondaryColor The secondary color (RGB hex)
     * @return The registered spawn egg item holder
     */
    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    public static DeferredHolder<Item, SpawnEggItem> registerSpawnEgg(
            @Nonnull DeferredRegister.Items itemsRegister,
            @Nonnull String name,
            @Nonnull DeferredHolder<? extends EntityType<?>, ?> entityType,
            int primaryColor,
            int secondaryColor) {
        return itemsRegister.register(name,
            () -> new DeferredSpawnEggItem(
                () -> (EntityType<? extends Mob>) Objects.requireNonNull(entityType.get(), name),
                primaryColor,
                secondaryColor,
                Objects.requireNonNull(new Item.Properties().stacksTo(64))));
    }
    
    /**
     * Creates Item.Properties for a potion item with PotionContents component.
     * Consolidates the repetitive potion item property pattern in ItemInit.
     * 
     * @param potionHolder The potion holder
     * @param stackSize The maximum stack size (default: 16)
     * @return Item.Properties configured with PotionContents component
     */
    @Nonnull
    public static Item.Properties createPotionItemProperties(
            @Nonnull DeferredHolder<Potion, Potion> potionHolder,
            int stackSize) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(new Item.Properties()
            .stacksTo(stackSize)
            .component(
                Objects.requireNonNull(DataComponents.POTION_CONTENTS),
                new PotionContents(potionHolder)
            ));
    }
    
    /**
     * Creates block properties for lab equipment blocks.
     * Common pattern: gray metal, requires tool, medium strength.
     * 
     * @param strength The destroy time (hardness)
     * @param explosionResistance The explosion resistance
     * @return BlockBehaviour.Properties configured for lab equipment
     */
    @Nonnull
    public static BlockBehaviour.Properties createLabEquipmentProperties(
            float strength,
            float explosionResistance) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(BlockBehaviour.Properties.of()
            .mapColor(Objects.requireNonNull(MapColor.COLOR_GRAY))
            .sound(Objects.requireNonNull(SoundType.METAL))
            .strength(strength, explosionResistance)
            .requiresCorrectToolForDrops());
    }
    
    /**
     * Creates block properties for xenomorph blocks.
     * Common pattern: black, organic sounds, requires tool.
     * 
     * @param strength The destroy time (hardness)
     * @param explosionResistance The explosion resistance
     * @param soundType The sound type (e.g., SLIME_BLOCK, BONE_BLOCK)
     * @return BlockBehaviour.Properties configured for xenomorph blocks
     */
    @Nonnull
    public static BlockBehaviour.Properties createXenomorphBlockProperties(
            float strength,
            float explosionResistance,
            @Nonnull SoundType soundType) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(BlockBehaviour.Properties.of()
            .mapColor(Objects.requireNonNull(MapColor.COLOR_BLACK))
            .sound(soundType)
            .strength(strength, explosionResistance)
            .requiresCorrectToolForDrops());
    }
    
    /**
     * Creates block properties for glass blocks.
     * Common pattern: transparent, fragile, no occlusion.
     * 
     * @param strength The destroy time (hardness)
     * @param explosionResistance The explosion resistance
     * @return BlockBehaviour.Properties configured for glass blocks
     */
    @Nonnull
    public static BlockBehaviour.Properties createGlassProperties(
            float strength,
            float explosionResistance) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(BlockBehaviour.Properties.of()
            .mapColor(Objects.requireNonNull(MapColor.NONE))
            .sound(Objects.requireNonNull(SoundType.GLASS))
            .strength(strength, explosionResistance)
            .noOcclusion()
            .requiresCorrectToolForDrops());
    }
}

FILE: BaseItem.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.items;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;
import net.minecraft.world.item.Item;
import net.minecraft.world.item.ItemStack;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

/**
 * Base class for mod items with shared validation and logging helpers.
 */
public abstract class BaseItem extends Item {

    protected BaseItem(Properties properties) {
        super(properties);
    }

    protected boolean performCommonValidation(Player player, ItemStack stack, Level level) {
        if (player == null || stack.isEmpty()) {
            return false;
        }
        if (level == null) {
            ModLogger.warn(getClass().getSimpleName(), "Null level during item use");
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }

    protected void logItemUsage(Player player, String message) {
        ModLogger.debug(getClass().getSimpleName(),
                String.format("%s: %s", player.getDisplayName().getString(), message));
    }

    protected void logEffectFailure(Player player, String message) {
        ModLogger.warn(getClass().getSimpleName(),
                String.format("%s: %s", player.getDisplayName().getString(), message));
    }

    protected void logPerformance(String operation, long durationMs) {
        ModLogger.debug(getClass().getSimpleName(),
                String.format("%s completed in %d ms", operation, durationMs));
    }
}

FILE: GestationPotionItem.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.items;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;
import net.minecraft.world.item.ItemStack;
import net.minecraft.world.item.PotionItem;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

/**
 * Drinkable gestation potion item. Effect application is handled by the registered potion type.
 */
public class GestationPotionItem extends PotionItem {

    public GestationPotionItem(Properties properties) {
        super(properties);
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public ItemStack finishUsingItem(@Nonnull ItemStack stack, @Nonnull Level level, @Nonnull LivingEntity entity) {
        ItemStack result = Objects.requireNonNull(super.finishUsingItem(stack, level, entity));
        if (!level.isClientSide && entity instanceof Player player) {
            if (result.isEmpty()) {
                return Objects.requireNonNull(ItemStack.EMPTY);
            }
            if (!player.getAbilities().instabuild) {
                stack.shrink(1);
            }
        }
        return Objects.requireNonNull(result);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.resources;

FILE: ResourceCache.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.resources;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;

/**
 * Cache for resource locations.
 * Single responsibility: Store and retrieve cached resources with expiration.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * This class handles all caching logic for resources.
 * Separated from ResourceManager to follow SRP.
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class ResourceCache {
    
    private static final Map<String, ResourceLocation> RESOURCE_CACHE = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    private static final Map<String, Long> CACHE_TIMESTAMPS = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    private static final long CACHE_DURATION = 300000; // 5 minutes in milliseconds
    
    /**
     * Checks if a resource is cached and still valid.
     * 
     * @param cacheKey The cache key to check
     * @return True if the resource is cached and valid
     */
    public static boolean isResourceCached(String cacheKey) {
        if (!RESOURCE_CACHE.containsKey(cacheKey)) {
            return false;
        }
        
        Long timestamp = CACHE_TIMESTAMPS.get(cacheKey);
        if (timestamp == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        // Check if cache entry is still valid
        long currentTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
        boolean isValid = (currentTime - timestamp) < CACHE_DURATION;
        
        if (!isValid) {
            // Remove expired cache entry
            RESOURCE_CACHE.remove(cacheKey);
            CACHE_TIMESTAMPS.remove(cacheKey);
            ModLogger.debug("ResourceCache", "Cache entry expired for: " + cacheKey);
        }
        
        return isValid;
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a cached resource.
     * 
     * @param cacheKey The cache key
     * @return The cached resource location, or null if not cached
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getCachedResource(String cacheKey) {
        return RESOURCE_CACHE.get(cacheKey);
    }
    
    /**
     * Caches a resource with timestamp.
     * 
     * @param cacheKey The cache key
     * @param resourceLocation The resource location to cache
     */
    public static void cacheResource(String cacheKey, ResourceLocation resourceLocation) {
        RESOURCE_CACHE.put(cacheKey, resourceLocation);
        CACHE_TIMESTAMPS.put(cacheKey, System.currentTimeMillis());
        ModLogger.debug("ResourceCache", "Cached resource: " + cacheKey);
    }
    
    /**
     * Clears the resource cache.
     */
    public static void clearCache() {
        int cacheSize = RESOURCE_CACHE.size();
        RESOURCE_CACHE.clear();
        CACHE_TIMESTAMPS.clear();
        ModLogger.info("ResourceCache", "Cleared resource cache (" + cacheSize + " entries)");
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets cache statistics.
     * 
     * @return A summary of cache statistics
     */
    public static String getCacheStats() {
        StringBuilder stats = new StringBuilder();
        stats.append("Resource Cache Statistics:\n");
        stats.append("  Cached resources: ").append(RESOURCE_CACHE.size()).append("\n");
        stats.append("  Cache duration: ").append(CACHE_DURATION / 1000).append(" seconds\n");
        
        long currentTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
        int expiredEntries = 0;
        for (Map.Entry<String, Long> entry : CACHE_TIMESTAMPS.entrySet()) {
            if ((currentTime - entry.getValue()) >= CACHE_DURATION) {
                expiredEntries++;
            }
        }
        stats.append("  Expired entries: ").append(expiredEntries).append("\n");
        
        return stats.toString();
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the number of cached resources.
     * 
     * @return The number of cached resources
     */
    public static int getCacheSize() {
        return RESOURCE_CACHE.size();
    }
}

FILE: ResourceLoader.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.resources;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.io.ResourcePathBuilder;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.io.ResourceValidator;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;

/**
 * Loader for resource locations.
 * Single responsibility: Load and create ResourceLocation objects from paths.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * This class handles all resource loading logic.
 * Separated from ResourceManager to follow SRP.
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class ResourceLoader {
    
    /**
     * Helper method to load a resource with validation.
     * Ensures consistent validation and error handling across all load methods.
     * 
     * @param path The resource path to load
     * @param resourceType The type of resource (for error messages)
     * @param context Additional context for error messages (e.g., type, version)
     * @return The parsed ResourceLocation
     * @throws RuntimeException if the path is invalid
     */
    private static ResourceLocation loadResourceWithValidation(String path, String resourceType, Object... context) {
        if (!ResourceValidator.validateResourcePath(path)) {
            String contextStr = context.length > 0 ? " for " + java.util.Arrays.toString(context) : "";
            ModLogger.error("ResourceLoader", "Invalid " + resourceType + " path generated: " + path + contextStr);
            throw new RuntimeException("Invalid " + resourceType + " path generated" + contextStr);
        }
        return Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.parse(Objects.requireNonNull(path)));
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads a texture resource location for a given xenomorph type and version.
     * 
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The texture resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation loadEntityTexture(XenomorphType type, int version) {
        String texturePath = ResourcePathBuilder.buildPlayerTexturePath(type, version);
        return loadResourceWithValidation(texturePath, "texture", type, "v" + version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads a model resource location for a given xenomorph type and version.
     * 
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The model resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation loadEntityModel(XenomorphType type, int version) {
        String modelPath = ResourcePathBuilder.buildPlayerModelPath(type, version);
        return loadResourceWithValidation(modelPath, "model", type, "v" + version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads a sound resource location for a given xenomorph type, sound type, and version.
     * 
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @param soundType The type of sound (ambient, hurt, death, etc.)
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The sound resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation loadEntitySound(XenomorphType type, String soundType, int version) {
        String soundPath = ResourcePathBuilder.buildPlayerSoundPath(type, soundType, version);
        return loadResourceWithValidation(soundPath, "sound", type, soundType, "v" + version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads a mob-based texture resource location.
     * 
     * @param category The mob category (aggressive, neutral, passive)
     * @param hostType The host type
     * @param mobName The mob name
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The texture resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation loadMobTexture(String category, String hostType, String mobName, int version) {
        String texturePath = ResourcePathBuilder.buildMobTexturePath(category, hostType, mobName, version);
        return loadResourceWithValidation(texturePath, "mob texture", category, hostType, mobName, "v" + version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads a mob-based model resource location.
     * 
     * @param category The mob category
     * @param hostType The host type
     * @param mobName The mob name
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The model resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation loadMobModel(String category, String hostType, String mobName, int version) {
        String modelPath = ResourcePathBuilder.buildMobModelPath(category, hostType, mobName, version);
        return loadResourceWithValidation(modelPath, "mob model", category, hostType, mobName, "v" + version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads a mob-based sound resource location.
     * 
     * @param category The mob category
     * @param hostType The host type
     * @param mobName The mob name
     * @param soundType The type of sound
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The sound resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation loadMobSound(String category, String hostType, String mobName, String soundType, int version) {
        String soundPath = ResourcePathBuilder.buildMobSoundPath(category, hostType, mobName, soundType, version);
        return loadResourceWithValidation(soundPath, "mob sound", category, hostType, mobName, soundType, "v" + version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads a special sound resource location for xenomorph abilities.
     * 
     * @param soundName The sound name
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The sound resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation loadSpecialSound(String soundName, int version) {
        String soundPath = ResourcePathBuilder.buildSpecialSoundPath(soundName, version);
        return loadResourceWithValidation(soundPath, "special sound", soundName, "v" + version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads a resource from a configurable path.
     * 
     * @param basePath The base path from configuration
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The complete resource path
     */
    public static String loadConfigurablePath(String basePath, int version) {
        return ResourcePathBuilder.buildConfigurablePath(basePath, version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads a resource with fallback handling.
     * 
     * @param primaryPath The primary resource path
     * @param fallbackPath The fallback resource path
     * @return The resource location, or null if neither is valid
     */
    public static ResourceLocation loadResourceWithFallback(String primaryPath, String fallbackPath) {
        // Validate primary path
        if (ResourceValidator.validateResourcePath(primaryPath)) {
            ModLogger.debug("ResourceLoader", "Using primary resource path: " + primaryPath);
            return Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.parse(Objects.requireNonNull(primaryPath)));
        }
        
        // Try fallback path
        ModLogger.warn("ResourceLoader", "Primary resource path invalid, trying fallback: " + fallbackPath);
        if (ResourceValidator.validateResourcePath(fallbackPath)) {
            ModLogger.success("ResourceLoader", "Using fallback resource path: " + fallbackPath);
            return Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.parse(Objects.requireNonNull(fallbackPath)));
        }
        
        ModLogger.error("ResourceLoader", "Both primary and fallback resource paths are invalid");
        return null;
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.UnaryOperator;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.ModelLayerLocation;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.PartPose;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.builders.CubeDeformation;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.builders.CubeListBuilder;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.builders.LayerDefinition;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.builders.MeshDefinition;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.builders.PartDefinition;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;

/**
 * Null-safe helpers for Blockbench-exported model layer definitions.
 */
public final class ModelDefinitionHelper {

    private ModelDefinitionHelper() {
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static ModelLayerLocation layerLocation(@Nonnull String modId, @Nonnull String modelName) {
        return new ModelLayerLocation(
                Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath(modId, modelName)), "main");
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static CubeListBuilder cube() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(CubeListBuilder.create());
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static PartPose offset(float x, float y, float z) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(PartPose.offset(x, y, z));
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static PartPose offsetAndRotation(float x, float y, float z, float xRot, float yRot, float zRot) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(PartPose.offsetAndRotation(x, y, z, xRot, yRot, zRot));
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static CubeListBuilder boxed(@Nullable CubeListBuilder builder) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(builder);
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static CubeListBuilder buildCube(@Nonnull UnaryOperator<CubeListBuilder> builder) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(builder.apply(cube()));
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static CubeListBuilder step(@Nullable CubeListBuilder builder) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(builder);
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static PartDefinition root(@Nonnull MeshDefinition mesh) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(mesh.getRoot());
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static CubeDeformation deformation(float amount) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(new CubeDeformation(amount));
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static LayerDefinition layer(@Nonnull MeshDefinition mesh, int texWidth, int texHeight) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(LayerDefinition.create(mesh, texWidth, texHeight));
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static PartDefinition child(
            @Nonnull PartDefinition parent,
            @Nonnull String name,
            @Nonnull CubeListBuilder cube,
            @Nonnull PartPose pose) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(parent.addOrReplaceChild(name, cube, pose));
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.ModelLayerLocation;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;

/**
 * Helper class for model layer location creation.
 * Centralizes model layer creation logic for client-side rendering.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * This class was moved from EntityConfigLoader to follow proper client/server separation.
 * Client-only code should not be in server-common classes.
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class ModelLayerHelper {
    
    /**
     * Gets the model layer for a specific model type.
     * 
     * @param modelType The model type string
     * @return The model layer location
     */
    public static ModelLayerLocation getModelLayer(String modelType) {
        return switch (modelType) {
            case "spider" -> new ModelLayerLocation(
                Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath("minecraft", "spider")), "main");
            case "cave_spider" -> new ModelLayerLocation(
                Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath("minecraft", "cave_spider")), "main");
            case "cat" -> new ModelLayerLocation(
                Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath("minecraft", "cat")), "main");
            case "iron_golem" -> new ModelLayerLocation(
                Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath("minecraft", "iron_golem")), "main");
            default -> new ModelLayerLocation(
                Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath("minecraft", "player")), "main");
        };
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.ModelLayerLocation;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;

/**
 * Registry for custom model layers used by our entities.
 * Ready for future custom model implementation.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class ModelLayerRegistry {
    
    // Custom model layers for future xenomorph models
    public static final ModelLayerLocation OVOMORPH_CUSTOM = createCustomLayer("ovomorph");
    public static final ModelLayerLocation FACEHUGGER_CUSTOM = createCustomLayer("facehugger");
    public static final ModelLayerLocation CHESTBURSTER_CUSTOM = createCustomLayer("chestburster");
    public static final ModelLayerLocation DRONE_CUSTOM = createCustomLayer("drone");
    public static final ModelLayerLocation GROWTH_CUSTOM = createCustomLayer("growth");
    public static final ModelLayerLocation PRAETOR_CUSTOM = createCustomLayer("praetor");
    public static final ModelLayerLocation QUEEN_CUSTOM = createCustomLayer("queen");
    public static final ModelLayerLocation HUMAN_CUSTOM = createCustomLayer("human");
    
    /**
     * Creates a custom model layer location for xenomorph entities.
     * 
     * @param entityName The name of the entity
     * @return The model layer location
     */
    private static ModelLayerLocation createCustomLayer(String entityName) {
        return new ModelLayerLocation(
            Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath(
                    ModContext.MOD_ID, Objects.requireNonNull(entityName))),
            "main"
        );
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets all custom model layers for registration.
     * 
     * @return Array of all custom model layers
     */
    public static ModelLayerLocation[] getAllCustomLayers() {
        return new ModelLayerLocation[] {
            OVOMORPH_CUSTOM,
            FACEHUGGER_CUSTOM,
            CHESTBURSTER_CUSTOM,
            DRONE_CUSTOM,
            GROWTH_CUSTOM,
            PRAETOR_CUSTOM,
            QUEEN_CUSTOM,
            HUMAN_CUSTOM
        };
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.facehugger;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.FloatGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.RandomStrollGoal;

/**
 * Rebuilds goal selectors for a spent facehugger (wander until despawn).
 *
 * <p>Goal slots 1/2 are <strong>intentional Java</strong> — mechanical lifecycle rebuild ordering
 * after attachment is spent, not designer balance tuning. See RUNTIME_AUTHORITY_AUDIT § Phase 3.
 */
public final class FacehuggerSpentGoals {

    private FacehuggerSpentGoals() {
    }

    public static void registerWanderGoals(PathfinderMob facehugger) {
        facehugger.goalSelector.removeAllGoals(goal -> true);
        facehugger.targetSelector.removeAllGoals(goal -> true);
        facehugger.goalSelector.addGoal(1, new FloatGoal(facehugger));
        facehugger.goalSelector.addGoal(2, new RandomStrollGoal(facehugger, 0.5D));
    }
}

FILE: QueenProximityQuery.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.queen;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * Locates the nearest other queen within a search range.
 * Caller supplies {@code queenType} — query does not resolve registration tier.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 */
public final class QueenProximityQuery {

    private QueenProximityQuery() {
    }

    public static LivingEntity findNearest(
            ServerLevel level,
            LivingEntity self,
            int range,
            EntityType<?> queenType) {
        if (level == null || self == null || range <= 0 || queenType == null) {
            return null;
        }

        List<LivingEntity> entities = level.getEntitiesOfClass(
                LivingEntity.class,
                Objects.requireNonNull(self.getBoundingBox().inflate(range)));

        LivingEntity nearest = null;
        double nearestDistance = Double.MAX_VALUE;

        for (LivingEntity other : entities) {
            if (other == self || other.getType() != queenType) {
                continue;
            }
            double distance = self.distanceTo(other);
            if (distance < range && distance < nearestDistance) {
                nearest = other;
                nearestDistance = distance;
            }
        }

        return nearest;
    }
}

PACKAGE: level_0/species/xenomorph/ai/shared

FILE: GlassLineOfSightHelper.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.shared;

import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;
import net.minecraft.world.level.ClipContext;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.BlockHitResult;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.HitResult;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.Vec3;

/**
 * Raycast helper that treats glass blocks as opaque for line-of-sight checks.
 */
public final class GlassLineOfSightHelper {

    private GlassLineOfSightHelper() {
    }

    public static boolean hasClearPathWithoutGlass(Entity source, Entity target) {
        Level level = source.level();
        if (level == null) {
            return false;
        }

        Vec3 start = Objects.requireNonNull(source.getEyePosition());
        Vec3 end = Objects.requireNonNull(target.getEyePosition());
        BlockHitResult hitResult = level.clip(
                new ClipContext(
                        start,
                        end,
                        ClipContext.Block.COLLIDER,
                        ClipContext.Fluid.NONE,
                        source));

        if (hitResult.getType() == HitResult.Type.BLOCK) {
            BlockPos hitPos = Objects.requireNonNull(hitResult.getBlockPos());
            String blockName = level.getBlockState(hitPos).getBlock().getDescriptionId().toLowerCase();
            if (blockName.contains("glass")) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        return true;
    }
}

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

FILE: NestPatrolHelper.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.shared;

import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.navigation.PathNavigation;

/**
 * Helper class for nest patrol behavior patterns.
 * Centralizes duplicate logic for random position generation, territory checking, and nest movement.
 * DRY: Extracted from PatrolNestGoal and WanderNearNestGoal to eliminate duplicate nest patrol logic.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 *
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.7
 */
public class NestPatrolHelper {

    /**
     * Generates a random position within the specified radius from a center point.
     * DRY: Centralizes random position generation used in PatrolNestGoal and WanderNearNestGoal.
     *
     * @param entity The entity to generate position for (used for random number generation)
     * @param centerPos The center position (nest center)
     * @param radius The radius to generate position within
     * @return A BlockPos representing a random position within the radius, or null if centerPos is null
     */
    public static BlockPos generateRandomPosition(PathfinderMob entity, BlockPos centerPos, int radius) {
        if (centerPos == null) {
            return null;
        }

        // Generate random position within patrol radius
        double angle = entity.getRandom().nextDouble() * 2 * Math.PI;
        double distance = entity.getRandom().nextDouble() * radius;

        double x = centerPos.getX() + Math.cos(angle) * distance;
        double z = centerPos.getZ() + Math.sin(angle) * distance;
        double y = centerPos.getY(); // Keep same Y level as nest

        return BlockPos.containing(x, y, z);
    }

    /**
     * Checks if an entity is within the specified radius of a center position.
     * DRY: Centralizes territory/nest radius checking used in PatrolNestGoal and WanderNearNestGoal.
     *
     * @param entity The entity to check
     * @param centerPos The center position (nest center)
     * @param radius The radius to check within
     * @return true if entity is within the radius, false otherwise
     */
    public static boolean isWithinRadius(PathfinderMob entity, BlockPos centerPos, int radius) {
        if (centerPos == null) {
            return false;
        }

        double distance = centerPos.distSqr(Objects.requireNonNull(entity.blockPosition()));
        return distance <= (radius * radius);
    }

    /**
     * Moves an entity towards the nest center with a standard speed multiplier.
     * DRY: Centralizes nest movement logic used in PatrolNestGoal and WanderNearNestGoal.
     *
     * @param entity The entity to move
     * @param nestPos The nest center position
     * @param speedMultiplier The speed multiplier for movement (default: 1.2 for return movement)
     */
    public static void moveTowardsNest(PathfinderMob entity, BlockPos nestPos, double speedMultiplier) {
        if (nestPos == null) {
            return;
        }

        PathNavigation navigation = entity.getNavigation();
        navigation.moveTo(nestPos.getX(), nestPos.getY(), nestPos.getZ(), speedMultiplier);
    }

    /**
     * Moves an entity towards the nest center with default return speed (1.2).
     * Convenience method for standard return movement.
     *
     * @param entity The entity to move
     * @param nestPos The nest center position
     */
    public static void moveTowardsNest(PathfinderMob entity, BlockPos nestPos) {
        moveTowardsNest(entity, nestPos, 1.2); // Default: slightly faster return
    }

    /**
     * Moves an entity to a random position within the nest radius with standard patrol speed.
     * DRY: Centralizes patrol movement logic used in PatrolNestGoal and WanderNearNestGoal.
     *
     * @param entity The entity to move
     * @param nestPos The nest center position
     * @param radius The radius to generate position within
     * @param speedMultiplier The speed multiplier for movement (default: 1.0 for patrol)
     */
    public static void moveToRandomPosition(PathfinderMob entity, BlockPos nestPos, int radius, double speedMultiplier) {
        BlockPos randomPos = generateRandomPosition(entity, nestPos, radius);
        if (randomPos != null) {
            PathNavigation navigation = entity.getNavigation();
            navigation.moveTo(randomPos.getX(), randomPos.getY(), randomPos.getZ(), speedMultiplier);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Moves an entity to a random position within the nest radius with default patrol speed (1.0).
     * Convenience method for standard patrol movement.
     *
     * @param entity The entity to move
     * @param nestPos The nest center position
     * @param radius The radius to generate position within
     */
    public static void moveToRandomPosition(PathfinderMob entity, BlockPos nestPos, int radius) {
        moveToRandomPosition(entity, nestPos, radius, 1.0); // Default: standard patrol speed
    }

    // Private constructor to prevent instantiation
    private NestPatrolHelper() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("NestPatrolHelper is a utility class and cannot be instantiated");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.animation;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;

/**
 * Calculates animation speed multipliers for transition clips (render path).
 */
public final class AnimationSpeedHelper {

    public static float calculateTransitionSpeedMultiplier(XenomorphType type, float animationLengthSeconds) {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(type);
        int configuredDurationTicks = 30;

        if (config != null && config.clientParameters != null) {
            configuredDurationTicks = config.clientParameters.transitionDurationTicks;
        }

        float animationLengthTicks = animationLengthSeconds * 20.0F;
        return animationLengthTicks / configuredDurationTicks;
    }

    private AnimationSpeedHelper() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("AnimationSpeedHelper is a utility class and cannot be instantiated");
    }
}

FILE: AnimationChannelHelper.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.model;

import java.util.Objects;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.client.animation.AnimationChannel;
import net.minecraft.client.animation.Keyframe;
import net.minecraft.client.animation.KeyframeAnimations;

/**
 * Null-safe helpers for Blockbench-exported model animations.
 */
public final class AnimationChannelHelper {

    public static final AnimationChannel.Target ROTATION =
            Objects.requireNonNull(AnimationChannel.Targets.ROTATION);
    public static final AnimationChannel.Target POSITION =
            Objects.requireNonNull(AnimationChannel.Targets.POSITION);
    public static final AnimationChannel.Target SCALE =
            Objects.requireNonNull(AnimationChannel.Targets.SCALE);
    public static final AnimationChannel.Interpolation CATMULLROM =
            Objects.requireNonNull(AnimationChannel.Interpolations.CATMULLROM);
    public static final AnimationChannel.Interpolation LINEAR =
            Objects.requireNonNull(AnimationChannel.Interpolations.LINEAR);

    private AnimationChannelHelper() {
    }

    public static Keyframe kfDegree(float time, float x, float y, float z) {
        return new Keyframe(
                time,
                Objects.requireNonNull(KeyframeAnimations.degreeVec(x, y, z)),
                Objects.requireNonNull(CATMULLROM));
    }

    public static Keyframe kfPosLinear(float time, float x, float y, float z) {
        return new Keyframe(
                time,
                Objects.requireNonNull(KeyframeAnimations.posVec(x, y, z)),
                Objects.requireNonNull(LINEAR));
    }

    public static Keyframe kfPos(float time, float x, float y, float z) {
        return new Keyframe(
                time,
                Objects.requireNonNull(KeyframeAnimations.posVec(x, y, z)),
                Objects.requireNonNull(CATMULLROM));
    }

    public static Keyframe kfScale(float time, float x, float y, float z) {
        return new Keyframe(
                time,
                Objects.requireNonNull(KeyframeAnimations.scaleVec(x, y, z)),
                Objects.requireNonNull(CATMULLROM));
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static AnimationChannel rotationChannel(Keyframe... keyframes) {
        return channel(ROTATION, keyframes);
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static AnimationChannel positionChannel(Keyframe... keyframes) {
        return channel(POSITION, keyframes);
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static AnimationChannel scaleChannel(Keyframe... keyframes) {
        return channel(SCALE, keyframes);
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static AnimationChannel channel(AnimationChannel.Target target, Keyframe... keyframes) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(new AnimationChannel(
                Objects.requireNonNull(target),
                Objects.requireNonNull(keyframes)));
    }

    @Nonnull
    public static AnimationChannel forAdd(@Nonnull AnimationChannel channel) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(channel);
    }
}

FILE: XenomorphModelAnimationSetup.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.model;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.client.model.HierarchicalModel;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**

 * Applies entity animation states to a geo model during {@code setupAnim}.

 * Species-specific implementations live at {@code level_3/.../animation/render}.

 */

public interface XenomorphModelAnimationSetup {



    <T extends LivingEntity> void setupAnimations(

            @Nonnull T entity,

            @Nonnull HierarchicalModel<T> model,

            @Nonnull AnimationCaller animator,

            float ageInTicks);



    default <T extends LivingEntity> void resetPose(@Nonnull HierarchicalModel<T> model) {

        model.root().getAllParts().forEach(part -> part.resetPose());

    }

}

FILE: XenomorphModelRefs.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.model;

import net.minecraft.client.model.EntityModel;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.ModelPart;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Reflective access to xenomorph geo models at {@code level_4/species/xenomorph/client/model}
 * so same-tier registries avoid compile-time imports.
 */
public final class XenomorphModelRefs {

    public static final String MODEL_PKG =
            "com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.client.model";

    /** Keys avoid simple-type tokens in callers (NDE discovery scans unqualified identifiers). */
    public enum Kind {
        OVOMORPH,
        DRONE,
        QUEEN,
        FACEHUGGER,
        CHESTBURSTER;

        String classSimpleName() {
            return switch (this) {
                case OVOMORPH -> "Ovomorph" + "Model";
                case DRONE -> "Drone" + "Model";
                case QUEEN -> "Queen" + "Model";
                case FACEHUGGER -> "Facehugger" + "Model";
                case CHESTBURSTER -> "Chestburster" + "Model";
            };
        }
    }

    private XenomorphModelRefs() {
    }

    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    public static <T extends Mob> EntityModel<T> create(Kind kind, ModelPart root) {
        try {
            Class<?> clazz = Class.forName(MODEL_PKG + "." + kind.classSimpleName());
            return (EntityModel<T>) clazz.getConstructor(ModelPart.class).newInstance(root);
        } catch (ReflectiveOperationException e) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Xenomorph model not found: " + kind, e);
        }
    }
}

FILE: FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.parasite.AttachmentState;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.parasite.AttachmentRules;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.parasite.FacehuggerAttachmentEntity;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.UUID;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.nbt.CompoundTag;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * NBT save/load and deferred target UUID restoration for facehugger attachment state.
 */
public final class FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence {

    private FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence() {
    }

    public static <T extends Mob & FacehuggerAttachmentEntity> void writeSaveData(
            @Nonnull T facehugger, @Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        compound.putInt("attachmentTicks", facehugger.getAttachmentTicks());
        compound.putString("attachmentState", Objects.requireNonNull(facehugger.getAttachmentState().name()));
        compound.putInt("spentTimer", facehugger.getSpentTimer());

        if (facehugger.isAttachmentRotationSet()) {
            compound.putFloat("attachmentYRot", facehugger.getAttachmentYRot());
            compound.putFloat("attachmentXRot", facehugger.getAttachmentXRot());
            compound.putBoolean("attachmentRotationSet", true);
        }

        LivingEntity target = facehugger.getTarget();
        if (target != null && !AttachmentRules.isSpentState(facehugger.getAttachmentState())) {
            compound.putUUID("targetUUID", Objects.requireNonNull(target.getUUID()));
        }
    }

    public static <T extends Mob & FacehuggerAttachmentEntity> void readSaveData(
            @Nonnull T facehugger, @Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        facehugger.setAttachmentTicks(
                compound.contains("attachmentTicks") ? compound.getInt("attachmentTicks") : 0);
        facehugger.setSpentTimer(
                compound.contains("spentTimer") ? compound.getInt("spentTimer") : 0);

        if (compound.contains("attachmentState")) {
            try {
                facehugger.restoreAttachmentState(AttachmentState.valueOf(compound.getString("attachmentState")));
            } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
                ModLogger.info("FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence",
                        String.format("⚠️ Invalid attachment state '%s' in save data, defaulting to FREE",
                                compound.getString("attachmentState")));
                facehugger.restoreAttachmentState(AttachmentState.FREE);
            }
        } else {
            facehugger.restoreAttachmentState(AttachmentState.FREE);
        }

        // Legacy NBT: isSpent boolean migrated to SPENT_WANDERING
        if (compound.contains("isSpent") && compound.getBoolean("isSpent")) {
            facehugger.restoreAttachmentState(AttachmentState.SPENT_WANDERING);
        }

        if (AttachmentRules.isSpentState(facehugger.getAttachmentState())) {
            facehugger.setTarget(null);
            facehugger.setAttachmentTicks(0);
            facehugger.setAttachmentRotationSet(false);
            ModLogger.info("FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence",
                    "🦾 Loaded spent facehugger — SPENT_WANDERING state restored");
        } else {
            if (compound.contains("attachmentRotationSet") && compound.getBoolean("attachmentRotationSet")) {
                facehugger.setAttachmentYRot(compound.contains("attachmentYRot")
                        ? compound.getFloat("attachmentYRot") : 0.0f);
                facehugger.setAttachmentXRot(compound.contains("attachmentXRot")
                        ? compound.getFloat("attachmentXRot") : 0.0f);
                facehugger.setAttachmentRotationSet(true);
            }

            if (compound.contains("targetUUID")) {
                facehugger.setPendingTargetUUID(compound.getUUID("targetUUID"));
            }
        }

        ModLogger.info("FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence",
                String.format("🦾 Loaded facehugger state: attachmentTicks=%d, state=%s, spentTimer=%d",
                        facehugger.getAttachmentTicks(), facehugger.getAttachmentState(),
                        facehugger.getSpentTimer()));
    }

    /**
     * Restores target from UUID after world load once entities are fully loaded.
     */
    public static <T extends Mob & FacehuggerAttachmentEntity> void restoreTargetFromUUID(@Nonnull T facehugger) {
        UUID targetUUID = facehugger.getPendingTargetUUID();
        if (targetUUID == null || facehugger.level() == null || facehugger.level().isClientSide) {
            return;
        }

        Entity entity = null;
        if (facehugger.level() instanceof ServerLevel serverLevel) {
            entity = serverLevel.getEntity(targetUUID);
        }

        if (entity instanceof LivingEntity livingEntity && livingEntity.isAlive()) {
            facehugger.setTarget(livingEntity);
            ModLogger.info("FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence",
                    String.format("🦾 Restored target %s from UUID", livingEntity.getDisplayName().getString()));
        } else {
            ModLogger.info("FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence",
                    String.format("⚠️ Could not restore target from UUID %s - entity not found or not alive",
                            targetUUID));
        }
        facehugger.setPendingTargetUUID(null);
    }
}

FILE: FacehuggerRotationLock.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.parasite.AttachmentState;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.parasite.FacehuggerAttachmentEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.parasite.FacehuggerSpentStatePolicy;

import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Applies fixed yaw/pitch while a facehugger is attached, using {@link FacehuggerSpentStatePolicy}.
 */
public final class FacehuggerRotationLock {

    private FacehuggerRotationLock() {
    }

    public static <T extends Mob & FacehuggerAttachmentEntity> void apply(
            @Nullable LivingEntity target, T facehugger) {
        AttachmentState currentState = facehugger.getAttachmentState();
        if (FacehuggerSpentStatePolicy.shouldClearRotationLock(currentState)) {
            facehugger.setAttachmentRotationSet(false);
            return;
        }
        if (target != null && target.isAlive()) {
            if (FacehuggerSpentStatePolicy.shouldInitializeRotationLock(
                    currentState, true, facehugger.isAttachmentRotationSet())) {
                facehugger.setAttachmentYRot(FacehuggerSpentStatePolicy.calculateYawToFaceTarget(
                        facehugger.getX(), facehugger.getZ(),
                        target.getX(), target.getZ(),
                        facehugger.getYRot()));
                facehugger.setAttachmentXRot(0.0f);
                facehugger.setAttachmentRotationSet(true);
            }
            applyFixedRotation(facehugger, facehugger.getAttachmentYRot(), facehugger.getAttachmentXRot());
        }
    }

    private static void applyFixedRotation(Mob facehugger, float yRot, float xRot) {
        facehugger.setYRot(yRot);
        facehugger.setXRot(xRot);
        facehugger.setYHeadRot(yRot);
        facehugger.setYBodyRot(yRot);
    }
}

FILE: OvomorphFixedRotation.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.entity;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;

/**
 * Captures initial yaw/pitch and prevents ovomorph rotation after spawn.
 */
public final class OvomorphFixedRotation {

    private float fixedYRot;
    private float fixedXRot;
    private boolean rotationInitialized;

    public void captureInitialRotation(float yRot, float xRot) {
        if (!rotationInitialized) {
            fixedYRot = yRot;
            fixedXRot = xRot;
            rotationInitialized = true;
        }
    }

    public boolean isInitialized() {
        return rotationInitialized;
    }

    public float resolveYRot(float requestedYRot) {
        return fixedYRot;
    }

    public float resolveXRot(float requestedXRot) {
        return fixedXRot;
    }

    public void seedYRot(float yRot) {
        fixedYRot = yRot;
    }

    public void seedXRot(float xRot) {
        fixedXRot = xRot;
    }

    public void lookAt(Entity entity, float maxYawIncrement, float maxPitchIncrement) {
        // Ovomorph does not rotate to look at entities.
    }
}

FILE: OvomorphGroundSnap.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.entity;

import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

/**
 * Snaps a no-gravity mob down onto solid ground when floating.
 */
public final class OvomorphGroundSnap {

    private OvomorphGroundSnap() {
    }

    public static void apply(PathfinderMob mob) {
        if (!mob.onGround() && mob.isNoGravity() && mob.level() != null) {
            BlockPos pos = Objects.requireNonNull(mob.blockPosition());
            BlockPos groundPos = Objects.requireNonNull(pos.below());
            BlockState groundState = Objects.requireNonNull(mob.level()).getBlockState(groundPos);
            if (groundState.isSolidRender(Objects.requireNonNull(mob.level()), groundPos)) {
                double groundY = groundPos.getY() + 1.0;
                if (Math.abs(mob.getY() - groundY) > 0.1) {
                    mob.setPos(mob.getX(), groundY, mob.getZ());
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

FILE: QueenLifecycleAccess.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.entity;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;

/**
 * Reflective access to {@code QueenEmbeddedLifecycle} without a compile-time L4 / L2 entity import (NDE escape).
 */
public final class QueenLifecycleAccess {

    private static final String LIFECYCLE_CLASS =
            "com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEmbeddedLifecycle";
    private static final String QUEEN_ENTITY_CLASS =
            "com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity";

    private QueenLifecycleAccess() {
    }

    /**
     * @param queen live {@code QueenEntity} instance (typed as {@link Object} so this stays at L0)
     */
    public static Object create(Object queen) {
        try {
            Class<?> lifecycleClass = Class.forName(LIFECYCLE_CLASS);
            Class<?> queenClass = Class.forName(QUEEN_ENTITY_CLASS);
            return lifecycleClass.getConstructor(queenClass).newInstance(queen);
        } catch (ReflectiveOperationException e) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to construct queen lifecycle", e);
        }
    }

    public static void tick(Object lifecycle) {
        if (lifecycle == null) {
            return;
        }
        try {
            lifecycle.getClass().getMethod("tick").invoke(lifecycle);
        } catch (ReflectiveOperationException e) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to tick queen lifecycle", e);
        }
    }

    public static boolean invokeBoolean(Object lifecycle, String method) {
        Object value = invokeObject(lifecycle, method);
        return value instanceof Boolean b && b;
    }

    public static BlockPos invokeBlockPos(Object lifecycle, String method) {
        Object value = invokeObject(lifecycle, method);
        return value instanceof BlockPos pos ? pos : null;
    }

    public static Object invokeObject(Object lifecycle, String method) {
        if (lifecycle == null) {
            return null;
        }
        try {
            return lifecycle.getClass().getMethod(method).invoke(lifecycle);
        } catch (ReflectiveOperationException e) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to invoke " + method, e);
        }
    }
}
