FILE: QueenNestPersistence.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.QueenNestProgress;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.nbt.CompoundTag;

/**
 * Nest NBT save/load for the queen entity via lifecycle + {@link QueenNestProgress}.
 */
public final class QueenNestPersistence {

    private QueenNestPersistence() {
    }

    public static void writeSaveData(
            @Nonnull CompoundTag compound,
            @Nullable Object lifecycle,
            @Nullable QueenNestProgress nestProgress) {
        if (lifecycle == null) {
            return;
        }
        compound.putBoolean("hasNest", QueenLifecycleAccess.invokeBoolean(lifecycle, "hasNest"));
        BlockPos nestPos = QueenLifecycleAccess.invokeBlockPos(lifecycle, "getNestPosition");
        if (nestPos != null) {
            compound.putLong("nestPosition", nestPos.asLong());
        }
        QueenNestProgressTags.write(compound, nestProgress);
    }

    public static void readSaveData(
            @Nonnull CompoundTag compound,
            @Nullable Object lifecycle,
            @Nullable QueenNestProgress nestProgress) {
        if (lifecycle == null) {
            return;
        }
        boolean hasNest = compound.contains("hasNest") && compound.getBoolean("hasNest");
        if (!hasNest || !compound.contains("nestPosition")) {
            return;
        }
        try {
            BlockPos nestPos = BlockPos.of(compound.getLong("nestPosition"));
            int buildingProgress = QueenNestProgressTags.readBuildingProgress(compound);
            int hiveBuildingProgress = QueenNestProgressTags.readHiveBuildingProgress(compound);
            boolean isExpandingToHive = QueenNestProgressTags.readExpandingToHive(compound);
            lifecycle.getClass()
                    .getMethod("restoreNestState", BlockPos.class, int.class, int.class, boolean.class)
                    .invoke(lifecycle, nestPos, buildingProgress, hiveBuildingProgress, isExpandingToHive);
            if (nestProgress != null) {
                nestProgress.restoreNestState(
                        new BlockPosRef(nestPos.getX(), nestPos.getY(), nestPos.getZ()),
                        buildingProgress,
                        hiveBuildingProgress,
                        isExpandingToHive);
            }
        } catch (ReflectiveOperationException e) {
            ModLogger.warn("QueenNestPersistence", "Failed to restore nest state: " + e.getMessage());
        }
    }
}

FILE: QueenNestProgressTags.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.QueenNestProgress;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;
import net.minecraft.nbt.CompoundTag;

/**
 * NBT tags for queen nest-building progress fields.
 */
public final class QueenNestProgressTags {

    private QueenNestProgressTags() {
    }

    public static void write(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound, @Nullable QueenNestProgress nestProgress) {
        if (nestProgress != null) {
            compound.putInt("buildingProgress", nestProgress.getBuildingProgress());
            compound.putInt("hiveBuildingProgress", nestProgress.getHiveBuildingProgress());
            compound.putBoolean("isExpandingToHive", nestProgress.isExpandingToHive());
        } else {
            compound.putInt("buildingProgress", 0);
            compound.putInt("hiveBuildingProgress", 0);
            compound.putBoolean("isExpandingToHive", false);
        }
    }

    public static int readBuildingProgress(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        return compound.contains("buildingProgress") ? compound.getInt("buildingProgress") : 0;
    }

    public static int readHiveBuildingProgress(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        return compound.contains("hiveBuildingProgress") ? compound.getInt("hiveBuildingProgress") : 0;
    }

    public static boolean readExpandingToHive(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        return compound.contains("isExpandingToHive") && compound.getBoolean("isExpandingToHive");
    }
}

FILE: OvomorphHatchConfigAccess.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.hatch;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.EntityConfigHelper;

/**
 * Config accessors for ovomorph hatching parameters.
 */
public final class OvomorphHatchConfigAccess {

    private OvomorphHatchConfigAccess() {
    }

    public static boolean isProximityRequired() {
        return EntityConfigHelper.getConfigValueRequired(
                XenomorphType.OVOMORPH,
                config -> config.hatching != null ? Boolean.valueOf(config.hatching.proximityRequired) : null,
                "hatching.proximityRequired");
    }

    public static int hatchTime() {
        return EntityConfigHelper.getConfigValueRequired(
                XenomorphType.OVOMORPH,
                config -> config.hatching != null ? Integer.valueOf(config.hatching.hatchTime) : null,
                "hatching.hatchTime");
    }

    public static double proximityDistance() {
        return EntityConfigHelper.getConfigValueRequired(
                XenomorphType.OVOMORPH,
                config -> config.hatching != null ? Double.valueOf(config.hatching.proximityDistance) : null,
                "hatching.proximityDistance");
    }

    public static double spawnOffsetX() {
        return EntityConfigHelper.getConfigValueRequired(
                XenomorphType.OVOMORPH,
                config -> config.hatching != null ? Double.valueOf(config.hatching.spawnOffsetX) : null,
                "hatching.spawnOffsetX");
    }

    public static double spawnOffsetY() {
        return EntityConfigHelper.getConfigValueRequired(
                XenomorphType.OVOMORPH,
                config -> config.hatching != null ? Double.valueOf(config.hatching.spawnOffsetY) : null,
                "hatching.spawnOffsetY");
    }

    public static double spawnOffsetZ() {
        return EntityConfigHelper.getConfigValueRequired(
                XenomorphType.OVOMORPH,
                config -> config.hatching != null ? Double.valueOf(config.hatching.spawnOffsetZ) : null,
                "hatching.spawnOffsetZ");
    }

    public static String spawnEntityKey() {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH);
        if (config != null && config.hatching != null && config.hatching.spawnEntity != null) {
            return config.hatching.spawnEntity;
        }
        return null;
    }

    public static XenomorphType resolveSpawnForm() {
        String spawnEntity = spawnEntityKey();
        if (spawnEntity == null || spawnEntity.isBlank()) {
            return null;
        }
        for (XenomorphType type : XenomorphType.values()) {
            if (type.getConfigKey().equalsIgnoreCase(spawnEntity)
                    || type.name().equalsIgnoreCase(spawnEntity)) {
                return type;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    public static boolean hasHatchSound() {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH);
        return config != null && config.hatching != null && config.hatching.hatchSound != null;
    }
}

FILE: BlockDamageBridge.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai;

import java.util.Objects;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.combat.BlockDamageOrchestrator;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.core.registries.BuiltInRegistries;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

/**
 * Thin minecraft facade for xenomorph block damage — delegates to {@link BlockDamageOrchestrator}.
 */
public final class BlockDamageBridge {

    private BlockDamageBridge() {
    }

    public static boolean attemptBlockDamage(Mob entity, Level level, BlockPos pos) {
        if (entity == null || level == null || pos == null || level.isClientSide()) {
            return false;
        }
        if (!BoundaryServices.isInitialized()) {
            return false;
        }
        var state = level.getBlockState(pos);
        if (state.isAir()) {
            return false;
        }
        String blockId = Objects.requireNonNull(BuiltInRegistries.BLOCK.getKey(Objects.requireNonNull(state.getBlock()))).toString();
        BlockPosRef blockPos = BoundaryRefs.from(pos);
        return BlockDamageOrchestrator.attemptBlockDamage(
                BoundaryServices.worldMutation(),
                BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(level),
                blockPos,
                blockId,
                entity.getType().getDescription().getString());
    }
}

FILE: SignalAwareGoal.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.ai.AISignalType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.signals.AISignalData;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.signals.AISignalSystem;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.Goal;

/**
 * Minecraft Goal base that can respond to domain AI signals.
 */
public abstract class SignalAwareGoal extends Goal {

    protected final PathfinderMob entity;

    public SignalAwareGoal(PathfinderMob entity) {
        this.entity = entity;
    }

    protected long currentGameTime() {
        return entity.level() != null ? entity.level().getGameTime() : 0L;
    }

    protected AISignalData getSignal(AISignalType signalType, double maxDistance) {
        if (entity.level() == null || entity.level().isClientSide()) {
            return null;
        }
        BlockPosRef position = BoundaryRefs.from(entity.blockPosition());
        return AISignalSystem.getSignal(signalType, position, maxDistance, currentGameTime());
    }

    protected boolean hasSignalForEntity(AISignalType signalType, java.util.UUID entityId) {
        return AISignalSystem.hasSignalForEntity(signalType, entityId, currentGameTime());
    }

    protected AISignalData broadcastSignal(
            AISignalType signalType, BlockPos position, double radius, int durationTicks) {
        if (entity.level() == null || entity.level().isClientSide()) {
            return null;
        }
        return AISignalSystem.broadcastSignal(
                signalType,
                BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity),
                BoundaryRefs.from(position),
                radius,
                currentGameTime(),
                durationTicks,
                entity.getDisplayName().getString());
    }

    protected BlockPos getEntityPosition() {
        return entity.blockPosition();
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai.chestburster;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.AIConfigResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.growth.XenomorphTypeHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_2.ai.ChestbursterFoodHuntPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.attributes.Attributes;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.Goal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.targeting.TargetingConditions;

/**
 * Thin MC goal for chestburster food hunting: world scan, navigation, and attack binding.
 * Activation, target validation, and consumption benefits live in {@link ChestbursterFoodHuntPolicy}.
 */
public class HuntSmallAnimalsGoal extends Goal {
    private final PathfinderMob entity;
    private final EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals;
    private LivingEntity target;

    public HuntSmallAnimalsGoal(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        this.entity = entity;
        this.aiGoals = aiGoals;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean canUse() {
        XenomorphType type = XenomorphTypeHelper.getXenomorphType(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity));
        float healthRatio = entity.getMaxHealth() > 0 ? entity.getHealth() / entity.getMaxHealth() : 1.0f;
        if (!ChestbursterFoodHuntPolicy.shouldActivateHunt(
                Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity)),
                healthRatio,
                AIConfigResolver.getHealthThresholdForFood(type))) {
            return false;
        }

        double searchRadius = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromMovement(aiGoals, "safety_search_radius");

        this.target = entity.level().getNearestEntity(
                Objects.requireNonNull(entity.level().getEntitiesOfClass(
                        LivingEntity.class, Objects.requireNonNull(entity.getBoundingBox().inflate(searchRadius)))),
                Objects.requireNonNull(TargetingConditions.forCombat().range(searchRadius)),
                entity,
                entity.getX(),
                entity.getY(),
                entity.getZ());

        boolean canHunt = target != null
                && ChestbursterFoodHuntPolicy.isValidFoodTarget(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(target), aiGoals);
        if (canHunt) {
            ModLogger.debug("HuntSmallAnimalsGoal", "🍖 Found potential food target: " + target.getDisplayName().getString());
        }

        return canHunt;
    }

    @Override
    public void start() {
        if (target != null) {
            ModLogger.debug("HuntSmallAnimalsGoal", "🎯 Starting hunt for: " + target.getDisplayName().getString());
            entity.getNavigation().moveTo(Objects.requireNonNull(target), aiGoals.strollSpeed);
        }
    }

    @Override
    public void tick() {
        double attackDistance = ChestbursterFoodHuntPolicy.resolveAttackDistance(aiGoals);

        if (target != null && target.isAlive() && entity.distanceTo(Objects.requireNonNull(target)) < attackDistance) {
            target.hurt(
                    Objects.requireNonNull(entity.damageSources().mobAttack(entity)),
                    (float) entity.getAttributeValue(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.ATTACK_DAMAGE)));
            ModLogger.debug("HuntSmallAnimalsGoal", "⚔️ Attacking food target: " + target.getDisplayName().getString());

            ChestbursterFoodHuntPolicy.FoodConsumptionPlan plan = ChestbursterFoodHuntPolicy.planFoodConsumption(aiGoals);
            if (plan.healAmount() > 0) {
                entity.heal(plan.healAmount());
                ModLogger.debug("HuntSmallAnimalsGoal", "💚 Healed " + plan.healAmount() + " HP from eating");
            }

            ChestbursterFoodHuntPolicy.applyFoodBenefits(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity)), plan);
            ModLogger.info("HuntSmallAnimalsGoal", "✅ Successfully hunted and ate: " + target.getDisplayName().getString());
        }
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai.drone;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.ConfigCacheHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.CommonGoalRegistrar;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;

/**
 * Utility class for swarm movement behavior.
 * Handles movement modifications for swarm coordination.
 */
public class SwarmMovementGoal {

    public static void registerGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        ModLogger.debug("SwarmMovementGoal", "🏃 Registering swarm movement goals");

        EntityConfig config = ConfigCacheHelper.getConfig(XenomorphType.DRONE);
        double strollMultiplier = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromSpecialAbilities(
                config, "swarm_stroll_speed_multiplier");
        double swarmStrollSpeed = aiGoals.strollSpeed * strollMultiplier;

        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerFloatGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.DRONE, "float"));
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerStrollGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.DRONE, "stroll"), swarmStrollSpeed);

        ModLogger.debug("SwarmMovementGoal", "✅ Swarm movement goals registered - speed: " + swarmStrollSpeed);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai.drone;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.ConfigCacheHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.CommonGoalRegistrar;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;

/**
 * Utility class for swarm targeting behavior.
 * Handles targeting modifications for swarm coordination.
 */
public class SwarmTargetingGoal {

    public static void registerGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        EntityConfig config = ConfigCacheHelper.getConfig(XenomorphType.DRONE);
        double lookMultiplier = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromSpecialAbilities(
                config, "swarm_look_range_multiplier");
        float swarmLookRange = (float) (aiGoals.lookAtPlayerRange * lookMultiplier);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerLookAtPlayerGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.DRONE, "look"), swarmLookRange);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerRandomLookAroundGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.DRONE, "random_look"));
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai.facehugger;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.ai.BehaviorConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.CommonGoalRegistrar;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.target.NearestAttackableTargetGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;

/**
 * Utility class for stealth targeting behavior.
 * Handles targeting modifications for stealth coordination.
 * Extracted from StealthyHunterAI.java for single responsibility.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.3
 */
public class StealthTargetingGoal {
    
    /**
     * Registers targeting goals with stealth modifications.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register goals for
     * @param aiGoals The AI goals configuration from JSON
     */
    public static void registerGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        // Enhanced look range for target detection (from config using centralized helper) using centralized registrar (DRY)
        float stealthLookRange = aiGoals.lookAtPlayerRange *
            BehaviorConfigHelper.requireLookRangeMultiplier("stealthy_hunter");
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerLookAtPlayerGoal(
                entity,
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER, "look_at_player"),
                stealthLookRange);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerRandomLookAroundGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER, "random_look"));

        entity.targetSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER, "stealth_target"),
                new NearestAttackableTargetGoal<>(entity, Player.class, true));
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerHurtByTargetGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER, "hurt_by_target"));
    }
}

 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai.praetor_PLANNED;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.CommonGoalRegistrar;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.MeleeAttackGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.target.NearestAttackableTargetGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;

/**
 * Strategic Commander AI behavior - tactical, intelligent, coordinates others.
 * Used by Praetor entities for strategic command and coordination.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * Basic AI behavior works, but needs expansion/completion.
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class StrategicCommanderAI {
    
    /**
     * Registers strategic commander AI goals using configuration parameters.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register goals for
     * @param aiGoals The AI goals configuration from JSON
     */
    public static void registerGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        // Basic goals with strategic modifications using centralized registrar (DRY)
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerFloatGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.PRAETOR, "float"));

        double meleeMultiplier = AIConfigHelper.getDouble(aiGoals.specialAbilities, "strategic_melee_speed_multiplier", 0.8);
        double strategicSpeed = aiGoals.meleeAttackSpeed * meleeMultiplier;
        entity.goalSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.PRAETOR, "melee"),
                new MeleeAttackGoal(entity, strategicSpeed, false));

        double strollMultiplier = AIConfigHelper.getDouble(aiGoals.specialAbilities, "strategic_stroll_speed_multiplier", 0.7);
        double strategicStrollSpeed = aiGoals.strollSpeed * strollMultiplier;
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerStrollGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.PRAETOR, "stroll"), strategicStrollSpeed);

        double lookRangeMultiplier = AIConfigHelper.getDouble(aiGoals.specialAbilities, "command_look_range_multiplier", 2.0);
        float commandLookRange = aiGoals.lookAtPlayerRange * (float) lookRangeMultiplier;
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerLookAtPlayerGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.PRAETOR, "look"), commandLookRange);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerRandomLookAroundGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.PRAETOR, "random_look"));

        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerHurtByTargetGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.PRAETOR, "hurt_by_target"));
        entity.targetSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.PRAETOR, "target_player"),
                new NearestAttackableTargetGoal<>(entity, Player.class, true));
        // HumanEntity targeting removed for simplicity - focus on core functionality
        
        // TODO: Future strategic-specific goals (placeholders for systems not yet implemented):
        // - CommandDronesGoal (coordinate nearby drones)
        // - StrategicPositioningGoal (find optimal command position)
        // - ThreatAssessmentGoal (analyze and prioritize threats)
        // - ResourceManagementGoal (manage hive resources)
    }
}

FILE: BaseLabBlock.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.blocks;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.SoundType;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockBehaviour;
import net.minecraft.world.level.material.MapColor;
import net.minecraft.world.level.material.PushReaction;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks.BaseModBlock;

/**
 * Base class for all lab equipment blocks.
 * Provides lab-specific properties and behavior for human-made lab equipment.
 * 
 * This class extends BaseModBlock to inherit common functionality while providing:
 * - Lab-specific property creation (metallic/glass materials, tech sounds)
 * - Lab-specific default values for sound and map color
 * 
 * NOTE: Lab equipment is human-made, separate from xenomorph-created blocks
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public abstract class BaseLabBlock extends BaseModBlock {
    
    /**
     * Constructs a BaseLabBlock with the specified properties.
     * 
     * @param properties The block properties
     */
    protected BaseLabBlock(Properties properties) {
        super(properties);
        ModLogger.debug("Initialized lab equipment: " + getClass().getSimpleName());
    }
    
    /**
     * Creates the base properties for lab equipment blocks.
     * All lab blocks share these common characteristics.
     * 
     * @return The base properties for lab blocks
     */
    protected static BlockBehaviour.Properties createBaseProperties() {
        return BlockBehaviour.Properties.of()
                .mapColor(Objects.requireNonNull(MapColor.COLOR_GRAY))  // Metallic/tech appearance
                .sound(Objects.requireNonNull(SoundType.METAL))        // Tech/metal sound
                .pushReaction(PushReaction.NORMAL)  // Can be pushed by pistons
                .lightLevel((state) -> 0)       // No light emission by default
                .requiresCorrectToolForDrops(); // Requires appropriate tool
    }
    
    /**
     * Creates properties for glass/transparent lab equipment.
     * 
     * @return The properties for transparent lab blocks
     */
    protected static BlockBehaviour.Properties createGlassProperties() {
        return BlockBehaviour.Properties.of()
                .mapColor(Objects.requireNonNull(MapColor.NONE))        // Transparent
                .sound(Objects.requireNonNull(SoundType.GLASS))        // Glass sound
                .pushReaction(PushReaction.NORMAL)
                .lightLevel((state) -> 0)
                .noOcclusion()                 // Transparent
                .requiresCorrectToolForDrops();
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the sound type for this block.
     * Lab blocks default to metallic sound.
     * 
     * @return The SoundType for this block
     */
    @Override
    public SoundType getSoundType() {
        return SoundType.METAL;
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the map color for this block.
     * Lab blocks default to gray (metallic appearance).
     * 
     * @return The MapColor for this block
     */
    @Override
    @Nonnull
    protected MapColor getMapColor() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(MapColor.COLOR_GRAY);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.blocks;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.SoundType;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockBehaviour;
import net.minecraft.world.level.material.MapColor;
import net.minecraft.world.level.material.PushReaction;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks.BaseModBlock;

/**
 * Base class for all xenomorph-related blocks.
 * Provides xenomorph-specific properties and behavior for xenomorph-created blocks.
 * 
 * This class extends BaseModBlock to inherit common functionality while providing:
 * - Xenomorph-specific property creation (black color, organic slime sounds)
 * - Xenomorph-specific default values for sound and map color
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public abstract class BaseXenomorphBlock extends BaseModBlock {
    
    /**
     * Constructs a BaseXenomorphBlock with the specified properties.
     * 
     * @param properties The block properties
     */
    protected BaseXenomorphBlock(Properties properties) {
        super(properties);
        ModLogger.debug("Initialized " + getClass().getSimpleName());
    }
    
    /**
     * Creates the base properties for xenomorph blocks.
     * All xenomorph blocks share these common characteristics.
     * 
     * @return The base properties for xenomorph blocks
     */
    protected static BlockBehaviour.Properties createBaseProperties() {
        return BlockBehaviour.Properties.of()
                .mapColor(Objects.requireNonNull(MapColor.COLOR_BLACK))  // All xenomorph blocks are black
                .sound(Objects.requireNonNull(SoundType.SLIME_BLOCK))   // Organic, slimy sound
                .pushReaction(PushReaction.NORMAL)  // Can be pushed by pistons
                .lightLevel((state) -> 0)       // No light emission
                .requiresCorrectToolForDrops(); // Requires appropriate tool
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the sound type for this block.
     * Xenomorph blocks default to slime sound (organic, slimy).
     * 
     * @return The SoundType for this block
     */
    @Override
    public SoundType getSoundType() {
        return SoundType.SLIME_BLOCK;
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the map color for this block.
     * Xenomorph blocks default to black.
     * 
     * @return The MapColor for this block
     */
    @Override
    @Nonnull
    protected MapColor getMapColor() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(MapColor.COLOR_BLACK);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.blocks;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.core.HolderLookup;
import net.minecraft.nbt.CompoundTag;
import net.minecraft.network.chat.Component;
import net.minecraft.network.protocol.Packet;
import net.minecraft.network.protocol.game.ClientGamePacketListener;
import net.minecraft.network.protocol.game.ClientboundBlockEntityDataPacket;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.lab.SpecimenPodState;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodWorkflow;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodBlockView;

/**
 * Block entity for the specimen pod controller block.
 */
public class SpecimenPodBlockEntity extends BlockEntity implements SpecimenPodBlockView {

    private SpecimenPodState structureState = SpecimenPodState.UNFORMED;
    private List<BlockPos> structureBlocks = new ArrayList<>();
    private BlockPos structureCenter;
    private int structureSize = 3;
    private String specimenType = "none";
    private boolean hasSpecimen = false;

    private SpecimenPodPort port;

    public SpecimenPodBlockEntity(BlockEntityType<?> type, BlockPos pos, BlockState state) {
        super(type, pos, state);
        ModLogger.debug("Created SpecimenPodBlockEntity at " + pos);
    }

    public void bindPort(SpecimenPodPort podPort) {
        this.port = podPort;
    }

    private SpecimenPodPort requirePort() {
        if (port == null) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("SpecimenPodPort not bound");
        }
        return port;
    }

    @Override
    public void loadAdditional(@Nonnull CompoundTag tag, @Nonnull HolderLookup.Provider lookupProvider) {
        super.loadAdditional(tag, lookupProvider);

        String stateName = tag.contains("structureState")
                ? tag.getString("structureState")
                : SpecimenPodState.UNFORMED.name();
        try {
            this.structureState = SpecimenPodState.valueOf(stateName);
        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
            ModLogger.warn("SpecimenPodBlockEntity", "Invalid structure state: " + stateName + ", defaulting to UNFORMED");
            this.structureState = SpecimenPodState.UNFORMED;
        }

        this.specimenType = tag.contains("specimenType") ? tag.getString("specimenType") : "none";
        this.hasSpecimen = tag.contains("hasSpecimen") ? tag.getBoolean("hasSpecimen") : false;
        this.structureSize = tag.contains("structureSize") ? tag.getInt("structureSize") : 3;
        this.structureCenter = tag.contains("structureCenter") ? BlockPos.of(tag.getLong("structureCenter")) : null;

        this.structureBlocks = new ArrayList<>();
        if (tag.contains("structureBlocks")) {
            for (long encoded : tag.getLongArray("structureBlocks")) {
                this.structureBlocks.add(BlockPos.of(encoded));
            }
        }

        ModLogger.debug("Loaded SpecimenPodBlockEntity state: " + structureState);
    }

    @Override
    protected void saveAdditional(@Nonnull CompoundTag tag, @Nonnull HolderLookup.Provider lookupProvider) {
        super.saveAdditional(tag, lookupProvider);

        tag.putString("structureState", Objects.requireNonNull(structureState.name()));
        tag.putString("specimenType", Objects.requireNonNull(specimenType));
        tag.putBoolean("hasSpecimen", hasSpecimen);
        tag.putInt("structureSize", structureSize);

        if (structureCenter != null) {
            tag.putLong("structureCenter", structureCenter.asLong());
        }

        if (!structureBlocks.isEmpty()) {
            long[] encodedBlocks = structureBlocks.stream().mapToLong(pos -> pos.asLong()).toArray();
            tag.putLongArray("structureBlocks", Objects.requireNonNull(encodedBlocks));
        }
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public CompoundTag getUpdateTag(@Nonnull HolderLookup.Provider registries) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(this.saveWithoutMetadata(registries));
    }

    @Override
    public Packet<ClientGamePacketListener> getUpdatePacket() {
        return ClientboundBlockEntityDataPacket.create(this);
    }

    public static void tick(Level level, BlockPos pos, BlockState state, SpecimenPodBlockView blockView) {
        if (level == null || level.isClientSide || !(blockView instanceof SpecimenPodBlockEntity blockEntity)) {
            return;
        }
        SpecimenPodWorkflow.processPeriodicTick(blockEntity.requirePort(), level.getGameTime());
    }

    @Override
    public boolean validateStructure() {
        return SpecimenPodWorkflow.validateStructure(requirePort());
    }

    @Override
    public void breakStructure() {
        SpecimenPodWorkflow.breakStructure(requirePort());
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isFormed() {
        return structureState.isFormed();
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public String getSpecimenType() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(specimenType);
    }

    @Override
    public void setSpecimenType(@Nonnull String type) {
        this.specimenType = type;
        setChanged();
    }

    @Override
    public boolean hasSpecimen() {
        return hasSpecimen;
    }

    @Override
    public int getStructureSize() {
        return structureSize;
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public Component formatStatusMessage(@Nonnull String translationPrefix) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(Component.translatable(
                translationPrefix + ".status",
                structureSize, structureSize, structureSize,
                Component.translatable("message.weylandyutani.specimen_pod.contains", specimenType)));
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public Component formatEmptyMessage(@Nonnull String translationPrefix) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(Component.translatable(
                translationPrefix + ".status",
                structureSize, structureSize, structureSize,
                Component.translatable(translationPrefix + ".empty")));
    }

    public void setStructureStateInternal(SpecimenPodState state) {
        this.structureState = state;
        if (!state.isFormed()) {
            this.structureCenter = null;
        }
    }

    public void setStructureCenterInternal(BlockPos center) {
        this.structureCenter = center;
    }

    public void setStructureSizeInternal(int size) {
        this.structureSize = size;
    }

    public List<BlockPos> getStructureBlocksInternal() {
        return structureBlocks;
    }

    public void setStructureBlocksInternal(List<BlockPos> blocks) {
        this.structureBlocks = new ArrayList<>(blocks);
    }

    public void clearSpecimenDataInternal() {
        this.hasSpecimen = false;
        this.specimenType = "none";
    }

    public SpecimenPodState getStructureState() {
        return structureState;
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.blocks;

import java.util.Objects;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.network.chat.Component;
import net.minecraft.world.InteractionHand;
import net.minecraft.world.InteractionResult;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.EntityBlock;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntityTicker;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockBehaviour;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.BlockHitResult;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.shapes.VoxelShape;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodVariant;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodBlockView;

/**
 * Controller block for the specimen pod multiblock structure.
 */
public class SpecimenPodControllerBlock extends BaseLabBlock implements EntityBlock {

    private static final VoxelShape SHAPE = createFullBlockShape();

    protected final SpecimenPodVariant variant;

    public SpecimenPodControllerBlock(BlockBehaviour.Properties properties) {
        this(properties, SpecimenPodVariant.GENERIC);
    }

    protected SpecimenPodControllerBlock(BlockBehaviour.Properties properties, SpecimenPodVariant variant) {
        super(properties);
        this.variant = variant;
    }

    public static SpecimenPodControllerBlock forVariant(BlockBehaviour.Properties properties, SpecimenPodVariant variant) {
        return new SpecimenPodControllerBlock(properties, variant);
    }

    @Override
    protected VoxelShape getBlockShape() {
        return SHAPE;
    }

    @Override
    public BlockEntity newBlockEntity(@Nonnull BlockPos pos, @Nonnull BlockState state) {
        return SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration.create(pos, state);
    }

    @Override
    @Nullable
    public <T extends BlockEntity> BlockEntityTicker<T> getTicker(
            @Nonnull Level level, @Nonnull BlockState state, @Nonnull BlockEntityType<T> type) {
        if (level.isClientSide) {
            return null;
        }
        return SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration.serverTicker();
    }

    public InteractionResult use(
            @Nonnull BlockState state,
            @Nonnull Level level,
            @Nonnull BlockPos pos,
            @Nonnull Player player,
            @Nonnull InteractionHand hand,
            @Nonnull BlockHitResult hit) {
        if (level.isClientSide) {
            return InteractionResult.SUCCESS;
        }

        BlockEntity blockEntity = level.getBlockEntity(pos);
        if (blockEntity instanceof SpecimenPodBlockView podEntity) {
            if (!podEntity.isFormed()) {
                handleStructureFormation(podEntity, player, pos);
            } else {
                handleFormedStructureInteraction(podEntity, player, pos);
            }
        }

        return InteractionResult.SUCCESS;
    }

    protected void handleStructureFormation(
            @Nonnull SpecimenPodBlockView podEntity, @Nonnull Player player, @Nonnull BlockPos pos) {
        if (podEntity.validateStructure()) {
            podEntity.setSpecimenType(Objects.requireNonNull(variant.specimenType()));
            player.sendSystemMessage(Objects.requireNonNull(Component.translatable(
                    Objects.requireNonNull(variant.translationPrefix()) + ".structure_formed")));
            ModLogger.info(variant.logPrefix(), "Structure formed by " + player.getName().getString() + " at " + pos);
        } else {
            player.sendSystemMessage(Objects.requireNonNull(
                    Component.translatable("message.weylandyutani.specimen_pod.invalid_structure")));
            ModLogger.debug(variant.logPrefix(), "Invalid structure attempt by " + player.getName().getString() + " at " + pos);
        }
    }

    protected void handleFormedStructureInteraction(
            @Nonnull SpecimenPodBlockView podEntity, @Nonnull Player player, @Nonnull BlockPos pos) {
        Component statusMessage = podEntity.hasSpecimen()
                ? Objects.requireNonNull(podEntity.formatStatusMessage(Objects.requireNonNull(variant.translationPrefix())))
                : Objects.requireNonNull(podEntity.formatEmptyMessage(Objects.requireNonNull(variant.translationPrefix())));
        player.sendSystemMessage(statusMessage);
        ModLogger.debug(variant.logPrefix(), "Player " + player.getName().getString() + " interacted with formed pod at " + pos);
    }

    @Override
    public void onRemove(
            @Nonnull BlockState state,
            @Nonnull Level level,
            @Nonnull BlockPos pos,
            @Nonnull BlockState newState,
            boolean isMoving) {
        if (!state.is(Objects.requireNonNull(newState.getBlock()))) {
            BlockEntity blockEntity = level.getBlockEntity(pos);
            if (blockEntity != null && blockEntity instanceof SpecimenPodBlockView podEntity) {
                podEntity.breakStructure();
            }
        }
        super.onRemove(state, level, pos, newState, isMoving);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.boundary;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.core.particles.ParticleTypes;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.attributes.AttributeModifier;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.common.NeoForgeMod;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.spawn.SpawnContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_2.entity.EntityPresentationPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeLevelResolver;

public final class NeoForgeEntityPresentationAdapter implements EntityPresentationPort {

    private static final ResourceLocation FACEHUGGER_FLIGHT_LOCK_ID = Objects.requireNonNull(
            ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath(ModContext.MOD_ID, "facehugger_attachment_flight_lock"));

    private final MinecraftServer server;

    public NeoForgeEntityPresentationAdapter(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        this.server = server;
    }

    @Override
    public String displayName(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref).map(entity -> entity.getDisplayName().getString()).orElse("");
    }

    @Override
    public float healthRatio(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref)
                .map(entity -> entity.getHealth() / entity.getMaxHealth())
                .orElse(1.0f);
    }

    @Override
    public void applyMagicDamage(LivingEntityRef target, float amount) {
        resolve(target).ifPresent(living -> living.hurt(
                Objects.requireNonNull(living.damageSources().magic()), amount));
    }

    @Override
    public void spawnDamageIndicatorParticles(LivingEntityRef ref, int count, float spread) {
        resolve(ref).ifPresent(living -> {
            if (living.level() instanceof net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel serverLevel) {
                serverLevel.sendParticles(
                        Objects.requireNonNull(ParticleTypes.DAMAGE_INDICATOR),
                        living.getX(),
                        living.getY() + living.getBbHeight() * 0.5,
                        living.getZ(),
                        count,
                        spread, spread, spread,
                        0.1);
            }
        });
    }

    @Override
    public void spawnExplosionParticles(LivingEntityRef ref, int count, float spread) {
        resolve(ref).ifPresent(living -> {
            if (living.level() instanceof net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel serverLevel) {
                serverLevel.sendParticles(
                        Objects.requireNonNull(ParticleTypes.EXPLOSION),
                        living.getX(),
                        living.getY() + living.getBbHeight() * 0.5,
                        living.getZ(),
                        count,
                        spread, spread, spread,
                        0.5);
            }
        });
    }

    @Override
    public SpawnContext spawnContextAt(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref)
                .map(living -> SpawnContext.at(
                        BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(living.level()),
                        living.getX(),
                        living.getY(),
                        living.getZ(),
                        living.getYRot(),
                        living.getXRot(),
                        living.getYHeadRot()))
                .orElseGet(() -> SpawnContext.at(
                        BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(server.overworld()), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0));
    }

    @Override
    public void setInvulnerable(LivingEntityRef ref, boolean value) {
        resolve(ref).ifPresent(entity -> entity.setInvulnerable(value));
    }

    @Override
    public void setNoGravity(LivingEntityRef ref, boolean value) {
        resolve(ref).ifPresent(entity -> entity.setNoGravity(value));
    }

    @Override
    public void setDeltaMovement(LivingEntityRef ref, double x, double y, double z) {
        resolve(ref).ifPresent(entity -> entity.setDeltaMovement(x, y, z));
    }

    @Override
    public void setRotation(LivingEntityRef ref, float yRot, float xRot) {
        resolve(ref).ifPresent(entity -> {
            entity.setYRot(yRot);
            entity.setXRot(xRot);
        });
    }

    @Override
    public void positionOnHost(LivingEntityRef facehugger, LivingEntityRef host, double faceHeightRatio) {
        resolve(facehugger).ifPresent(fh -> resolve(host).ifPresent(h -> {
            double faceY = h.getY() + h.getBbHeight() * faceHeightRatio;
            fh.setPos(h.getX(), faceY, h.getZ());
            fh.setNoGravity(true);
            fh.setDeltaMovement(0, 0, 0);
        }));
    }

    @Override
    public double distance(LivingEntityRef a, LivingEntityRef b) {
        LivingEntity first = resolve(a).orElse(null);
        LivingEntity second = resolve(b).orElse(null);
        if (first == null || second == null) {
            return Double.MAX_VALUE;
        }
        return first.distanceTo(second);
    }

    @Override
    public int tickCount(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return resolve(ref).map(entity -> entity.tickCount).orElse(0);
    }

    @Override
    public void releaseUsingItem(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        resolve(ref).ifPresent(entity -> {
            if (entity.isUsingItem()) {
                entity.releaseUsingItem();
            }
        });
    }

    @Override
    public void applyPlayerAttachmentPose(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        resolve(ref)
                .filter(entity -> entity instanceof Player)
                .map(entity -> (Player) entity)
                .ifPresent(player -> {
            player.setXRot(90.0f);
            player.setSprinting(false);
            player.setSwimming(false);
            player.setJumping(false);
            player.getAbilities().flying = false;
            lockCreativeFlight(player);
            player.getAbilities().invulnerable = false;
            player.getAbilities().mayBuild = false;
            player.onUpdateAbilities();
            player.stopUsingItem();
        });
    }

    @Override
    public void restorePlayerAttachmentPose(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        resolve(ref)
                .filter(entity -> entity instanceof Player)
                .map(entity -> (Player) entity)
                .ifPresent(player -> {
            player.setXRot(0.0f);
            player.getAbilities().mayBuild = true;
            unlockCreativeFlight(player);
            player.getAbilities().flying = false;
            player.onUpdateAbilities();
        });
    }

    private static void lockCreativeFlight(Player player) {
        var flight = player.getAttribute(Objects.requireNonNull(NeoForgeMod.CREATIVE_FLIGHT));
        if (flight != null && !flight.hasModifier(Objects.requireNonNull(FACEHUGGER_FLIGHT_LOCK_ID))) {
            flight.addTransientModifier(new AttributeModifier(
                    Objects.requireNonNull(FACEHUGGER_FLIGHT_LOCK_ID),
                    -1.0,
                    AttributeModifier.Operation.ADD_MULTIPLIED_TOTAL));
        }
    }

    private static void unlockCreativeFlight(Player player) {
        var flight = player.getAttribute(Objects.requireNonNull(NeoForgeMod.CREATIVE_FLIGHT));
        if (flight != null) {
            flight.removeModifier(Objects.requireNonNull(FACEHUGGER_FLIGHT_LOCK_ID));
        }
    }

    private Optional<LivingEntity> resolve(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        if (ref == null) {
            return Optional.empty();
        }
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, ref.world())
                .flatMap(level -> {
                    var entity = level.getEntity(Objects.requireNonNull(ref.entityId()));
                    if (entity instanceof LivingEntity living) {
                        return Optional.of(living);
                    }
                    return Optional.empty();
                });
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeFacehuggerSpentTransitionAdapter.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.boundary;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AttachmentConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.parasite.FacehuggerAttachmentEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.parasite.FacehuggerSpentTransitionPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_3.parasite.FacehuggerTickWorkflow;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeLevelResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.facehugger.FacehuggerSpentGoals;

/**
 * NeoForge binding for {@link FacehuggerSpentTransitionPort}.
 */
public final class NeoForgeFacehuggerSpentTransitionAdapter implements FacehuggerSpentTransitionPort {

    private static final String LOG = "FacehuggerSpent";

    private final MinecraftServer server;

    public NeoForgeFacehuggerSpentTransitionAdapter(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        this.server = server;
    }

    @Override
    public void initializeSpentSession(LivingEntityRef facehugger) {
        FacehuggerAttachmentEntity entity = require(facehugger);
        FacehuggerTickWorkflow.applyMarkAsSpent(entity);
        configureSpentWanderGoals(entity);
        int spentWanderTime = AttachmentConfigHelper.getSpentWanderTime();
        ModLogger.info(LOG, String.format("🦾 Facehugger spent session initialized — wander for %d ticks",
                spentWanderTime));
    }

    @Override
    public void resumeSpentWandering(LivingEntityRef facehugger) {
        configureSpentWanderGoals(require(facehugger));
        ModLogger.info(LOG, "🦾 Facehugger spent wandering resumed from save");
    }

    private static void configureSpentWanderGoals(FacehuggerAttachmentEntity entity) {
        if (entity instanceof PathfinderMob pathfinderMob) {
            FacehuggerSpentGoals.registerWanderGoals(pathfinderMob);
        }
    }

    @Nonnull
    private FacehuggerAttachmentEntity require(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        FacehuggerAttachmentEntity contract = resolve(entity);
        if (contract == null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Entity does not support spent transition: " + entity);
        }
        return contract;
    }

    private FacehuggerAttachmentEntity resolve(LivingEntityRef entity) {
        LivingEntity living = resolveEntity(entity).orElse(null);
        if (living instanceof FacehuggerAttachmentEntity attachment) {
            return attachment;
        }
        return null;
    }

    private Optional<LivingEntity> resolveEntity(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, ref.world())
                .flatMap(serverLevel -> {
                    var entity = serverLevel.getEntity(Objects.requireNonNull(ref.entityId()));
                    if (entity instanceof LivingEntity living) {
                        return Optional.of(living);
                    }
                    return Optional.empty();
                });
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgePositionSearchAdapter.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.boundary;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.Vec3Ref;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.BlockPosSearchPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.Vec3SearchPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.Vec3;

/**
 * L3 bridge: PathfinderMob + MC positions ↔ L2 search policies.
 */
public final class NeoForgePositionSearchAdapter {

    @FunctionalInterface
    public interface BlockPosPredicate {
        boolean test(BlockPos pos);
    }

    @FunctionalInterface
    public interface Vec3Predicate {
        boolean test(Vec3 pos);
    }

    private NeoForgePositionSearchAdapter() {}

    public static BlockPos searchBlockPosInRadius(
            PathfinderMob entity,
            double maxRadius,
            int attemptsPerRadius,
            BlockPosPredicate predicate) {
        if (entity == null || entity.level() == null || predicate == null) {
            return null;
        }

        BlockPosRef center = BoundaryRefs.from(entity.blockPosition());
        BlockPosRef found = BlockPosSearchPolicy.searchInRadius(
                center,
                maxRadius,
                attemptsPerRadius,
                bound -> entity.getRandom().nextInt(bound),
                ref -> predicate.test(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(ref)));
        return found != null ? BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(found) : null;
    }

    public static Vec3 searchVec3InRadius(
            PathfinderMob entity,
            Vec3 baseDirection,
            double baseDistance,
            int maxAttempts,
            Vec3Predicate predicate) {
        if (entity == null || entity.level() == null || baseDirection == null || predicate == null) {
            return null;
        }

        Vec3Ref origin = new Vec3Ref(entity.getX(), entity.getY(), entity.getZ());
        Vec3Ref direction = new Vec3Ref(baseDirection.x, baseDirection.y, baseDirection.z);
        Vec3Ref found = Vec3SearchPolicy.search(
                origin,
                direction,
                baseDistance,
                maxAttempts,
                bound -> entity.getRandom().nextInt(bound),
                ref -> predicate.test(new Vec3(ref.x(), ref.y(), ref.z())));
        return found != null ? new Vec3(found.x(), found.y(), found.z()) : null;
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeSpawnLocationAdapter.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.boundary;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.SpawnSuitabilityRules;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.spawn.SpawnLocationSearchPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;

/**
 * L3 adapter: MC block probes + L0 suitability rules + L2 search loop.
 */
public final class NeoForgeSpawnLocationAdapter {

    private NeoForgeSpawnLocationAdapter() {}

    @Nullable
    public static BlockPos findSafeSpawnLocation(
            @Nonnull Level level,
            @Nonnull BlockPos originalPos,
            int searchRadius,
            int maxHeight) {
        validateSearchParams(level, originalPos, searchRadius, maxHeight);
        ModLogger.startTimer("SpawnLocationSearch");
        try {
            ModLogger.debug("NeoForgeSpawnLocationAdapter",
                    "Searching for safe spawn location around " + originalPos
                            + " (radius: " + searchRadius + ", height: " + maxHeight + ")");

            BlockPosRef origin = BoundaryRefs.from(originalPos);
            BlockPosRef found = SpawnLocationSearchPolicy.findFirstSuitable(
                    origin, searchRadius, maxHeight, ref -> isSafeSpawnLocation(level, ref));
            if (found != null) {
                BlockPos result = BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(found);
                ModLogger.success("NeoForgeSpawnLocationAdapter", "Found safe spawn location at: " + result);
                return result;
            }
            ModLogger.warn("NeoForgeSpawnLocationAdapter", "No safe spawn location found");
            return null;
        } finally {
            ModLogger.endTimer("SpawnLocationSearch");
        }
    }

    @Nullable
    public static BlockPos findSafeSpawnLocationForEntity(
            @Nonnull Level level,
            @Nonnull BlockPos originalPos,
            int entityHeight,
            int entityWidth) {
        int searchRadius = Math.max(5, entityWidth + 1);
        int maxHeight = Math.max(10, entityHeight + 2);
        BlockPosRef origin = BoundaryRefs.from(originalPos);
        BlockPosRef found = SpawnLocationSearchPolicy.findFirstSuitable(
                origin,
                searchRadius,
                maxHeight,
                ref -> isSafeSpawnLocationForEntity(level, ref, entityHeight, entityWidth));
        return found != null ? BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(found) : null;
    }

    private static void validateSearchParams(
            @Nonnull Level level,
            @Nonnull BlockPos originalPos,
            int searchRadius,
            int maxHeight) {
        if (searchRadius <= 0) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Search radius must be positive");
        }
        if (maxHeight <= 0) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Max height must be positive");
        }
    }

    private static boolean isSafeSpawnLocation(@Nonnull Level level, BlockPosRef pos) {
        return SpawnSuitabilityRules.isSafeSpawn(
                isAirBlock(level, pos),
                hasSolidGroundBelow(level, pos),
                hasEnoughVerticalSpace(level, pos, 2));
    }

    private static boolean isSafeSpawnLocationForEntity(
            @Nonnull Level level, BlockPosRef pos, int entityHeight, int entityWidth) {
        return SpawnSuitabilityRules.isSafeSpawnForEntity(
                isAirBlock(level, pos),
                hasSolidGroundBelow(level, pos),
                hasEnoughVerticalSpace(level, pos, entityHeight),
                hasEnoughHorizontalSpace(level, pos, entityWidth));
    }

    private static boolean isAirBlock(@Nonnull Level level, BlockPosRef pos) {
        return level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(pos))).isAir();
    }

    private static boolean hasSolidGroundBelow(@Nonnull Level level, BlockPosRef pos) {
        BlockState belowBlock = level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(pos.below())));
        return !belowBlock.isAir() && belowBlock.canOcclude();
    }

    private static boolean hasEnoughVerticalSpace(@Nonnull Level level, BlockPosRef pos, int height) {
        for (int y = 1; y <= height; y++) {
            if (!isAirBlock(level, pos.offset(0, y, 0))) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        return true;
    }

    private static boolean hasEnoughHorizontalSpace(@Nonnull Level level, BlockPosRef pos, int entityWidth) {
        int halfWidth = entityWidth / 2;
        for (int x = -halfWidth; x <= halfWidth; x++) {
            for (int z = -halfWidth; z <= halfWidth; z++) {
                if (x == 0 && z == 0) {
                    continue;
                }
                if (!isAirBlock(level, pos.offset(x, 0, z))) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        return true;
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeWorldMutationAdapter.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.boundary;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.core.registries.BuiltInRegistries;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.Block;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.WorldRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.world.WorldMutationPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeLevelResolver;

public final class NeoForgeWorldMutationAdapter implements WorldMutationPort {

    private final MinecraftServer server;

    public NeoForgeWorldMutationAdapter(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        this.server = server;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean breakBlock(WorldRef world, BlockPosRef pos) {
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, world)
                .map(level -> level.destroyBlock(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(pos)), true))
                .orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean placeBlock(WorldRef world, BlockPosRef pos, String blockId) {
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, world)
                .map(level -> {
                    Block block = Objects.requireNonNull(BuiltInRegistries.BLOCK.get(
                            Objects.requireNonNull(ResourceLocation.parse(Objects.requireNonNull(blockId)))));
                    BlockState state = Objects.requireNonNull(block.defaultBlockState());
                    return level.setBlock(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(pos)), state, 3);
                })
                .orElse(false);
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeWorldQueryAdapter.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.boundary;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.UUID;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.core.registries.BuiltInRegistries;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.AABB;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.EntityScanHit;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.WorldRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.spatial.AxisAlignedRegion;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_2.world.WorldQueryPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeLevelResolver;

public final class NeoForgeWorldQueryAdapter implements WorldQueryPort {

    private final MinecraftServer server;

    public NeoForgeWorldQueryAdapter(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        this.server = server;
    }

    @Override
    public List<EntityScanHit> scanLivingEntities(WorldRef world, AxisAlignedRegion region) {
        List<EntityScanHit> hits = new ArrayList<>();
        NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, world).ifPresent(level -> {
            AABB box = new AABB(
                    region.min().x(), region.min().y(), region.min().z(),
                    region.max().x(), region.max().y(), region.max().z());
            for (LivingEntity living : level.getEntitiesOfClass(LivingEntity.class, Objects.requireNonNull(box), entity -> true)) {
                UUID entityId = Objects.requireNonNull(living.getUUID(), "living entity UUID");
                hits.add(new EntityScanHit(entityId, living.distanceToSqr(Objects.requireNonNull(box.getCenter()))));
            }
        });
        return hits;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isAirAt(WorldRef world, BlockPosRef pos) {
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, world)
                .map(level -> level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(pos))).isAir())
                .orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean canOccludeAt(WorldRef world, BlockPosRef pos) {
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, world)
                .map(level -> level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(pos))).canOcclude())
                .orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isInBounds(WorldRef world, BlockPosRef pos) {
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, world)
                .map(level -> level.isInWorldBounds(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(pos))))
                .orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isUnbreakableAt(WorldRef world, BlockPosRef pos) {
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, world)
                .map(level -> {
                    BlockPos blockPos = Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(pos));
                    var state = level.getBlockState(blockPos);
                    return state.getDestroySpeed(level, blockPos) < 0.0F;
                })
                .orElse(false);
    }

    @Override
    public String blockIdAt(WorldRef world, BlockPosRef pos) {
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, world)
                .map(level -> {
                    var block = level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(pos))).getBlock();
                    @Nullable ResourceLocation key = BuiltInRegistries.BLOCK.getKey(Objects.requireNonNull(block));
                    return key != null ? key.toString() : "";
                })
                .orElse("");
    }
}

FILE: BaseConfigLoader.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.config;

import com.google.gson.Gson;
import com.google.gson.GsonBuilder;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.io.ResourceLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.registry.ConfigLoaderBase;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.MinecraftResourceLoader;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.server.packs.resources.ResourceManager;

/**
 * Abstract base class for configuration loaders using Minecraft's ResourceManager.
 * Extends ConfigLoaderBase and provides ResourceManager-based resource loading.
 * 
 * This abstract class implements the DRY principle by centralizing:
 * - Common loading lifecycle (load, validate, cache, reload)
 * - Standardized error handling and logging patterns
 * - Resource path building helpers
 * - Validation framework
 * - Thread-safe caching
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * Enhanced to extend ConfigLoaderBase and use ResourceLoader strategy pattern.
 * Supports flexible resource loading while maintaining backward compatibility.
 * 
 * @param <T> The type of configuration object this loader manages
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public abstract class BaseConfigLoader<T> extends ConfigLoaderBase<T> {
    
    protected static final Gson GSON = new GsonBuilder().setPrettyPrinting().create();
    protected ResourceLoader resourceLoader;
    protected ResourceManager resourceManager;
    
    /**
     * Constructs a BaseConfigLoader with the specified name.
     * 
     * @param loaderName The name of this loader for logging purposes
     */
    protected BaseConfigLoader(String loaderName) {
        super(loaderName);
    }
    
    /**
     * Sets the ResourceManager and creates a MinecraftResourceLoader.
     * Must be called before loadConfigs().
     * 
     * @param resourceManager The Minecraft ResourceManager
     */
    public void setResourceManager(ResourceManager resourceManager) {
        this.resourceManager = resourceManager;
        this.resourceLoader = new MinecraftResourceLoader(Objects.requireNonNull(resourceManager));
    }
    
    /**
     * Sets a custom ResourceLoader strategy.
     * Allows using different resource loading mechanisms.
     * 
     * @param resourceLoader The resource loader to use
     */
    protected void setResourceLoader(ResourceLoader resourceLoader) {
        this.resourceLoader = resourceLoader;
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the resource path for a specific configuration.
     * Subclasses must implement this to define where their configs are located.
     * 
     * @param configName The name of the configuration
     * @return The resource path for the configuration
     */
    protected abstract String getResourcePath(String configName);
    
    /**
     * Gets the class type for deserialization.
     * Subclasses must implement this to define their config class.
     * 
     * @return The class type for this loader's configuration
     */
    protected abstract Class<T> getConfigClass();
    
    /**
     * Validates a loaded configuration.
     * Subclasses can override this for custom validation logic.
     * 
     * @param config The configuration to validate
     * @param configName The name of the configuration
     * @return True if the configuration is valid
     */
    protected boolean validateConfig(T config, String configName) {
        return config != null;
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the default configuration names to load.
     * Subclasses must implement this to define which configs to load by default.
     * 
     * @return Array of default configuration names
     */
    protected abstract String[] getDefaultConfigNames();
    
    /**
     * Loads all configurations from JSON files.
     * Requires ResourceManager to be set via setResourceManager() or loadConfigs(ResourceManager).
     */
    @Override
    public void loadConfigs() {
        if (resourceManager == null) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("ResourceManager not set. Call setResourceManager() or loadConfigs(ResourceManager) first.");
        }
        loadConfigs(resourceManager);
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads all configurations from JSON files.
     * Sets ResourceManager and delegates to loadConfigs().
     * 
     * @param resourceManager The resource manager to load from
     */
    public void loadConfigs(ResourceManager resourceManager) {
        setResourceManager(resourceManager);
        
        if (loaded) {
            ModLogger.debug(loaderName + " configurations already loaded");
            return;
        }
        
        ModLogger.loading("Loading " + loaderName + " configurations...");
        ModLogger.startTimer(loaderName + "_load");
        
        try {
            clearConfigs();
            String[] configNames = getDefaultConfigNames();
            for (String configName : configNames) {
                loadConfig(configName);
            }
            
            setLoaded(true);
            ModLogger.endTimer(loaderName + "_load");
            ModLogger.success("Loaded " + getConfigCount() + " " + loaderName + " configurations");
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("Failed to load " + loaderName + " configurations", e);
            throw new RuntimeException("Failed to load " + loaderName + " configurations", e);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Loads a specific configuration.
     * 
     * @param configName The name of the configuration to load
     */
    protected void loadConfig(String configName) {
        if (resourceLoader == null) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("ResourceLoader not initialized. Call setResourceManager() first.");
        }
        
        try {
            String resourcePath = getResourcePath(configName);
            com.google.gson.JsonObject jsonData = resourceLoader.loadJson(resourcePath, this.getClass());
            
            if (jsonData != null) {
                T config = GSON.fromJson(jsonData, getConfigClass());
                
                if (validateConfig(config, configName)) {
                    putConfig(configName, config);
                    ModLogger.success("Loaded " + loaderName + " config: " + configName);
                } else {
                    ModLogger.warn("Invalid " + loaderName + " config: " + configName);
                }
            } else {
                ModLogger.warn(loaderName + " config not found: " + configName);
            }
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("Failed to load " + loaderName + " config " + configName, e);
            throw new RuntimeException("Failed to load " + loaderName + " config " + configName, e);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a configuration by name.
     * 
     * @param configName The name of the configuration
     * @return The configuration, or null if not found
     */
    public T getConfig(String configName) {
        if (!loaded) {
            ModLogger.warn("Attempting to get config before " + loaderName + " is loaded: " + configName);
            return null;
        }
        return super.getConfigInternal(configName);
    }
    
    /**
     * Reloads all configurations.
     * Requires ResourceManager to be set.
     */
    @Override
    public void reloadConfigs() {
        if (resourceManager == null) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("ResourceManager not set. Cannot reload.");
        }
        reloadConfigs(resourceManager);
    }
    
    /**
     * Reloads all configurations.
     * 
     * @param resourceManager The resource manager
     */
    public void reloadConfigs(ResourceManager resourceManager) {
        ModLogger.loading("Reloading " + loaderName + " configurations...");
        clearConfigs();
        setLoaded(false);
        loadConfigs(resourceManager);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets all loaded configuration names.
     * 
     * @return Set of all loaded configuration names
     */
    public java.util.Set<String> getLoadedConfigNames() {
        return getConfigNames();
    }
}
