package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.effects;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffect;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffectCategory;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.entity.EntityValidationHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;

/**
 * Base class for all xenomorph-related effects.
 * Provides common effect logic and behavior shared across xenomorph effects.
 * 
 * This abstract class implements the DRY principle by centralizing:
 * - Common effect configuration access patterns
 * - Standardized logging for effect lifecycle events
 * - Common error handling and validation
 * - Effect lifecycle hooks (onApply, onTick, onRemove)
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.0.1
 */
public abstract class BaseXenomorphEffect extends MobEffect {
    
    /**
     * Constructs a BaseXenomorphEffect with the specified category and color.
     * 
     * @param category The effect category (HARMFUL, BENEFICIAL, NEUTRAL)
     * @param color The color of the effect
     */
    protected BaseXenomorphEffect(MobEffectCategory category, int color) {
        super(category, color);
        ModLogger.debug("Initialized " + getClass().getSimpleName());
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the effect name for logging purposes.
     * 
     * @return The name of this effect
     */
    protected String getEffectName() {
        return getClass().getSimpleName();
    }
    
    /**
     * Called when the effect is applied to an entity.
     * Subclasses can override this for custom application logic.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity the effect is being applied to
     * @param amplifier The amplifier level
     */
    protected void onApply(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        ModLogger.debug("Applied " + getEffectName() + " to " + entity.getDisplayName().getString());
    }
    
    /**
     * Called when the effect is removed from an entity.
     * Subclasses can override this for custom removal logic.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity the effect is being removed from
     * @param amplifier The amplifier level
     */
    protected void onRemove(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        ModLogger.debug("Removed " + getEffectName() + " from " + entity.getDisplayName().getString());
    }
    
    /**
     * Called each tick while the effect is active.
     * Subclasses must implement this to define the effect's behavior.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity the effect is active on
     * @param amplifier The amplifier level
     * @return True if the effect should continue, false to remove it
     */
    protected abstract boolean onTick(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier);
    
    /**
     * Determines if the effect should apply this tick.
     * Subclasses can override this for custom tick timing.
     * 
     * @param duration The remaining duration in ticks
     * @param amplifier The amplifier level
     * @return True if the effect should apply this tick
     */
    protected boolean shouldApplyThisTick(int duration, int amplifier) {
        return true; // Apply every tick by default
    }
    
    /**
     * Validates that the entity can have this effect applied.
     * Uses centralized LivingEntityChecks for consistency with codebase validation patterns.
     * Subclasses can override this for custom validation logic.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to validate
     * @return True if the entity can have this effect
     */
    protected boolean canApplyTo(LivingEntity entity) {
        return !EntityValidationHelper.isInvalid(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity), BoundaryServices.entityQuery());
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the configuration key for this effect.
     * Used for loading effect-specific configuration.
     * 
     * @return The configuration key for this effect
     */
    protected String getConfigKey() {
        return getClass().getSimpleName().toLowerCase().replace("effect", "");
    }
    
    @Override
    public boolean applyEffectTick(@Nonnull LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        // Validate entity
        if (!canApplyTo(entity)) {
            ModLogger.warn("Cannot apply " + getEffectName() + " to invalid entity");
            return false;
        }
        
        // Apply the effect
        try {
            return onTick(entity, amplifier);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("Error applying " + getEffectName() + " to " + entity.getDisplayName().getString(), e);
            return false;
        }
    }
    
    @Override
    public boolean shouldApplyEffectTickThisTick(int duration, int amplifier) {
        return shouldApplyThisTick(duration, amplifier);
    }
    
    @Override
    public void onEffectAdded(@Nonnull LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        super.onEffectAdded(entity, amplifier);
        onApply(entity, amplifier);
    }
    
    /**
     * Logs effect application with standardized format.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity the effect is being applied to
     * @param message Additional message to log
     */
    protected void logEffectApplication(LivingEntity entity, String message) {
        ModLogger.info("Applied " + getEffectName() + " to " + entity.getDisplayName().getString() + ": " + message);
    }
    
    /**
     * Logs effect removal with standardized format.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity the effect is being removed from
     * @param message Additional message to log
     */
    protected void logEffectRemoval(LivingEntity entity, String message) {
        ModLogger.info("Removed " + getEffectName() + " from " + entity.getDisplayName().getString() + ": " + message);
    }
    
    /**
     * Logs effect tick with standardized format.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity the effect is active on
     * @param message Additional message to log
     */
    protected void logEffectTick(LivingEntity entity, String message) {
        ModLogger.debug("Tick " + getEffectName() + " on " + entity.getDisplayName().getString() + ": " + message);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.effects;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.parasite.HostEffectManager;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffectCategory;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * Custom effect applied to hosts during facehugger attachment.
 * Immobilizes the host and applies visual/audio effects.
 * 
 * Extends BaseXenomorphEffect to inherit common effect behavior
 * and standardized logging. Implements DRY principle by using base class
 * functionality while providing host immobilization-specific behavior.
 * 
 * This effect is designed to be:
 * - Short duration (refreshed each tick)
 * - Configurable via JSON
 * - Simple and focused on host immobilization
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.2
 */
public class FacehuggerAttachmentEffect extends BaseXenomorphEffect {
    
    public FacehuggerAttachmentEffect() {
        super(MobEffectCategory.HARMFUL, 0x4B0082); // Dark purple color
    }
    
    @Override
    protected boolean onTick(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        // Delegate to focused HostEffectManager
        HostEffectManager.applyHostImmobilization(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity));
        
        return true; // Continue effect
    }
    
    @Override
    protected void onApply(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        super.onApply(entity, amplifier);
        logEffectApplication(entity, "Host immobilized for facehugger attachment");
    }
    
    @Override
    protected void onRemove(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        super.onRemove(entity, amplifier);
        logEffectRemoval(entity, "Host immobilization removed");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.effects;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.FacehuggerImplantationAdapter;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffectCategory;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * Custom effect applied to facehuggers during implantation.
 * Manages facehugger positioning, rotation, and state during attachment.
 *
 * Extends BaseXenomorphEffect to inherit common effect behavior
 * and standardized logging. Implements DRY principle by using base class
 * functionality while providing facehugger implantation-specific behavior.
 *
 * This effect is designed to be:
 * - Applied to the facehugger entity itself
 * - Manages positioning and rotation
 * - Prevents damage and movement during implantation
 * - Simple and focused on facehugger state
 *
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 *
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.2
 */
public class FacehuggerImplantationEffect extends BaseXenomorphEffect {

    public FacehuggerImplantationEffect() {
        super(MobEffectCategory.NEUTRAL, 0x8B4513); // Brown color
    }

    @Override
    protected boolean onTick(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        FacehuggerImplantationAdapter.applyImplantationState(entity);

        if (entity.tickCount % 100 == 0) {
            logEffectTick(entity, "Facehugger is implanting - immobile and protected");
        }

        return true;
    }

    @Override
    protected void onApply(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        super.onApply(entity, amplifier);
        logEffectApplication(entity, "Facehugger implantation started - entity immobilized");
    }

    @Override
    protected void onRemove(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        super.onRemove(entity, amplifier);
        FacehuggerImplantationAdapter.removeImplantationState(entity);
        logEffectRemoval(entity, "Facehugger implantation completed - entity mobility restored");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.effects;

import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffectCategory;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffectInstance;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.gestation.GestationManager;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.ModEffectRegistry;

/**
 * Gestation effect for xenomorph embryo development.
 * MC tick glue only — logic in {@link GestationManager} (L2).
 */
public class GestationEffect extends BaseXenomorphEffect {

    public static final GestationEffect INSTANCE = new GestationEffect();

    public GestationEffect() {
        super(MobEffectCategory.HARMFUL, 0x8B0000);
    }

    @Override
    protected boolean onTick(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        if (entity.level().isClientSide) {
            return true;
        }

        ModLogger.debug("GestationEffect",
                String.format("GestationEffect.onTick() called for %s (type: %s)",
                        entity.getDisplayName().getString(), entity.getClass().getSimpleName()));

        var gestationEffect = Objects.requireNonNull(ModEffectRegistry.gestation());
        if (!entity.hasEffect(gestationEffect)) {
            ModLogger.warn("GestationEffect",
                    String.format("Entity %s does not have gestation effect", entity.getDisplayName().getString()));
            return true;
        }

        MobEffectInstance effect = entity.getEffect(gestationEffect);
        if (effect == null) {
            ModLogger.warn("GestationEffect",
                    String.format("Effect instance is null for %s", entity.getDisplayName().getString()));
            return true;
        }

        ModLogger.debug("GestationEffect",
                String.format("Effect duration read: %d ticks for %s",
                        effect.getDuration(), entity.getDisplayName().getString()));
        return GestationManager.handleGestationTick(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity), effect.getDuration());
    }

    @Override
    protected void onApply(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        super.onApply(entity, amplifier);
        logEffectApplication(entity, "Xenomorph embryo gestation started");
    }

    @Override
    protected void onRemove(LivingEntity entity, int amplifier) {
        super.onRemove(entity, amplifier);
        logEffectRemoval(entity, "Xenomorph embryo gestation completed");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.resources;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.io.ResourceValidator;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.resources.ResourceCache;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.resources.ResourceLoader;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;

/**
 * Orchestrator for resource management.
 * Coordinates loading, caching, and validation of resources.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FLUX
 * 
 * REFACTORED: This class now follows SRP by delegating to:
 * - ResourceLoader: Resource loading logic
 * - ResourceCache: Caching logic
 * - ResourceValidator: Validation logic
 * 
 * This class orchestrates resource operations and maintains the public API.
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class ResourceManager {
    
    /**
     * Gets the texture resource location for a given xenomorph type and version.
     * Includes validation, caching, and detailed logging.
     * 
     * @param type The xenomorph type (must not be null)
     * @param version The version number (must be positive)
     * @return The texture resource location
     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if parameters are invalid
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getEntityTexture(XenomorphType type, int version) {
        // Validate input parameters
        ResourceValidator.validateResourceParameters(type, version);
        
        // Create cache key
        String cacheKey = "texture_" + type.name() + "_v" + version;
        
        // Check cache first
        if (ResourceCache.isResourceCached(cacheKey)) {
            ModLogger.debug("ResourceManager", "Using cached texture: " + type + " v" + version);
            return ResourceCache.getCachedResource(cacheKey);
        }
        
        // Start performance timing
        ModLogger.startTimer("TextureLoad_" + type.name() + "_v" + version);
        
        try {
            // Load the resource
            ResourceLocation resourceLocation = ResourceLoader.loadEntityTexture(type, version);
            
            // Cache the resource
            ResourceCache.cacheResource(cacheKey, resourceLocation);
            
            ModLogger.success("ResourceManager", "Generated texture resource: " + resourceLocation);
            return resourceLocation;
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("ResourceManager", "Failed to get entity texture for " + type + " v" + version + ": " + e.getMessage(), e);
            throw new RuntimeException("Failed to get entity texture", e);
        } finally {
            ModLogger.endTimer("TextureLoad_" + type.name() + "_v" + version);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the texture resource location for a given xenomorph type (defaults to v1).
     * 
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @return The texture resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getEntityTexture(XenomorphType type) {
        return getEntityTexture(type, 1);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the model resource location for a given xenomorph type and version.
     * 
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The model resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getEntityModel(XenomorphType type, int version) {
        return ResourceLoader.loadEntityModel(type, version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the model resource location for a given xenomorph type (defaults to v1).
     * 
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @return The model resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getEntityModel(XenomorphType type) {
        return getEntityModel(type, 1);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the sound resource location for a given xenomorph type, sound type, and version.
     * 
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @param soundType The type of sound (ambient, hurt, death, etc.)
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The sound resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getEntitySound(XenomorphType type, String soundType, int version) {
        return ResourceLoader.loadEntitySound(type, soundType, version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets the sound resource location for a given xenomorph type and sound type (defaults to v1).
     * 
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @param soundType The type of sound
     * @return The sound resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getEntitySound(XenomorphType type, String soundType) {
        return getEntitySound(type, soundType, 1);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a mob-based texture resource location.
     * 
     * @param category The mob category (aggressive, neutral, passive)
     * @param hostType The host type
     * @param mobName The mob name
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The texture resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getMobTexture(String category, String hostType, String mobName, int version) {
        return ResourceLoader.loadMobTexture(category, hostType, mobName, version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a mob-based texture resource location (defaults to v1).
     * 
     * @param category The mob category
     * @param hostType The host type
     * @param mobName The mob name
     * @return The texture resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getMobTexture(String category, String hostType, String mobName) {
        return getMobTexture(category, hostType, mobName, 1);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a mob-based model resource location.
     * 
     * @param category The mob category
     * @param hostType The host type
     * @param mobName The mob name
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The model resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getMobModel(String category, String hostType, String mobName, int version) {
        return ResourceLoader.loadMobModel(category, hostType, mobName, version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a mob-based model resource location (defaults to v1).
     * 
     * @param category The mob category
     * @param hostType The host type
     * @param mobName The mob name
     * @return The model resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getMobModel(String category, String hostType, String mobName) {
        return getMobModel(category, hostType, mobName, 1);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a mob-based sound resource location.
     * 
     * @param category The mob category
     * @param hostType The host type
     * @param mobName The mob name
     * @param soundType The type of sound
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The sound resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getMobSound(String category, String hostType, String mobName, String soundType, int version) {
        return ResourceLoader.loadMobSound(category, hostType, mobName, soundType, version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a mob-based sound resource location (defaults to v1).
     * 
     * @param category The mob category
     * @param hostType The host type
     * @param mobName The mob name
     * @param soundType The type of sound
     * @return The sound resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getMobSound(String category, String hostType, String mobName, String soundType) {
        return getMobSound(category, hostType, mobName, soundType, 1);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a special sound resource location for xenomorph abilities.
     * 
     * @param soundName The sound name
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The sound resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getSpecialSound(String soundName, int version) {
        return ResourceLoader.loadSpecialSound(soundName, version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a special sound resource location (defaults to v1).
     * 
     * @param soundName The sound name
     * @return The sound resource location
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getSpecialSound(String soundName) {
        return getSpecialSound(soundName, 1);
    }
    
    /**
     * Generic method to get all resources for all xenomorph types.
     * Reduces code duplication in collection methods.
     * 
     * @param loader Function that loads a resource for a given xenomorph type and version
     * @param version The version number
     * @return Map of xenomorph types to resource locations
     */
    private static Map<XenomorphType, ResourceLocation> getAllResources(
            java.util.function.BiFunction<XenomorphType, Integer, ResourceLocation> loader, 
            int version) {
        Map<XenomorphType, ResourceLocation> resources = new HashMap<>();
        for (XenomorphType type : XenomorphType.values()) {
            resources.put(type, loader.apply(type, version));
        }
        return resources;
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets all texture resource locations for all xenomorph types.
     * 
     * @param version The version number
     * @return Map of xenomorph types to texture resource locations
     */
    public static Map<XenomorphType, ResourceLocation> getAllTextures(int version) {
        return getAllResources((type, versionValue) -> getEntityTexture(type, versionValue), version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets all texture resource locations for all xenomorph types (defaults to v1).
     * 
     * @return Map of xenomorph types to texture resource locations
     */
    public static Map<XenomorphType, ResourceLocation> getAllTextures() {
        return getAllTextures(1);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets all model resource locations for all xenomorph types.
     * 
     * @param version The version number
     * @return Map of xenomorph types to model resource locations
     */
    public static Map<XenomorphType, ResourceLocation> getAllModels(int version) {
        return getAllResources((type, versionValue) -> getEntityModel(type, versionValue), version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets all model resource locations for all xenomorph types (defaults to v1).
     * 
     * @return Map of xenomorph types to model resource locations
     */
    public static Map<XenomorphType, ResourceLocation> getAllModels() {
        return getAllModels(1);
    }
    
    /**
     * Validates that a resource path is valid and follows the expected structure.
     * Enhanced with detailed logging and error reporting.
     * 
     * @param path The resource path to validate
     * @return True if the path is valid
     */
    public static boolean validateResourcePath(String path) {
        return ResourceValidator.validateResourcePath(path);
    }
    
    /**
     * Builds a resource path from configuration data.
     * 
     * @param basePath The base path from configuration
     * @param version The version number
     * @return The complete resource path
     */
    public static String buildConfigurablePath(String basePath, int version) {
        return ResourceLoader.loadConfigurablePath(basePath, version);
    }
    
    /**
     * Clears the resource cache.
     */
    public static void clearCache() {
        ResourceCache.clearCache();
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets cache statistics.
     * 
     * @return A summary of cache statistics
     */
    public static String getCacheStats() {
        return ResourceCache.getCacheStats();
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets a resource with fallback handling.
     * 
     * @param primaryPath The primary resource path
     * @param fallbackPath The fallback resource path
     * @return The resource location, or null if neither is valid
     */
    public static ResourceLocation getResourceWithFallback(String primaryPath, String fallbackPath) {
        return ResourceLoader.loadResourceWithFallback(primaryPath, fallbackPath);
    }
}

PACKAGE: level_1/species/common

FILE: BaseDataDrivenRenderer.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.common;

import com.mojang.blaze3d.vertex.PoseStack;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.entity.EntityType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.renderer.EntityTypeResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.renderer.ModelRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.renderer.RenderConfigProvider;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.renderer.TextureRegistry;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.client.model.EntityModel;
import net.minecraft.client.renderer.entity.EntityRendererProvider;
import net.minecraft.client.renderer.entity.MobRenderer;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Base class for data-driven renderers that use modular components.
 * Generic implementation that works with any EntityType, not species-specific.
 * 
 * Follows Single Responsibility Principle - only handles rendering coordination.
 * Uses dependency injection for model creation, texture resolution, and configuration.
 * 
 * Species-specific renderers should extend this class and provide:
 * - EntityTypeResolver for resolving entity types from entities
 * - ModelRegistry for model creation
 * - TextureRegistry for texture resolution
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: NEW
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8
 */
public abstract class BaseDataDrivenRenderer<T extends Mob> extends MobRenderer<T, EntityModel<T>> {
    
    protected final ResourceLocation texture;
    protected final ModelRegistry modelRegistry;
    protected final TextureRegistry textureRegistry;
    protected final EntityTypeResolver entityTypeResolver;
    protected final EntityType entityType;
    protected final RenderConfigProvider configProvider;
    
    /**
     * Constructor with dependency injection for testing and extensibility.
     * Follows Dependency Inversion Principle.
     * 
     * @param context The renderer context
     * @param entityType The entity type for this renderer
     * @param modelRegistry The model registry for creating models
     * @param textureRegistry The texture registry for resolving textures
     * @param entityTypeResolver The resolver for determining entity types from entities
     * @param configProvider The config provider for species-specific config access
     */
    protected BaseDataDrivenRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context,
                                    EntityType entityType,
                                    ModelRegistry modelRegistry,
                                    TextureRegistry textureRegistry,
                                    EntityTypeResolver entityTypeResolver,
                                    RenderConfigProvider configProvider) {
        super(context, createModelFromConfig(context, entityType, modelRegistry, configProvider), 
              configProvider.getShadowSize(entityType));
        
        this.entityType = entityType;
        this.modelRegistry = modelRegistry;
        this.textureRegistry = textureRegistry;
        this.entityTypeResolver = entityTypeResolver;
        this.configProvider = configProvider;
        this.texture = textureRegistry.resolveTexture(entityType);
    }
    
    /**
     * Creates the appropriate model using the injected ModelRegistry.
     * Delegates model creation to the registry, following Single Responsibility Principle.
     */
    private static <T extends Mob> EntityModel<T> createModelFromConfig(EntityRendererProvider.Context context,
                                                                        EntityType entityType,
                                                                        ModelRegistry modelRegistry,
                                                                        RenderConfigProvider configProvider) {
        try {
            // Get model name from config using provider
            String modelName = configProvider.getModelName(entityType);
            if (modelName == null || modelName.isEmpty()) {
                modelName = "player";
            }
            
            return modelRegistry.createModel(context, modelName, entityType);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            // Fallback to player model
            return modelRegistry.createModel(context, "player", entityType);
        }
    }
    
    @Override
    public @Nonnull ResourceLocation getTextureLocation(@Nonnull T entity) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(texture);
    }
    
    @Override
    public void render(@Nonnull T entity, float entityYaw, float partialTick, @Nonnull PoseStack poseStack,
                      @Nonnull net.minecraft.client.renderer.MultiBufferSource bufferSource, int packedLight) {
        // Rate limit rendering debug logs to every 100 ticks (5 seconds) to reduce spam
        if (entity.tickCount % 100 == 0) {
            com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger.debug("BaseDataDrivenRenderer",
                String.format("🎨 Rendering %s at %s", entity.getType().toString(), entity.blockPosition()));
        }
        super.render(entity, entityYaw, partialTick, poseStack, bufferSource, packedLight);
    }
    
    /**
     * Applies scaling to the entity model based on configuration.
     * Uses the config provider for species-specific scaling logic.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity
     * @param poseStack The pose stack
     * @param partialTick The partial tick
     */
    @Override
    protected void scale(@Nonnull T entity, @Nonnull PoseStack poseStack, float partialTick) {
        EntityType resolvedType = entityTypeResolver != null ? entityTypeResolver.resolveEntityType(entity) : null;
        if (resolvedType != null && configProvider != null) {
            float scale = configProvider.getScale(resolvedType);
            if (scale != 1.0f) {
                poseStack.scale(scale, scale, scale);
            }
        }
    }
}

FILE: EntityDetectionHelper.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.ai.core;

import java.util.Objects;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init.EntityInitRefs;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.AABB;

/**
 * Helper class for detecting entities in the world.
 * Centralizes entity detection logic to make behavior files more focused.
 * 
 * DRY: Eliminates duplicate entity detection patterns across AI files.
 * SOLID: Makes behavior files more focused by extracting detection logic.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class EntityDetectionHelper {
    
    /**
     * Checks if there's an ovomorph entity at the specified position.
     * 
     * @param level The server level
     * @param pos The position to check
     * @return true if an ovomorph is found at the position
     */
    public static boolean hasOvomorphAt(ServerLevel level, BlockPos pos) {
        if (level == null || pos == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        return level.getEntitiesOfClass(LivingEntity.class, 
            Objects.requireNonNull(AABB.ofSize(
                Objects.requireNonNull(net.minecraft.world.phys.Vec3.atCenterOf(pos)), 0.5, 0.5, 0.5)))
            .stream()
            .anyMatch(entity -> entity.getType() == EntityInitRefs.holder("OVOMORPH").get());
    }
    
    /**
     * Checks if there's an ovomorph nearby within the specified distance.
     * 
     * @param level The server level
     * @param pos The center position
     * @param distance The search distance in blocks
     * @return true if an ovomorph is found nearby
     */
    public static boolean hasOvomorphNearby(ServerLevel level, BlockPos pos, int distance) {
        if (level == null || pos == null || distance < 0) {
            return false;
        }
        
        for (int x = -distance; x <= distance; x++) {
            for (int z = -distance; z <= distance; z++) {
                for (int y = -2; y <= 2; y++) {
                    if (x == 0 && z == 0 && y == 0) continue; // Skip center position
                    
                    BlockPos checkPos = pos.offset(x, y, z);
                    if (hasOvomorphAt(level, checkPos)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
    
    /**
     * Counts ovomorph entities in a specified area.
     * 
     * @param level The server level
     * @param centerPos The center position
     * @param searchRadius The search radius in blocks
     * @param yRange The vertical search range (from -yRange to +yRange)
     * @return The count of ovomorphs found in the area
     */
    public static int countOvomorphsInArea(ServerLevel level, BlockPos centerPos, int searchRadius, int yRange) {
        if (level == null || centerPos == null || searchRadius < 0 || yRange < 0) {
            return 0;
        }
        
        int count = 0;
        for (int x = -searchRadius; x <= searchRadius; x++) {
            for (int z = -searchRadius; z <= searchRadius; z++) {
                for (int y = -yRange; y <= yRange; y++) {
                    BlockPos checkPos = centerPos.offset(x, y, z);
                    if (hasOvomorphAt(level, checkPos)) {
                        count++;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return count;
    }
    
    // Private constructor to prevent instantiation
    private EntityDetectionHelper() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("EntityDetectionHelper is a utility class and cannot be instantiated");
    }
}

FILE: PrioritizedHostTargetGoal.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.ai.shared;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.ai.XenomorphTargetingHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.target.NearestAttackableTargetGoal;

/**
 * Thin combat target goal; priority scoring lives in {@link XenomorphTargetingHelper}.
 */
public final class PrioritizedHostTargetGoal extends NearestAttackableTargetGoal<LivingEntity> {

    public PrioritizedHostTargetGoal(PathfinderMob mob) {
        super(mob, LivingEntity.class, true,
                living -> XenomorphTargetingHelper.isValidTargetEntity(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(living)));
    }

    @Override
    protected void findTarget() {
        List<XenomorphTargetingHelper.ScoredTarget> candidates = new ArrayList<>();
        Map<LivingEntityRef, LivingEntity> refToEntity = new HashMap<>();

        for (LivingEntity candidate : mob.level().getEntitiesOfClass(
                LivingEntity.class,
                Objects.requireNonNull(getTargetSearchArea(getFollowDistance())),
                living -> XenomorphTargetingHelper.isValidTargetEntity(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(living)))) {
            if (!mob.getSensing().hasLineOfSight(Objects.requireNonNull(candidate))) {
                continue;
            }
            LivingEntityRef ref = BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(candidate);
            XenomorphTargetingHelper.addScoredCandidate(candidates, ref, mob.distanceToSqr(Objects.requireNonNull(candidate)));
            refToEntity.put(ref, candidate);
        }

        LivingEntityRef bestRef = XenomorphTargetingHelper.selectBestTarget(candidates);
        this.target = bestRef != null ? refToEntity.get(bestRef) : null;
    }
}

FILE: StandardTargetingHelper.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.ai.shared;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.ai.XenomorphTargetingHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.CommonGoalRegistrar;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.target.NearestAttackableTargetGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.animal.Animal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.animal.IronGolem;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.animal.SnowGolem;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.npc.AbstractVillager;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;

/**
 * Helper class for registering standard targeting goals across form packages.
 * Centralizes duplicate targeting logic from DroneAI and QueenAI to eliminate DRY violations.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 *
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.7
 */
public class StandardTargetingHelper {

    /**
     * Registers standard targeting goals for xenomorph entities.
     * Registers: HurtByTargetGoal, Player, Villager, Animal, Golem, SnowGolem, LivingEntity.
     * DRY: Extracted from DroneAI and QueenAI to eliminate duplicate targeting code.
     *
     * @param entity The entity to register targeting goals for
     * @param type   xenomorph type whose {@code goal_priorities} map supplies slot ordering
     */
    public static void registerStandardTargetingGoals(PathfinderMob entity, XenomorphType type) {
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerHurtByTargetGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(type, "hurt_by_target"));

        entity.targetSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(type, "target_player"),
                new NearestAttackableTargetGoal<>(entity, Player.class, true,
                        living -> XenomorphTargetingHelper.isValidTargetEntity(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(living))));
        entity.targetSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(type, "target_villager"),
                new NearestAttackableTargetGoal<>(entity, AbstractVillager.class, true,
                        living -> XenomorphTargetingHelper.isValidTargetEntity(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(living))));
        entity.targetSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(type, "target_animal"),
                new NearestAttackableTargetGoal<>(entity, Animal.class, true,
                        living -> XenomorphTargetingHelper.isValidTargetEntity(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(living))));

        entity.targetSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(type, "target_iron_golem"),
                new NearestAttackableTargetGoal<>(entity, IronGolem.class, true));
        entity.targetSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(type, "target_snow_golem"),
                new NearestAttackableTargetGoal<>(entity, SnowGolem.class, true));

        entity.targetSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(type, "prioritized_host"),
                new PrioritizedHostTargetGoal(entity));
    }

    // Private constructor to prevent instantiation
    private StandardTargetingHelper() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("StandardTargetingHelper is a utility class and cannot be instantiated");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.api;

/**
 * API interface for entity growth lifecycle operations.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 */
public interface EntityGrowthAPI {

        return BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity);
    }

        return EntityGrowthSystem.processGrowth(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(entity)));

        return EntityGrowthSystem.canTransform(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(entity)));

        return EntityGrowthSystem.getGrowthProgress(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(entity)));
    }

        return MaturationSystem.getMaturationUrgency(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(entity)));
    }

        return MaturationSystem.shouldPrioritizeFoodHunting(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(entity)));
    }

        return MaturationSystem.getFoodTimerReduction(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(entity)));
    }

    static int getMaturationTimer(LivingEntity entity) {
        return MaturationSystem.getMaturationTimer(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(entity)));
    }

    static void reduceMaturationTimer(LivingEntity entity, int reduction) {
        MaturationSystem.reduceMaturationTimer(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(entity)), reduction);
    }
}

FILE: ParasiteLifecycleAPI.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.api;

import java.util.Objects;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.parasite.FacehuggerAttachmentEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_3.parasite.ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * API interface for parasite lifecycle operations.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 */
public interface ParasiteLifecycleAPI {

    static LivingEntityRef toRef(LivingEntity entity) {
        return BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity);
    }

    static boolean processParasiteLifecycle(LivingEntity facehugger, LivingEntity host) {
        return ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.processAttachment(
                Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(facehugger)), Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(host)));
    }

    static boolean processParasiteLifecycleTick(LivingEntity facehugger, LivingEntity host, int attachmentTicks) {
        LivingEntityRef hostRef = Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(host));
        if (facehugger instanceof FacehuggerAttachmentEntity attachment && attachment.getAttachmentTarget() != null) {
            return ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.processAttachmentTick(
                    Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(facehugger)), hostRef, attachmentTicks);
        }
        if (!ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.isHostInfected(hostRef)) {
            return false;
        }
        int timeRemaining = ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.getRemainingGestationTime(hostRef);
        return ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.processGestationTick(hostRef, timeRemaining);
    }

    static void processHostGestation(LivingEntity host) {
        ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.processGestation(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(host)));
    }

    static boolean isHostInfected(LivingEntity host) {
        return ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.isHostInfected(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(host)));
    }

    static ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.InfectionStage getInfectionStage(LivingEntity host) {
        return ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.getInfectionStage(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(host)));
    }

    static int getRemainingGestationTime(LivingEntity host) {
        return ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.getRemainingGestationTime(Objects.requireNonNull(toRef(host)));
    }

    static int getAttachmentDuration() {
        return ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.getAttachmentDuration();
    }

    static double getAttachmentDistance() {
        return ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.getAttachmentDistance();
    }
}

FILE: CrawlingFormAnimationSetup.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.client;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.animation.AnimationSpeedHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.model.AnimationCaller;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.model.XenomorphModelAnimationSetup;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.client.animation.AnimationDefinition;
import net.minecraft.client.model.HierarchicalModel;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.AnimationState;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * Shared render-time animation priority for crawling xenomorph forms (drone, queen).
 */
public final class CrawlingFormAnimationSetup {

    public record AnimationStates(
            AnimationState standingToCrawling,
            AnimationState crawlingToStanding,
            AnimationState moving,
            AnimationState idle) {
    }

    public record AnimationDefinitions(
            AnimationDefinition standingToCrawling,
            AnimationDefinition crawlingToStanding,
            AnimationDefinition crawlPose,
            AnimationDefinition idleStanding) {
    }

    private CrawlingFormAnimationSetup() {
    }

    public static <T extends LivingEntity> void apply(
            XenomorphModelAnimationSetup setup,
            T entity,
            HierarchicalModel<T> model,
            AnimationCaller animator,
            float ageInTicks,
            XenomorphType type,
            float transitionLengthSeconds,
            AnimationStates states,
            AnimationDefinitions definitions) {
        Objects.requireNonNull(setup).resetPose(Objects.requireNonNull(model));

        if (states.standingToCrawling().isStarted()) {
            float speedMultiplier = AnimationSpeedHelper.calculateTransitionSpeedMultiplier(
                    type, transitionLengthSeconds);
            animator.animate(states.standingToCrawling(), definitions.standingToCrawling(),
                    ageInTicks * speedMultiplier);
        } else if (states.crawlingToStanding().isStarted()) {
            float speedMultiplier = AnimationSpeedHelper.calculateTransitionSpeedMultiplier(
                    type, transitionLengthSeconds);
            animator.animate(states.crawlingToStanding(), definitions.crawlingToStanding(),
                    ageInTicks * speedMultiplier);
        } else if (states.moving().isStarted()) {
            animator.animate(states.moving(), definitions.crawlPose(), ageInTicks);
        } else if (states.idle().isStarted()) {
            animator.animate(states.idle(), definitions.idleStanding(), ageInTicks);
        }
    }
}

FILE: XenomorphModelRegistry.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.client;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.entity.EntityType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.ModelLayerRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.renderer.ModelRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.model.XenomorphModelRefs;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.client.model.EntityModel;
import net.minecraft.client.model.HumanoidModel;
import net.minecraft.client.model.SilverfishModel;
import net.minecraft.client.model.SlimeModel;
import net.minecraft.client.model.SpiderModel;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.ModelLayers;
import net.minecraft.client.renderer.entity.EntityRendererProvider;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Xenomorph-specific model registry implementation.
 * Handles model creation for xenomorph entities.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: NEW
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8
 */
public class XenomorphModelRegistry implements ModelRegistry {
    
    @Override
    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    public <T extends Mob> EntityModel<T> createModel(EntityRendererProvider.Context context, 
                                                       String modelName, 
                                                       EntityType entityType) {
        String normalizedName = modelName.toLowerCase();
        
        ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", 
            String.format("🔧 Creating model: '%s' for %s", normalizedName, entityType.getConfigKey()));
        
        return (EntityModel<T>) switch (normalizedName) {
            // Vanilla models
            case "spider" -> new SpiderModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.SPIDER))));
            case "cave_spider" -> new SpiderModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.CAVE_SPIDER))));
            case "silverfish" -> new SilverfishModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.SILVERFISH))));
            case "endermite" -> new SpiderModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.ENDERMITE))));
            case "player" -> new HumanoidModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.PLAYER))));
            case "iron_golem" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🔧 Creating iron golem model using scaled humanoid model");
                yield new HumanoidModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.PLAYER))));
            }
            case "enderdragon_egg" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🥚 Creating ender dragon egg model using slime model (egg-shaped)");
                yield new SlimeModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.SLIME))));
            }
            
            // Custom xenomorph models
            case "ovomorph_custom" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating custom ovomorph model");
                yield XenomorphModelRefs.create(XenomorphModelRefs.Kind.OVOMORPH, Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.OVOMORPH_CUSTOM))));
            }
            case "drone_custom" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating custom drone model");
                yield XenomorphModelRefs.create(XenomorphModelRefs.Kind.DRONE, Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.DRONE_CUSTOM))));
            }
            case "queen_custom" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating custom queen model");
                yield XenomorphModelRefs.create(XenomorphModelRefs.Kind.QUEEN, Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.QUEEN_CUSTOM))));
            }
            
            // V2 model paths
            case "weylandyutani:models/entity/drone_v2" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating v2 drone model");
                yield XenomorphModelRefs.create(XenomorphModelRefs.Kind.DRONE, Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.DRONE_CUSTOM))));
            }
            case "weylandyutani:models/entity/ovomorph_v2" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating v2 ovomorph model");
                yield XenomorphModelRefs.create(XenomorphModelRefs.Kind.OVOMORPH, Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.OVOMORPH_CUSTOM))));
            }
            case "weylandyutani:models/entity/queen_v2" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating v2 queen model");
                yield XenomorphModelRefs.create(XenomorphModelRefs.Kind.QUEEN, Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.QUEEN_CUSTOM))));
            }
            
            // Custom xenomorph models
            case "facehugger_custom" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating custom facehugger model");
                yield XenomorphModelRefs.create(XenomorphModelRefs.Kind.FACEHUGGER, Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.FACEHUGGER_CUSTOM))));
            }
            case "chestburster_custom" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating custom chestburster model");
                yield XenomorphModelRefs.create(XenomorphModelRefs.Kind.CHESTBURSTER, Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.CHESTBURSTER_CUSTOM))));
            }
            case "growth_custom" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating custom growth model");
                yield new HumanoidModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.PLAYER)))); // Fallback
            }
            case "praetor_custom" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating custom praetor model");
                yield new HumanoidModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.PLAYER)))); // Fallback
            }
            case "human_custom" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating custom human model");
                yield new HumanoidModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.PLAYER)))); // Fallback
            }
            
            // V2 model paths
            case "weylandyutani:models/entity/chestburster_v2" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating v2 chestburster model");
                yield XenomorphModelRefs.create(XenomorphModelRefs.Kind.CHESTBURSTER, Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.CHESTBURSTER_CUSTOM))));
            }
            case "weylandyutani:models/entity/facehugger_v2" -> {
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelRegistry", "🎨 Creating v2 facehugger model");
                yield XenomorphModelRefs.create(XenomorphModelRefs.Kind.FACEHUGGER, Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.FACEHUGGER_CUSTOM))));
            }
            
            default -> {
                ModLogger.warn("XenomorphModelRegistry", 
                    String.format("⚠️ Unknown model '%s', using player model fallback", normalizedName));
                yield new HumanoidModel<>(Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.PLAYER))));
            }
        };
    }
}

FILE: XenomorphRenderConfigProvider.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.client;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.entity.EntityType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.renderer.RenderConfigProvider;

/**
 * Xenomorph-specific render configuration adapter.
 * Resolves model name, shadow size, and scale from entity JSON config.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: NEW
 */
public class XenomorphRenderConfigProvider implements RenderConfigProvider {

    @Override
    public String getModelName(EntityType entityType) {
        if (!(entityType instanceof XenomorphType xenomorphType)) {
            return "player";
        }

        try {
            EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);
            String modelName = (config != null && config.model != null) ? config.model : "player";

            ModLogger.info("XenomorphRenderConfigProvider",
                    String.format("Loading model for %s: '%s' (config: %s)",
                            entityType.getConfigKey(), modelName, config != null ? "loaded" : "null"));

            return modelName;
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.warn("XenomorphRenderConfigProvider",
                    String.format("Failed to get model name for %s: %s, using fallback",
                            entityType.getConfigKey(), e.getMessage()));
            return "player";
        }
    }

    @Override
    public float getShadowSize(EntityType entityType) {
        if (!(entityType instanceof XenomorphType xenomorphType)) {
            return 0.5f;
        }
        return EntityConfigStorage.getShadowSize(xenomorphType);
    }

    @Override
    public float getScale(EntityType entityType) {
        if (!(entityType instanceof XenomorphType xenomorphType)) {
            return 1.0f;
        }

        try {
            EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);
            if (config != null && config.entitySize != null) {
                return config.entitySize.scale;
            }
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.warn("XenomorphRenderConfigProvider",
                    String.format("Failed to get scale for %s: %s", entityType.getConfigKey(), e.getMessage()));
        }

        return 1.0f;
    }
}

FILE: XenomorphRendererRegistry.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.client;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init.EntityInitRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.renderer.RendererRegistry;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.client.renderer.entity.EntityRenderer;
import net.minecraft.client.renderer.entity.EntityRendererProvider;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.client.event.EntityRenderersEvent;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredHolder;

/**
 * Xenomorph-specific renderer registry.
 *
 * <p>NDE escape hatch: {@link #registerOne} loads
 * {@code com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.client.renderer.XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer$*}
 * via {@code Class.forName} so this registry stays at {@code level_4} without compile-time L3 imports.
 */
public class XenomorphRendererRegistry implements RendererRegistry {

    private static String rendererFqn(String rendererClass) {
        return "com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.client.renderer.XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer$"
                + rendererClass;
    }

    @Override
    public void registerRenderers(EntityRenderersEvent.RegisterRenderers event) {
        ModLogger.info("XenomorphRendererRegistry", "Loading xenomorph renderers...");

        int registeredCount = 0;
        int[] failedCount = {0};

        registeredCount += registerAndTrack(event, "FACEHUGGER", "FacehuggerRenderer", failedCount);
        registeredCount += registerAndTrack(event, "CHESTBURSTER", "ChestbursterRenderer", failedCount);
        registeredCount += registerAndTrack(event, "DRONE", "DroneRenderer", failedCount);
        registeredCount += registerAndTrack(event, "GROWTH", "GrowthRenderer", failedCount);
        registeredCount += registerAndTrack(event, "PRAETOR", "PraetorRenderer", failedCount);
        registeredCount += registerAndTrack(event, "QUEEN", "QueenRenderer", failedCount);
        registeredCount += registerAndTrack(event, "OVOMORPH", "OvomorphRenderer", failedCount);

        if (failedCount[0] > 0) {
            ModLogger.warn("XenomorphRendererRegistry",
                    String.format("Xenomorph renderer registration completed with %d successful and %d failed registrations",
                            registeredCount, failedCount[0]));
        } else {
            ModLogger.info("XenomorphRendererRegistry",
                    String.format("All xenomorph renderers loaded successfully (%d renderers)", registeredCount));
        }
    }

    private int registerAndTrack(
            EntityRenderersEvent.RegisterRenderers event,
            String entityKey,
            String rendererClass,
            int[] failedCount) {
        int result = registerOne(event, EntityInitRefs.holder(entityKey), rendererClass);
        if (result == 0) {
            failedCount[0]++;
        }
        return result;
    }

    private int registerOne(
            EntityRenderersEvent.RegisterRenderers event,
            DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<?>> holder,
            String rendererClass) {
        try {
            EntityType<?> entityType = holder.get();
            var ctor = Class.forName(rendererFqn(rendererClass))
                    .getConstructor(EntityRendererProvider.Context.class);
            @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
            var castedEntityType = (EntityType<Entity>) entityType;
            event.registerEntityRenderer(Objects.requireNonNull(castedEntityType), context -> {
                try {
                    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
                    EntityRenderer<Entity> renderer = (EntityRenderer<Entity>) ctor.newInstance(context);
                    return renderer;
                } catch (ReflectiveOperationException e) {
                    throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to construct " + rendererClass, e);
                }
            });
            ModLogger.debug("XenomorphRendererRegistry", "Registered " + rendererClass);
            return 1;
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("XenomorphRendererRegistry", "Failed to register " + rendererClass + ": " + e.getMessage());
            return 0;
        }
    }

    @Override
    public String getSpeciesName() {
        return "xenomorph";
    }
}

FILE: XenomorphTextureRegistry.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.client;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.entity.EntityType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.renderer.TextureRegistry;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;

/**
 * Xenomorph-specific texture registry implementation.
 * Handles texture resolution for xenomorph entities.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: NEW
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8
 */
public class XenomorphTextureRegistry implements TextureRegistry {
    
    private static final ResourceLocation DEFAULT_FALLBACK = ResourceLocation.parse("minecraft:textures/entity/cat/cat.png");
    
    @Override
    public ResourceLocation resolveTexture(EntityType entityType) {
        // Cast to XenomorphType for config access
        if (!(entityType instanceof XenomorphType xenomorphType)) {
            ModLogger.warn("XenomorphTextureRegistry", 
                String.format("⚠️ EntityType %s is not a XenomorphType, using default texture", entityType.getConfigKey()));
            return DEFAULT_FALLBACK;
        }
        
        try {
            EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);
            
            if (config == null) {
                ModLogger.warn("XenomorphTextureRegistry", 
                    String.format("⚠️ No config found for %s, using default texture", entityType.getConfigKey()));
                return DEFAULT_FALLBACK;
            }
            
            // Prioritize primary texture for proper rendering
            if (config.texture != null && !config.texture.isEmpty()) {
                ResourceLocation primaryTexture = ResourceLocation.parse(Objects.requireNonNull(config.texture));
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphTextureRegistry", 
                    String.format("🎨 Using primary texture for %s: %s", entityType.getConfigKey(), config.texture));
                
                // DEBUG: Check if texture resource exists
                if (xenomorphType == XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER) {
                    ModLogger.info("XenomorphTextureRegistry", 
                        String.format("🦾 DEBUG: Facehugger texture path: %s", config.texture));
                    ModLogger.info("XenomorphTextureRegistry", 
                        String.format("🦾 DEBUG: Parsed ResourceLocation: %s", primaryTexture));
                }
                
                return primaryTexture;
            }
            
            // Fall back to fallback texture if primary is not available
            if (config.textureFallback != null && !config.textureFallback.isEmpty()) {
                ResourceLocation fallbackTexture = ResourceLocation.parse(Objects.requireNonNull(config.textureFallback));
                ModLogger.info("XenomorphTextureRegistry", 
                    String.format("🎨 Using fallback texture for %s: %s", entityType.getConfigKey(), config.textureFallback));
                return fallbackTexture;
            }
            
            ModLogger.warn("XenomorphTextureRegistry", 
                String.format("⚠️ No texture config for %s, using default", entityType.getConfigKey()));
            return DEFAULT_FALLBACK;
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.warn("XenomorphTextureRegistry", 
                String.format("⚠️ Failed to resolve texture for %s: %s", entityType.getConfigKey(), e.getMessage()));
            return DEFAULT_FALLBACK;
        }
    }
}

FILE: AIContextDetector.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.client.animation;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.ai.AIContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.ai.AIContextPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIContextThresholdsConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AnimationTransitionConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.growth.XenomorphTypeHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Thin adapter: reads Minecraft entity state and delegates to {@link AIContextPolicy}.
 */
public class AIContextDetector {

    @Deprecated
    public enum LegacyAIContext {
        NORMAL,
        STALKING,
        CHASING,
        FIGHTING;

        public AIContext toDomain() {
            return AIContext.valueOf(name());
        }
    }

    public static class TransitionSpeedModifiers {
        public float normalModifier;
        public float stalkingModifier;
        public float chasingModifier;
        public float fightingModifier;

        public TransitionSpeedModifiers() {
        }

        public static TransitionSpeedModifiers fromConfig(EntityConfig config) {
            AIContextPolicy.TransitionSpeedModifiers domain = AnimationTransitionConfigHelper.resolve(config);
            TransitionSpeedModifiers modifiers = new TransitionSpeedModifiers();
            modifiers.normalModifier = domain.normalModifier();
            modifiers.stalkingModifier = domain.stalkingModifier();
            modifiers.chasingModifier = domain.chasingModifier();
            modifiers.fightingModifier = domain.fightingModifier();
            return modifiers;
        }

        AIContextPolicy.TransitionSpeedModifiers toDomain() {
            return new AIContextPolicy.TransitionSpeedModifiers(
                    normalModifier, stalkingModifier, chasingModifier, fightingModifier);
        }
    }

    public static AIContext detectContext(LivingEntity entity) {
        if (!(entity instanceof Mob mob)) {
            return AIContext.NORMAL;
        }

        var target = mob.getTarget();
        if (target == null) {
            return AIContextPolicy.classify(new AIContextPolicy.ContextInputs(
                    false,
                    false,
                    mob.isCrouching(),
                    Double.MAX_VALUE,
                    mob.getLastHurtByMob() != null,
                    mob.getNavigation().isInProgress(),
                    null
            ), AIContextThresholdsConfigHelper.resolve(
                    XenomorphTypeHelper.getXenomorphType(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity))));
        }

        boolean targetAlive = target.isAlive();
        double distanceToTargetSq = mob.distanceToSqr(target);

        Double distanceToPathTargetSq = null;
        if (mob.getNavigation().isInProgress()) {
            var pathTarget = mob.getNavigation().getTargetPos();
            if (pathTarget != null) {
                distanceToPathTargetSq = mob.distanceToSqr(
                        pathTarget.getX(), pathTarget.getY(), pathTarget.getZ());
            }
        }

        AIContextPolicy.ContextThresholds thresholds = AIContextThresholdsConfigHelper.resolve(
                XenomorphTypeHelper.getXenomorphType(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity)));

        return AIContextPolicy.classify(new AIContextPolicy.ContextInputs(
                true,
                targetAlive,
                mob.isCrouching(),
                distanceToTargetSq,
                mob.getLastHurtByMob() != null,
                mob.getNavigation().isInProgress(),
                distanceToPathTargetSq
        ), thresholds);
    }

    public static float getTransitionSpeedModifier(AIContext context, TransitionSpeedModifiers modifiers) {
        if (modifiers == null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("TransitionSpeedModifiers is required");
        }
        return AIContextPolicy.transitionSpeedModifier(context, modifiers.toDomain());
    }

    public static float getTransitionSpeedModifier(LivingEntity entity, AIContext context, TransitionSpeedModifiers modifiers) {
        AIContextPolicy.TransitionSpeedModifiers domain = modifiers != null
                ? modifiers.toDomain()
                : AnimationTransitionConfigHelper.resolve(XenomorphTypeHelper.getXenomorphType(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity)));
        return AIContextPolicy.transitionSpeedModifier(context, domain);
    }

    private AIContextDetector() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("AIContextDetector is a utility class");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_3.parasite.ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.entity.EntityAttributeHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.api.XenomorphTyped;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.attributes.AttributeSupplier;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

/**
 * Minecraft base class for xenomorph mob entities (persistence + shared mob behavior).
 */
public abstract class BaseXenomorphEntity extends PathfinderMob implements XenomorphTyped {

    public BaseXenomorphEntity(EntityType<? extends BaseXenomorphEntity> entityType, Level level) {
        super(entityType, level);
        this.setPersistenceRequired();
    }

    @Override
    public void tick() {
        super.tick();
        if (!this.isPersistenceRequired()) {
            this.setPersistenceRequired();
        }
    }

    @Override
    public boolean removeWhenFarAway(double distanceToClosestPlayer) {
        return false;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean requiresCustomPersistence() {
        return true;
    }

    public static AttributeSupplier.Builder createBaseAttributes() {
        return PathfinderMob.createMobAttributes();
    }

    protected static AttributeSupplier.Builder createAttributesForType(XenomorphType xenomorphType) {
        return EntityAttributeHelper.createXenomorphAttributes(xenomorphType);
    }

    @Override
    public abstract XenomorphType getXenomorphType();

    protected void logPersistenceStatus() {
        ModLogger.debug(
                "BaseXenomorphEntity",
                String.format(
                        "🦾 %s at %s - Persistence: %s, Required: %s",
                        this.getType().toString(),
                        this.blockPosition(),
                        this.isPersistenceRequired(),
                        this.requiresCustomPersistence()));
    }

    protected boolean shouldAvoidTarget(LivingEntity target) {
        if (target == null) {
            return false;
        }
        if (ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.isHostInfected(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(target)))) {
            ModLogger.debug(
                    "BaseXenomorphEntity",
                    String.format(
                            "🦾 %s avoiding target %s - currently infected (facehugged or gestating)",
                            this.getDisplayName().getString(),
                            target.getDisplayName().getString()));
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
}

FILE: XenomorphSoundRegistry.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.registry.ConfigContractException;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigPaths;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.config.SoundHelper;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.core.Holder;
import net.minecraft.core.registries.BuiltInRegistries;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;
import net.minecraft.sounds.SoundEvent;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Centralized sound registry for xenomorph entities.
 * Runtime sound IDs are read from entity JSON via {@link EntityConfigStorage}.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 *
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.0.1
 */
public class XenomorphSoundRegistry {

    /**
     * Gets the ambient sound for a xenomorph type.
     *
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @return The ambient sound event, or null if not registered in the sound registry
     */
    public static SoundEvent getAmbientSound(XenomorphType type) {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(type);
        return resolveSoundEvent(config.ambientSound, type, "visual.ambient_sound");
    }

    /**
     * Gets the hurt sound for a xenomorph type.
     *
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @return The hurt sound event, or null if not registered in the sound registry
     */
    public static SoundEvent getHurtSound(XenomorphType type) {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(type);
        return resolveSoundEvent(config.hurtSound, type, "visual.hurt_sound");
    }

    /**
     * Gets the death sound for a xenomorph type.
     *
     * @param type The xenomorph type
     * @return The death sound event, or null if not registered in the sound registry
     */
    public static SoundEvent getDeathSound(XenomorphType type) {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(type);
        return resolveSoundEvent(config.deathSound, type, "visual.death_sound");
    }

    /**
     * Gets a special sound event by unqualified mod-local key.
     *
     * @param soundKey The special sound key (e.g., "xenomorph.intelligence_activate")
     * @return The sound event, or null if not found
     */
    public static SoundEvent getSpecialSound(String soundKey) {
        return resolveModLocalSoundEvent(soundKey);
    }

    public static void playStepSound(Mob entity, XenomorphType type) {
        SoundEvent soundEvent = getAmbientSound(type);
        SoundHelper.playStepSound(entity, type, soundEvent);
    }

    private static SoundEvent resolveSoundEvent(String soundRef, XenomorphType type, String fieldPath) {
        ResourceLocation soundLocation = parseSoundLocation(soundRef, type, fieldPath);
        return lookupRegisteredSound(soundLocation);
    }

    private static SoundEvent resolveModLocalSoundEvent(String soundKey) {
        ResourceLocation soundLocation = Objects.requireNonNull(
                ResourceLocation.fromNamespaceAndPath(ModContext.MOD_ID, Objects.requireNonNull(soundKey)));
        return lookupRegisteredSound(soundLocation);
    }

    private static ResourceLocation parseSoundLocation(String soundRef, XenomorphType type, String fieldPath) {
        if (soundRef == null || soundRef.isBlank()) {
            throw new ConfigContractException(
                    "XenomorphSoundRegistry", EntityConfigPaths.resourcePath(type), fieldPath, "required when entity config is loaded");
        }
        ResourceLocation location = ResourceLocation.tryParse(soundRef);
        if (location == null) {
            throw new ConfigContractException(
                    "XenomorphSoundRegistry", EntityConfigPaths.resourcePath(type), fieldPath,
                    "invalid ResourceLocation: " + soundRef);
        }
        return location;
    }

    private static SoundEvent lookupRegisteredSound(ResourceLocation soundLocation) {
        Holder.Reference<SoundEvent> holder = BuiltInRegistries.SOUND_EVENT
                .getHolder(Objects.requireNonNull(soundLocation))
                .orElse(null);
        if (holder != null && holder.isBound()) {
            return holder.value();
        }
        return null;
    }
}
