FILE: XenomorphTypeHelper.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.api.XenomorphTyped;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;

/**
 * MC-layer helper: resolves {@link XenomorphType} from {@link LivingEntity} via {@link XenomorphTyped}.
 *
 * <p>Distinct from {@code com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.growth.XenomorphTypeHelper}
 * which operates on {@code LivingEntityRef} through {@code BoundaryServices}. Do not merge.
 */
public final class XenomorphTypeHelper {

    public static XenomorphType getXenomorphType(LivingEntity entity) {
        if (entity == null || !entity.isAlive() || entity.isRemoved()) {
            return null;
        }
        if (entity instanceof XenomorphTyped typed) {
            return typed.getXenomorphType();
        }
        return null;
    }

    public static XenomorphType getXenomorphType(PathfinderMob entity) {
        XenomorphType type = getXenomorphType((LivingEntity) entity);
        return type != null ? type : XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER;
    }

    public static boolean isXenomorph(LivingEntity entity) {
        return getXenomorphType(entity) != null;
    }

    public static String getEntityTypeName(LivingEntity entity) {
        XenomorphType type = getXenomorphType(entity);
        if (type != null) {
            return switch (type) {
                case FACEHUGGER -> "Facehugger";
                case CHESTBURSTER -> "Chestburster";
                case DRONE -> "Drone";
                case GROWTH -> "Growth";
                case PRAETOR -> "Praetor";
                case QUEEN -> "Queen";
                case OVOMORPH -> "Ovomorph";
                case HUMAN -> "Human";
            };
        }
        return entity.getType().getDescription().getString();
    }

    private XenomorphTypeHelper() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("XenomorphTypeHelper is a utility class");
    }
}

PACKAGE: level_1/species/xenomorph/hatch
====================================================================================================

FILE: OvomorphHostQuery.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.hatch;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.EntityConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_2.ovomorph.OvomorphHostSelectionPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.GlassLineOfSightHelper;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

/**
 * MC-side host proximity scan for ovomorph hatching; viability rules delegate to L2 policy.
 */
public final class OvomorphHostQuery {

    private OvomorphHostQuery() {
    }

    public static LivingEntity findNearestViableHost(@Nonnull Mob ovomorph) {
        double proximityDistance = EntityConfigHelper.getConfigValueRequired(
                XenomorphType.OVOMORPH,
                config -> config.hatching != null ? Double.valueOf(config.hatching.proximityDistance) : null,
                "hatching.proximityDistance");

        Level level = ovomorph.level();
        if (level == null) {
            return null;
        }

        List<LivingEntity> nearbyEntities = level.getEntitiesOfClass(
                LivingEntity.class,
                Objects.requireNonNull(ovomorph.getBoundingBox().inflate(proximityDistance)),
                entity -> entity != ovomorph && entity.isAlive());

        LivingEntity nearestHost = null;
        double nearestDistance = Double.MAX_VALUE;

        for (LivingEntity entity : nearbyEntities) {
            var hostRef = BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity);
            if (OvomorphHostSelectionPolicy.isCreativePlayer(hostRef)) {
                continue;
            }
            if (!OvomorphHostSelectionPolicy.isViableHost(hostRef)) {
                continue;
            }
            if (!hasClearLineOfSight(ovomorph, entity)) {
                continue;
            }
            double distance = ovomorph.distanceTo(Objects.requireNonNull(entity));
            if (distance < nearestDistance) {
                nearestDistance = distance;
                nearestHost = entity;
            }
        }
        return nearestHost;
    }

    private static boolean hasClearLineOfSight(Mob ovomorph, LivingEntity target) {
        if (ovomorph.level() == null || target == null || !ovomorph.hasLineOfSight(target)) {
            return false;
        }
        return GlassLineOfSightHelper.hasClearPathWithoutGlass(ovomorph, target);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_10;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.HumanEntityType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.HumanGoalRegistration;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.XenomorphGoalRegistration;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.human.HumanAIBehaviorFactory;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.human.HumanEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_9.XenomorphCompositionDispatch;

/**
 * Wires L0 goal-registration hooks to L5/L2 implementations at mod construction.
 *
 * <p>Human goals resolve {@link HumanType} from {@link HumanEntity} when available.
 */
public final class GoalHookBootstrap {

    private GoalHookBootstrap() {
    }

    public static void wire() {
        XenomorphGoalRegistration.init(XenomorphCompositionDispatch::registerGoals);
        HumanGoalRegistration.init(entity -> {
            HumanEntityType humanType = entity instanceof HumanEntity human
                    ? human.getHumanType()
                    : HumanEntityType.VILLAGER;
            HumanAIBehaviorFactory.registerAIBehavior(entity, humanType);
        });
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_11;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.registry.SystemLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.registry.BlockDamageSystemRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.registry.XenomorphSystemRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_10.GoalHookBootstrap;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.XenomorphTargetRegistration;

/**
 * Wires goal hooks, L2 systems, and xenomorph target registration.
 *
 * <p>Called from L8 {@code ModRegistrationBootstrap} after deferred registers are bound.
 * Maturation is handled by L2 {@code MaturationSystem} (static registration) with timer I/O
 * via {@code BoundaryBootstrap} on server start and {@code MaturationTimed} on entities.
 */
public final class SystemWiringBootstrap {

    private SystemWiringBootstrap() {
    }

    public static void wireAll() {
        GoalHookBootstrap.wire();
        wireSystems();
    }

    private static void wireSystems() {
        SystemLoader.registerSystem(new BlockDamageSystemRegistry());
        SystemLoader.registerSystem(new XenomorphSystemRegistry());
        SystemLoader.loadSystems();
        XenomorphTargetRegistration.registerXenomorphTargets();
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_12.lifecycle;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.lifecycle.ConfigLoaderBootstrap;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_11.lifecycle.SystemWiringBootstrap;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.neoforged.bus.api.IEventBus;

/**
 * Loads static configs before deferred registry lambdas, then registers all mod content.
 */
public final class ModRegistrationBootstrap {

    private ModRegistrationBootstrap() {
    }

    public static void register(@Nonnull IEventBus modEventBus) {
        ConfigLoaderBootstrap.registerConfigLoaders();
        ConfigLoaderBootstrap.loadStaticConfigLoaders();
        ReloadListenerBootstrap.register();
        DeferredRegisterBootstrap.registerAll(modEventBus);
        SystemWiringBootstrap.wireAll();
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.ai.drone;

 * Registers swarm movement, melee, and targeting goals for drones.
 */
public final class DroneSwarmGoalRegistrar {

    private DroneSwarmGoalRegistrar() {
    }

    public static void registerGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        SwarmMovementGoal.registerGoals(entity, aiGoals);
        entity.goalSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.DRONE, "swarm"),
                new MeleeAttackGoal(entity, aiGoals.meleeAttackSpeed, false));
        SwarmTargetingGoal.registerGoals(entity, aiGoals);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.blocks;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.blocks.BaseXenomorphBlock;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.Block;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockBehaviour;
import net.minecraft.world.level.material.PushReaction;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.shapes.VoxelShape;

/**
 * Cocoon Block - Multi-block structure for captured hosts.
 * Placeholder implementation for now (single block).
 * Future enhancement will support 3x1 to 3x3 multi-block structures.
 * 
 * Extends BaseXenomorphBlock to inherit common xenomorph block properties
 * and standardized logging. Implements DRY principle by using base class
 * functionality while providing protective cocoon-specific characteristics.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class CocoonBlock extends BaseXenomorphBlock {
    
    // Full block hitbox for now
    private static final VoxelShape SHAPE = Block.box(0.0D, 0.0D, 0.0D, 16.0D, 16.0D, 16.0D);
    
    /**
     * Constructs a CocoonBlock with the specified properties.
     * Used by DeferredRegister.Blocks.registerBlock() which automatically sets the block ID.
     * 
     * @param properties The block properties (with ID already set)
     */
    public CocoonBlock(BlockBehaviour.Properties properties) {
        super(properties);
    }
    
    @Override
    protected VoxelShape getBlockShape() {
        return SHAPE;
    }
    
    @Override
    protected PushReaction getPushReaction() {
        return PushReaction.BLOCK; // Override to prevent piston movement
    }
    
    // TODO: Future enhancement - multi-block structure support
    // This will require implementing IMultiBlockPart and related interfaces
    // For now, this is a placeholder single block implementation
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.blocks.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.blocks.SpecimenPodBlockEntity;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntityType;

/**
 * L4 indirection for specimen-pod block entity type (breaks L5 ModBlockEntities ↔ Bootstrap cycle).
 *
 * <p>NDE escape hatch: registration lives at {@code level_5} while this supplier indirection
 * at {@code level_2} lets L2 specimen-pod behavior reference the block entity type without a
 * compile-time import of the L5 registration class.
 */
public final class SpecimenPodBlockEntityTypeRegistry {

    private static Supplier<BlockEntityType<SpecimenPodBlockEntity>> supplier;

    private SpecimenPodBlockEntityTypeRegistry() {
    }

    public static void register(Supplier<BlockEntityType<SpecimenPodBlockEntity>> typeSupplier) {
        supplier = typeSupplier;
    }

    public static BlockEntityType<SpecimenPodBlockEntity> get() {
        if (supplier == null) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("SpecimenPodBlockEntityTypeRegistry not initialized");
        }
        return supplier.get();
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.boundary;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.AttachmentServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeEffectApplicationAdapter;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeEntitySpawnAdapter;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeMaturationStateAdapter;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.boundary.NeoForgeEntityPresentationAdapter;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.event.server.ServerStartingEvent;

public final class BoundaryBootstrap {
    private BoundaryBootstrap() {}

    public static void onServerStarting(ServerStartingEvent event) {
        initServerBoundaryStack(Objects.requireNonNull(event.getServer()));
    }

    public static void initServerBoundaryStack(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        MinecraftServer boundServer = Objects.requireNonNull(server);
        BoundaryServices.init(
                new NeoForgeWorldQueryAdapter(boundServer),
                new NeoForgeWorldMutationAdapter(boundServer),
                new NeoForgeEntitySpawnAdapter(boundServer),
                new NeoForgeEffectApplicationAdapter(boundServer),
                new NeoForgeXenomorphFormQueryAdapter(boundServer),
                new NeoForgeEntityQueryAdapter(boundServer),
                new NeoForgeEntityPresentationAdapter(boundServer)
        );
        AttachmentServices.init(new NeoForgeAttachmentStateAdapter(boundServer));
        FacehuggerSpentTransitionServices.init(new NeoForgeFacehuggerSpentTransitionAdapter(boundServer));
        MaturationServices.init(new NeoForgeMaturationStateAdapter(boundServer));
    }
}

FILE: NeoForgeSuffocationProbe.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.boundary;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.AIConfigResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.SurvivalSuffocationPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeStuckInBlocksProbe;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity.XenomorphTypeHelper;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;

/**
 * L3 survival probe: reads MC entity state and applies L2 suffocation policy.
 */
public final class NeoForgeSuffocationProbe {

    private NeoForgeSuffocationProbe() {}

    public static boolean isSuffocating(PathfinderMob entity) {
        if (entity.isInWall()) {
            ModLogger.debug("NeoForgeSuffocationProbe", "Entity detected as in wall - triggering escape");
            return true;
        }

        XenomorphType type = XenomorphTypeHelper.getXenomorphType(entity);
        boolean stuck = NeoForgeStuckInBlocksProbe.isStuckInBlocks(entity, Objects.requireNonNull(entity.level()));
        double lowThreshold = AIConfigResolver.getLowAirSupplyThreshold(type);
        double criticalThreshold = AIConfigResolver.getCriticalAirSupplyThreshold(type);

        boolean suffocating = SurvivalSuffocationPolicy.isSuffocating(
                false,
                stuck,
                entity.getAirSupply(),
                entity.getMaxAirSupply(),
                lowThreshold,
                criticalThreshold);

        if (suffocating) {
            if (stuck) {
                ModLogger.debug("NeoForgeSuffocationProbe",
                        "Entity stuck in blocks with low air supply - triggering escape");
            } else {
                ModLogger.debug("NeoForgeSuffocationProbe",
                        "Entity has critically low air supply - triggering escape");
            }
        }
        return suffocating;
    }
}

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.server.MinecraftServer;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.LivingEntityRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_2.xenomorph.XenomorphFormQueryPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeLevelResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity.XenomorphTypeHelper;

public final class NeoForgeXenomorphFormQueryAdapter implements XenomorphFormQueryPort {

    private final MinecraftServer server;

    public NeoForgeXenomorphFormQueryAdapter(@Nonnull MinecraftServer server) {
        this.server = server;
    }

    @Override
    public XenomorphType resolveForm(LivingEntityRef ref) {
        if (ref == null) {
            return XenomorphType.DRONE;
        }
        UUID entityId = Objects.requireNonNull(ref.entityId(), "entityId");
        return NeoForgeLevelResolver.resolve(server, ref.world())
                .flatMap(level -> {
                    var entity = level.getEntity(entityId);
                    if (entity instanceof LivingEntity living) {
                        return Optional.of(XenomorphTypeHelper.getXenomorphType(living));
                    }
                    return Optional.empty();
                })
                .orElse(XenomorphType.DRONE);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.config;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.ai.AIBehaviorConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.ai.AIBehaviorConfigNames;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.ai.AIBehaviorConfigCatalog;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.config.BaseConfigLoader;
import net.minecraft.server.packs.resources.ResourceManager;

/**
 * Loads AI behavior configurations from JSON files.
 *
 * <p>Populates {@link AIBehaviorConfigCatalog} (L1) on load/reload for {@code BehaviorConfigHelper}.
 */
public class AIBehaviorConfigLoader extends BaseConfigLoader<AIBehaviorConfig> {

    private static AIBehaviorConfigLoader instance;

    private AIBehaviorConfigLoader() {
        super("AIBehaviorConfigLoader");
    }

    public static AIBehaviorConfigLoader getInstance() {
        if (instance == null) {
            instance = new AIBehaviorConfigLoader();
        }
        return instance;
    }

    @Override
    protected void putConfig(String configName, AIBehaviorConfig config) {
        super.putConfig(configName, config);
        AIBehaviorConfigCatalog.register(configName, config);
    }

    @Override
    protected void clearConfigs() {
        super.clearConfigs();
        AIBehaviorConfigCatalog.clear();
    }

    @Override
    protected String getResourcePath(String configName) {
        return "weylandyutani:ai_behaviors/" + configName + ".json";
    }

    @Override
    protected Class<AIBehaviorConfig> getConfigClass() {
        return AIBehaviorConfig.class;
    }

    @Override
    protected String[] getDefaultConfigNames() {
        return AIBehaviorConfigNames.shipped();
    }

    @Override
    protected boolean validateConfig(AIBehaviorConfig config, String configName) {
        if (config == null) {
            ModLogger.warn("AI behavior config is null: " + configName);
            return false;
        }
        if (config.behaviorType == null || config.behaviorType.isEmpty()) {
            ModLogger.warn("AI behavior config missing behaviorType: " + configName);
            return false;
        }
        if (config.speedMultipliers == null) {
            ModLogger.warn("AI behavior config missing speedMultipliers: " + configName);
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }

    public static AIBehaviorConfig getBehaviorConfig(String behaviorType) {
        return getInstance().getConfig(behaviorType);
    }

    public static void loadBehaviorConfigs(ResourceManager resourceManager) {
        getInstance().loadConfigs(resourceManager);
    }

    public static boolean areConfigsLoaded() {
        return getInstance().isLoaded();
    }

    public static void reloadBehaviorConfigs(ResourceManager resourceManager) {
        getInstance().reloadConfigs(resourceManager);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.init;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.core.registries.Registries;
import net.minecraft.world.effect.MobEffect;
import net.neoforged.bus.api.IEventBus;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredHolder;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredRegister;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.effects.FacehuggerAttachmentEffect;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.effects.FacehuggerImplantationEffect;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.effects.GestationEffect;

/**
 * Registry for custom status effects.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 *
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class EffectInit {

    public static final DeferredRegister<MobEffect> EFFECTS =
            DeferredRegister.create(Objects.requireNonNull(Registries.MOB_EFFECT), ModContext.MOD_ID);

    public static final DeferredHolder<MobEffect, GestationEffect> GESTATION =
            EFFECTS.register("gestation", () -> new GestationEffect());

    public static final DeferredHolder<MobEffect, FacehuggerAttachmentEffect> FACEHUGGER_ATTACHMENT =
            EFFECTS.register("facehugger_attachment", () -> new FacehuggerAttachmentEffect());

    public static final DeferredHolder<MobEffect, FacehuggerImplantationEffect> FACEHUGGER_IMPLANTATION =
            EFFECTS.register("facehugger_implantation", () -> new FacehuggerImplantationEffect());

    /**
     * Registers all effects with the mod event bus.
     *
     * @param eventBus The mod event bus
     */
    public static void register(@Nonnull IEventBus eventBus) {
        EFFECTS.register(eventBus);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.items;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.network.chat.Component;
import net.minecraft.sounds.SoundEvents;
import net.minecraft.sounds.SoundSource;
import net.minecraft.world.InteractionHand;
import net.minecraft.world.InteractionResultHolder;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;
import net.minecraft.world.item.ItemStack;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.AABB;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.items.MotionTrackerConfigLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.detection.MotionTrackerDetectionPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.entity.DirectionHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.items.BaseItem;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity.XenomorphTypeHelper;

/**
 * Motion Tracker — thin MC item; scan classification via {@link MotionTrackerDetectionPolicy}.
 */
public class MotionTrackerItem extends BaseItem {

    public MotionTrackerItem(Properties properties) {
        super(properties);
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public InteractionResultHolder<ItemStack> use(
            @Nonnull Level level,
            @Nonnull Player player,
            @Nonnull InteractionHand hand) {
        ItemStack itemStack = Objects.requireNonNull(player.getItemInHand(hand));

        if (!performCommonValidation(player, itemStack, level)) {
            return Objects.requireNonNull(InteractionResultHolder.fail(itemStack));
        }

        if (!level.isClientSide) {
            long startTime = System.currentTimeMillis();

            try {
                if (player.getCooldowns().isOnCooldown(this)) {
                    player.displayClientMessage(
                            Objects.requireNonNull(
                                    Component.translatable("message.weylandyutani.motion_tracker.charging")),
                            true);
                    return Objects.requireNonNull(InteractionResultHolder.fail(itemStack));
                }

                scanForEntities(level, player);
                player.getCooldowns().addCooldown(this, MotionTrackerConfigLoader.cooldownTicks());
                BlockPos soundPos = Objects.requireNonNull(player.blockPosition());
                level.playSound(
                        null,
                        soundPos,
                        Objects.requireNonNull(SoundEvents.NOTE_BLOCK_PLING.value()),
                        SoundSource.PLAYERS,
                        0.5f,
                        1.0f);
                logItemUsage(player, "Motion tracker activated");
            } catch (Exception e) {
                logEffectFailure(player, "Motion tracker scan failed: " + e.getMessage());
            } finally {
                logPerformance("motion_tracker_scan", System.currentTimeMillis() - startTime);
            }
        }

        return Objects.requireNonNull(InteractionResultHolder.sidedSuccess(itemStack, level.isClientSide));
    }

    private void scanForEntities(@Nonnull Level level, @Nonnull Player player) {
        int entitiesFound = 0;
        AABB scanArea = Objects.requireNonNull(player.getBoundingBox())
                .inflate(MotionTrackerConfigLoader.detectionRadius());

        for (LivingEntity entity : level.getEntitiesOfClass(LivingEntity.class, Objects.requireNonNull(scanArea))) {

            if (entity == player) {
                continue;
            }
            if (entitiesFound >= MotionTrackerConfigLoader.maxEntitiesToReport()) {
                break;
            }

            boolean hostileMob = entity instanceof Mob mob && !mob.getType().getCategory().isFriendly();
            if (MotionTrackerDetectionPolicy.shouldReport(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity), hostileMob)) {
                double distance = player.distanceTo(Objects.requireNonNull(entity));
                String direction = DirectionHelper.getCardinalDirection(player, entity);
                String entityType = XenomorphTypeHelper.getEntityTypeName(entity);

                player.displayClientMessage(
                        Objects.requireNonNull(Component.translatable(
                                "message.weylandyutani.motion_tracker.detected",
                                entityType,
                                direction,
                                String.format("%.1f", distance))),
                        false);
                entitiesFound++;
            }
        }

        if (entitiesFound == 0) {
            player.displayClientMessage(
                    Objects.requireNonNull(
                            Component.translatable("message.weylandyutani.motion_tracker.no_entities")),
                    false);
        } else if (MotionTrackerDetectionPolicy.shouldPlayAlertTone(entitiesFound)) {
            BlockPos soundPos = Objects.requireNonNull(player.blockPosition());
            level.playSound(
                    null,
                    soundPos,
                    Objects.requireNonNull(SoundEvents.NOTE_BLOCK_BASS.value()),
                    SoundSource.PLAYERS,
                    0.7f,
                    0.5f);
        }
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.human;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.HumanEntityType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.XenomorphTargetRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.human.DefensiveVillagerAI;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.monster.Monster;

/**
 * Human-specific AI behavior factory.
 * Routes human entities to the correct AI behavior class based on behavior_type.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: NEW
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8
 */
public class HumanAIBehaviorFactory {
    
    /**
     * Registers AI goals for a human entity based on its JSON configuration.
     * Uses behavior_type to determine which AI class to use.
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to register goals for
     * @param humanType The human type to get configuration for
     */
    public static void registerAIBehavior(PathfinderMob entity, HumanEntityType humanType) {
        // TODO: Refactor EntityConfigStorage to use EntityType interface instead of XenomorphType
        // For now, bridge to XenomorphType.HUMAN for config access until we have separate human configs
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(XenomorphType.HUMAN);
        
        if (config == null || config.aiGoals == null) {
            ModLogger.warn("HumanAIBehaviorFactory", "⚠️ No AI goals config found for " + humanType);
            return;
        }
        
        String behaviorType = config.aiGoals.behaviorType;
        if (behaviorType == null) {
            ModLogger.warn("HumanAIBehaviorFactory", "⚠️ No behavior type specified for " + humanType + " - using fallback");
            behaviorType = "defensive_villager";
        }
        ModLogger.debug("HumanAIBehaviorFactory", "🤖 Registering AI behavior: " + behaviorType + " for " + humanType);
        
        // Route to appropriate AI behavior class based on behavior_type
        switch (behaviorType) {
            case "defensive_villager":
                DefensiveVillagerAI.registerGoals(entity, config.aiGoals);
                break;
                
            default:
                ModLogger.warn("HumanAIBehaviorFactory", "⚠️ Unknown behavior type: " + behaviorType + " for " + humanType);
                // Fallback to defensive villager behavior
                DefensiveVillagerAI.registerGoals(entity, config.aiGoals);
                break;
        }

        if (entity instanceof Monster human) {
            XenomorphTargetRegistry.registerXenomorphTargets(human);
        }
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.human;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.nbt.CompoundTag;
import net.minecraft.sounds.SoundEvent;
import net.minecraft.world.damagesource.DamageSource;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.attributes.AttributeSupplier;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.monster.Monster;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.HumanEntityType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.HumanGoalRegistration;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.entity.EntityAttributeHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity.XenomorphSoundRegistry;

/**
 * Human entity for testing xenomorph interactions.
 * Simple, concrete implementation focused on basic survival behavior.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 *
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class HumanEntity extends Monster {

    private static final XenomorphType HUMAN = XenomorphType.HUMAN;
    private static final String NBT_HUMAN_TYPE = "HumanType";

    private HumanEntityType humanType = HumanEntityType.VILLAGER;

    public HumanEntity(EntityType<? extends Monster> entityType, Level level) {
        super(entityType, level);
    }

    public HumanEntityType getHumanType() {
        return humanType;
    }

    public void setHumanType(HumanEntityType humanType) {
        this.humanType = humanType != null ? humanType : HumanEntityType.VILLAGER;
    }

    public static AttributeSupplier.Builder createAttributes() {
        // TODO: Refactor EntityAttributeHelper to use EntityType interface instead of XenomorphType
        return EntityAttributeHelper.createHumanAttributes(HUMAN);
    }

    @Override
    protected void registerGoals() {
        HumanGoalRegistration.registerGoals(this);
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getAmbientSound() {
        // TODO: Refactor XenomorphSoundRegistry to use EntityType interface instead of XenomorphType
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getAmbientSound(HUMAN);
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getHurtSound(@Nonnull DamageSource damageSource) {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getHurtSound(HUMAN);
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getDeathSound() {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getDeathSound(HUMAN);
    }

    @Override
    protected void playStepSound(@Nonnull BlockPos pos, @Nonnull BlockState state) {
        XenomorphSoundRegistry.playStepSound(this, HUMAN);
    }

    @Override
    public void addAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.addAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        compound.putString(NBT_HUMAN_TYPE, Objects.requireNonNull(humanType.name()));
    }

    @Override
    public void readAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.readAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        if (compound.contains(NBT_HUMAN_TYPE)) {
            try {
                humanType = HumanEntityType.valueOf(compound.getString(NBT_HUMAN_TYPE));
            } catch (IllegalArgumentException ignored) {
                humanType = HumanEntityType.VILLAGER;
            }
        }
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.ai.chestburster;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeCombatThreatAdapter;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.boundary.NeoForgePositionSearchAdapter;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.Goal;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.Vec3;

/**
 * Goal for fleeing from threats.
 * Extracted from EscapeAndHideBehaviorCoordinator for single responsibility.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.0.2
 */
public class FleeFromThreatsGoal extends Goal {
    private final PathfinderMob entity;
    private final EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals;
    private LivingEntity threat;
    
    public FleeFromThreatsGoal(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        this.entity = entity;
        this.aiGoals = aiGoals;
    }
    
    @Override
    public boolean canUse() {
        double fleeDistance = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromMovement(aiGoals, "flee_distance");
        
        // Find nearby threats using centralized helper
        this.threat = NeoForgeCombatThreatAdapter.findNearestThreat(Objects.requireNonNull(entity), fleeDistance);
        
        boolean shouldFlee = threat != null && entity.distanceTo(Objects.requireNonNull(threat)) < fleeDistance;
        if (shouldFlee) {
            ModLogger.debug("FleeFromThreatsGoal", "🚨 Threat detected! Distance: " + String.format("%.1f", entity.distanceTo(Objects.requireNonNull(threat))) + " blocks");
        }
        
        return shouldFlee;
    }
    
    @Override
    public void start() {
        if (threat != null) {
            ModLogger.debug("FleeFromThreatsGoal", "🏃 Starting flee behavior from threat");
            // Move away from threat using centralized helper
            Vec3 threatPos = Objects.requireNonNull(threat.position());
            Vec3 entityPos = Objects.requireNonNull(entity.position());
            Vec3 fleeDirection = Objects.requireNonNull(entityPos.subtract(threatPos).normalize());
            
            Vec3 fleePos = NeoForgePositionSearchAdapter.searchVec3InRadius(
                entity, 
                fleeDirection, 
                8.0, 
                10, 
                pos -> entity.level().getBlockState(
                        Objects.requireNonNull(BlockPos.containing(Objects.requireNonNull(pos)))).isAir()
            );
            
            if (fleePos != null) {
                double escapeSpeedMultiplier = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromMovement(
                        aiGoals, "escape_speed_multiplier");
                entity.getNavigation().moveTo(fleePos.x, fleePos.y, fleePos.z, aiGoals.strollSpeed * escapeSpeedMultiplier);
                ModLogger.debug("FleeFromThreatsGoal", "✅ Fleeing to position: " + String.format("%.1f, %.1f, %.1f", fleePos.x, fleePos.y, fleePos.z));
            } else {
                ModLogger.warn("FleeFromThreatsGoal", "⚠️ Could not find safe flee position");
            }
        }
    }
}

FILE: HideInDarkPlacesGoal.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.ai.chestburster;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.WorldRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.AIConfigResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_3.ai.ChestbursterHidePolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeCombatThreatAdapter;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.boundary.NeoForgePositionSearchAdapter;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.Goal;
import net.minecraft.world.level.LightLayer;

/**
 * Goal for hiding in dark places.
 * Extracted from EscapeAndHideBehaviorCoordinator for single responsibility.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.0.2
 */
public class HideInDarkPlacesGoal extends Goal {
    private final PathfinderMob entity;
    private final EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals;
    private BlockPos hidePos;
    
    public HideInDarkPlacesGoal(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        this.entity = entity;
        this.aiGoals = aiGoals;
    }
    
    @Override
    public boolean canUse() {
        double threatRadius = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromMovement(aiGoals, "safety_search_radius");
        boolean hasThreats = NeoForgeCombatThreatAdapter.hasThreatsNearby(Objects.requireNonNull(entity), threatRadius);
        
        if (!ChestbursterHidePolicy.shouldSeekHide(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(entity), hasThreats)) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ModLogger.debug("HideInDarkPlacesGoal", "🌑 Threats detected, seeking dark hiding place");
        return true;
    }
    
    @Override
    public void start() {
        this.hidePos = findDarkHidingSpot();
        if (hidePos != null) {
            ModLogger.debug("HideInDarkPlacesGoal", "🏃 Moving to dark hiding spot: " + hidePos.toString());
            if (entity.level() != null) {
                ModLogger.debug("HideInDarkPlacesGoal", "✅ Found dark hiding spot at light level: " + entity.level().getBrightness(LightLayer.BLOCK, Objects.requireNonNull(hidePos)));
            }
            entity.getNavigation().moveTo(hidePos.getX(), hidePos.getY(), hidePos.getZ(), aiGoals.strollSpeed);
        } else {
            ModLogger.warn("HideInDarkPlacesGoal", "⚠️ Could not find suitable dark hiding spot");
        }
    }
    
    private BlockPos findDarkHidingSpot() {
        double maxSearchRadius = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromMovement(aiGoals, "hide_search_radius");
        int searchAttempts = AIConfigHelper.requireIntFromMovement(aiGoals, "search_attempts");
        int lightLevelDark = AIConfigResolver.getLightLevelDark(XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER);
        
        return NeoForgePositionSearchAdapter.searchBlockPosInRadius(
            entity,
            maxSearchRadius,
            searchAttempts,
            pos -> {
                if (entity.level() == null) {
                    return false;
                }
                WorldRef world = BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(entity.level());
                BlockPosRef ref = BoundaryRefs.from(pos);
                int brightness = entity.level().getBrightness(LightLayer.BLOCK, Objects.requireNonNull(pos));
                return ChestbursterHidePolicy.isValidHideSpot(world, ref, brightness, lightLevelDark);
            }
        );
    }
}

FILE: package-info.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/**

FILE: EggLayingAreaValidator.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.ai.queen;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.queen.EggLayingPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.EggLayingWorkflow;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.queen.EggLayingConfigAccess;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.ai.core.EntityDetectionHelper;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

/**
 * Spatial validation for queen egg laying.
 */
public final class EggLayingAreaValidator {

    private final EggLayingConfigAccess configAccess;

    public EggLayingAreaValidator(EggLayingConfigAccess configAccess) {
        this.configAccess = configAccess;
    }

    public boolean canLayEggInArea(ServerLevel level, BlockPos centerPos) {
        EggLayingWorkflow.Limits limits = configAccess.limits();
        var world = BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(level);
        var center = BoundaryRefs.from(centerPos);

        int eggCount = EggLayingWorkflow.countEggsInArea(world, center, limits);
        int chunkEggCount = countEggsInSameChunk(level, centerPos, limits);

        if (!EggLayingWorkflow.canLayInArea(eggCount, chunkEggCount, limits)) {
            if (!EggLayingPolicy.isChunkBelowEggLimit(chunkEggCount, limits.maxEggsPerChunk())) {
                ModLogger.info("EggLayingAreaValidator",
                        "Chunk egg limit reached: " + chunkEggCount + "/" + limits.maxEggsPerChunk());
            } else {
                ModLogger.info("EggLayingAreaValidator",
                        "Area egg limit reached: " + eggCount + "/" + limits.maxEggsInArea());
            }
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }

    public boolean isSuitableEggLocation(ServerLevel level, BlockPosRef pos) {
        if (!EggLayingWorkflow.isLocationClearOfEggs(
                BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(level), pos, configAccess.getMinDistanceBetweenEggs())) {
            return false;
        }

        BlockPos blockPos = new BlockPos(pos.x(), pos.y(), pos.z());
        BlockState groundBlock = level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(blockPos.below()));
        BlockState airBlock = level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(blockPos));
        BlockState airAbove = level.getBlockState(Objects.requireNonNull(blockPos.above()));

        return groundBlock.canOcclude() && airBlock.isAir() && airAbove.isAir();
    }

    private int countEggsInSameChunk(ServerLevel level, BlockPos centerPos, EggLayingWorkflow.Limits limits) {
        int chunkEggCount = 0;
        int searchRadius = limits.searchRadius();

        for (int x = -searchRadius; x <= searchRadius; x++) {
            for (int z = -searchRadius; z <= searchRadius; z++) {
                for (int y = -limits.verticalSearchRange(); y <= limits.verticalSearchRange(); y++) {
                    BlockPos checkPos = centerPos.offset(x, y, z);
                    if (EntityDetectionHelper.hasOvomorphAt(level, checkPos)
                            && level.getChunkAt(Objects.requireNonNull(checkPos)).getPos().equals(level.getChunkAt(centerPos).getPos())) {
                        chunkEggCount++;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return chunkEggCount;
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.ai.queen;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.CommonGoalRegistrar;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.StandardTargetingHelper;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.MeleeAttackGoal;

/**
 * Hive Mother AI behavior - stay near nest, reproduce, command hive.
 * Used by Queen entities for hive management behavior.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class HiveMotherAI {
    
    public static void registerGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerFloatGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.QUEEN, "float"));

        entity.goalSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.QUEEN, "melee"),
                new MeleeAttackGoal(entity, aiGoals.meleeAttackSpeed, false));

        double speedMultiplier = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromSpecialAbilities(
                aiGoals, "hive_mother_speed_multiplier");
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerStrollGoal(
                entity,
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.QUEEN, "stroll"),
                aiGoals.strollSpeed * speedMultiplier);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerRandomLookAroundGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.QUEEN, "random_look"));

        StandardTargetingHelper.registerStandardTargetingGoals(entity, XenomorphType.QUEEN);

        // TODO: Future hive-specific goals (placeholders for systems not yet implemented):
        // - StayNearNestGoal (stay within nest protection radius)
        // - SpawnEggsGoal (spawn eggs periodically)
        // - BuildNestGoal (build and maintain nest)
        // - CommandHiveGoal (command all xenomorphs in hive)
        // - AlterEnvironmentGoal (modify blocks around nest)
    }
}

FILE: AnimationTransitionHelper.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.client.animation;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.ai.AIContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.client.animation.AIContextDetector;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * Helper class for animation transition duration calculations.
 * Extracted from animation handlers to eliminate duplicate logic.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class AnimationTransitionHelper {
    
    /**
     * Gets the transition duration from entity config, adjusted by AI context.
     * Falls back to 30 ticks (1.5 seconds) if config is not available.
     * 
     * TUNING: Adjust "transition_duration_ticks" and "transition_modifiers" in entity JSON config files
     * (e.g., data/weylandyutani/entity/xenomorph/human/drone.json under "client_parameters")
     * 
     * @param entity The entity to get transition duration for
     * @param xenomorphType The xenomorph type for config lookup
     * @return Transition duration in ticks (clamped to 10-60 ticks)
     */
    public static int getTransitionDuration(LivingEntity entity, XenomorphType xenomorphType) {
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);
        int baseDuration = 30; // Default fallback: 1.5 seconds at 20 TPS
        
        if (config != null && config.clientParameters != null) {
            baseDuration = config.clientParameters.transitionDurationTicks;
        }
        
        // Detect AI context and apply speed modifier
        AIContext context = AIContextDetector.detectContext(entity);
        AIContextDetector.TransitionSpeedModifiers modifiers = AIContextDetector.TransitionSpeedModifiers.fromConfig(config);
        float speedModifier = AIContextDetector.getTransitionSpeedModifier(entity, context, modifiers);
        
        // Apply modifier (faster = shorter duration, slower = longer duration)
        int adjustedDuration = Math.round(baseDuration / speedModifier);
        
        // Clamp to reasonable bounds (10-60 ticks)
        return Math.max(10, Math.min(60, adjustedDuration));
    }
    
    // Private constructor to prevent instantiation
    private AnimationTransitionHelper() {
        throw new UnsupportedOperationException("AnimationTransitionHelper is a utility class and cannot be instantiated");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity;

        XenomorphSoundRegistry.playStepSound(this, XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER);
    }
    
    @Override
    public void tick() {
        super.tick();
        if (!level().isClientSide()) {
            EntityGrowthAPI.processEntityGrowth(this);
        }
    }
    
    public int getMaturationTimer() {
        return this.maturationTimer;
    }
    
    public void setMaturationTimer(int timer) {
        this.maturationTimer = timer;
    }
    
    @Override
    public void addAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.addAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        MaturationTimedPersistence.writeSaveData(this, compound);
    }
    
    @Override
    public void readAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.readAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        MaturationTimedPersistence.readSaveData(this, compound);
    }
}

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.parasite.MaturationTimed;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.territory.DroneTerritoryHelper;

/**
 * Drone entity - the worker xenomorph.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class DroneEntity extends BaseXenomorphEntity implements MaturationTimed {
    
    // Animation state tracking for rendering
    public final AnimationState walkingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState idleAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState standingToCrawlingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState crawlingToStandingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState jumpingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState fallingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    
    // Track transition start times (1.5 seconds = 30 ticks default, configurable in handler) - public for handler access
    public int standingToCrawlingStartTick = -1;
    public int crawlingToStandingStartTick = -1;
    
    private int maturationTimer = 0;
    
    public DroneEntity(EntityType<? extends DroneEntity> entityType, Level level) {
        super(entityType, level);
    }
    
    public static AttributeSupplier.Builder createAttributes() {
        // Use centralized helper for extra attributes (DRY principle)
        return EntityAttributeHelper.addAttackKnockback(
            createAttributesForType(XenomorphType.DRONE), 
            XenomorphType.DRONE
        );
    }
    
    @Override
    public XenomorphType getXenomorphType() {
        return XenomorphType.DRONE;
    }
    
    @Override
    protected void registerGoals() {
        // Delegate to AI system for clean separation of concerns
        XenomorphGoalRegistration.registerGoals(this, XenomorphType.DRONE);
    }
    
    // MobType method removed - not needed for basic functionality
    
    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getAmbientSound() {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getAmbientSound(XenomorphType.DRONE);
    }
    
    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getHurtSound(@Nonnull DamageSource damageSource) {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getHurtSound(XenomorphType.DRONE);
    }
    
    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getDeathSound() {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getDeathSound(XenomorphType.DRONE);
    }
    
    @Override
    protected void playStepSound(@Nonnull BlockPos pos, @Nonnull BlockState state) {
        XenomorphSoundRegistry.playStepSound(this, XenomorphType.DRONE);
    }
    
    @Override
    public void tick() {
        super.tick();
        if (!level().isClientSide()) {
            EntityGrowthAPI.processEntityGrowth(this);
        }
    }
    
    public int getMaturationTimer() {
        return this.maturationTimer;
    }
    
    public void setMaturationTimer(int timer) {
        this.maturationTimer = timer;
    }
    
    @Override
    public void addAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.addAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        MaturationTimedPersistence.writeSaveData(this, compound);
    }
    
    @Override
    public void readAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.readAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        MaturationTimedPersistence.readSaveData(this, compound);
    }
    
    /**
     * Find the nearest nest to patrol.
     * Delegates to DroneTerritoryHelper for territory queries.
     * 
     * @return The nearest nest position, or null if none found
     */
    public BlockPos findNearestNest() {
        if (level().isClientSide()) {
            return null;
        }
        var nest = DroneTerritoryHelper.findNearestNest(BoundaryRefs.from(blockPosition()));
        return nest != null ? BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(nest) : null;
    }

    public boolean isWithinNestTerritory() {
        if (level().isClientSide()) {
            return false;
        }
        return DroneTerritoryHelper.isWithinNestTerritory(BoundaryRefs.from(blockPosition()));
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.parasite.AttachmentState;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.UUID;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import javax.annotation.Nullable;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.nbt.CompoundTag;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;
import net.minecraft.sounds.SoundEvent;
import net.minecraft.world.damagesource.DamageSource;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.AnimationState;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.attributes.AttributeSupplier;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

/**
 * Facehugger entity — aggressive parasite that impregnates hosts.
 *
 * <p>L0 helpers: {@link FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence}, {@link FacehuggerRotationLock},
 * {@link FacehuggerSpentGoals}. FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 *
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.0.1
 */
public class FacehuggerEntity extends BaseXenomorphEntity
        implements FacehuggerAttachmentEntity {

    private int attachmentTicks = 0;
    private AttachmentState attachmentState = AttachmentState.FREE;
    private int spentTimer = 0;
    private float attachmentYRot = 0.0f;
    private float attachmentXRot = 0.0f;
    private boolean attachmentRotationSet = false;
    @Nullable
    private UUID pendingTargetUUID = null;

    public final AnimationState walkAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState idleAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState attachmentAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState jumpingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState fallingAnimationState = new AnimationState();

    public FacehuggerEntity(EntityType<? extends FacehuggerEntity> entityType, Level level) {
        super(entityType, level);
    }

    @Override
    public AttachmentState getAttachmentState() {
        return attachmentState;
    }

    @Override
    public void setAttachmentState(AttachmentState state) {
        if (this.attachmentState != state) {
            ModLogger.info("FacehuggerEntity",
                    String.format("🦾 Facehugger %s state changed: %s -> %s",
                            this.getDisplayName().getString(), this.attachmentState, state));
            this.attachmentState = state;
        }
    }

    @Override
    public void restoreAttachmentState(AttachmentState state) {
        this.attachmentState = state;
    }

    @Override
    public int getSpentTimer() {
        return spentTimer;
    }

    @Override
    public void setSpentTimer(int ticks) {
        this.spentTimer = ticks;
    }

    @Override
    public float getAttachmentYRot() {
        return attachmentYRot;
    }

    @Override
    public void setAttachmentYRot(float yRot) {
        this.attachmentYRot = yRot;
    }

    @Override
    public float getAttachmentXRot() {
        return attachmentXRot;
    }

    @Override
    public void setAttachmentXRot(float xRot) {
        this.attachmentXRot = xRot;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isAttachmentRotationSet() {
        return attachmentRotationSet;
    }

    @Override
    public void setAttachmentRotationSet(boolean set) {
        this.attachmentRotationSet = set;
    }

    @Override
    @Nullable
    public UUID getPendingTargetUUID() {
        return pendingTargetUUID;
    }

    @Override
    public void setPendingTargetUUID(@Nullable UUID uuid) {
        this.pendingTargetUUID = uuid;
    }

    public static AttributeSupplier.Builder createAttributes() {
        return createAttributesForType(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);
    }

    @Override
    public XenomorphType getXenomorphType() {
        return XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER;
    }

    @Override
    protected void registerGoals() {
        ModLogger.info("FacehuggerEntity",
                "🦾 Facehugger " + this.getDisplayName().getString() + " registering AI goals...");
        XenomorphGoalRegistration.registerGoals(this, XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);
        ModLogger.info("FacehuggerEntity",
                String.format("🦾 Facehugger %s AI goals registered - goalSelector size: %d, targetSelector size: %d",
                        this.getDisplayName().getString(),
                        this.goalSelector.getAvailableGoals().size(),
                        this.targetSelector.getAvailableGoals().size()));
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getAmbientSound() {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getAmbientSound(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getHurtSound(@Nonnull DamageSource damageSource) {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getHurtSound(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getDeathSound() {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getDeathSound(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);
    }

    @Override
    protected void playStepSound(@Nonnull BlockPos pos, @Nonnull BlockState state) {
        XenomorphSoundRegistry.playStepSound(this, XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean hurt(@Nonnull DamageSource damageSource, float amount) {
        LivingEntity target = this.getTarget();
        if (target != null && AttachmentRules.shouldRedirectDamageToHost(this.getAttachmentState(), this.attachmentTicks)) {
            if (target.isAlive()) {
                target.hurt(damageSource, amount);
            }
            return false;
        }
        return super.hurt(damageSource, amount);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean doHurtTarget(@Nonnull Entity target) {
        return AttachmentRules.shouldFacehuggerDealDamage();
    }

    @Override
    public void push(@Nonnull Entity entity) {
        if (AttachmentRules.isImmovableDuringAttachment(this.getAttachmentState(), this.attachmentTicks)) {
            return;
        }
        super.push(entity);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isPushable() {
        if (AttachmentRules.isImmovableDuringAttachment(this.getAttachmentState(), this.attachmentTicks)) {
            return false;
        }
        return super.isPushable();
    }

    public static boolean isEntityBeingFacehugged(LivingEntity entity) {
        return ParasiteLifecycleAPI.getInfectionStage(entity)
                == ParasiteLifecycleBootstrap.InfectionStage.ATTACHING;
    }

    @Override
    public void markAsSpent() {
        FacehuggerTickWorkflow.applyMarkAsSpent(this);
        FacehuggerSpentGoals.registerWanderGoals(this);

        int spentWanderTime = AttachmentConfigHelper.getSpentWanderTime();
        ModLogger.info("FacehuggerEntity",
                String.format("🦾 Facehugger %s marked as spent - will wander for %d ticks",
                        this.getDisplayName().getString(), spentWanderTime));
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isSpent() {
        return AttachmentRules.isSpentState(this.attachmentState);
    }

    @Override
    public LivingEntityRef getAttachmentTarget() {
        LivingEntity target = getTarget();
        return target != null ? BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(target) : null;
    }

    @Override
    public void setAttachmentTarget(LivingEntityRef target) {
        if (target == null) {
            setTarget((LivingEntity) null);
            return;
        }
        if (this.level() instanceof ServerLevel serverLevel
                && serverLevel.getEntity(Objects.requireNonNull(target.entityId())) instanceof LivingEntity living) {
            setTarget(living);
        }
    }

    @Override
    public int getAttachmentTicks() {
        return attachmentTicks;
    }

    @Override
    public void setAttachmentTicks(int ticks) {
        this.attachmentTicks = ticks;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean requiresCustomPersistence() {
        return !this.isDeadOrDying();
    }

    @Override
    public void tick() {
        super.tick();

        int spentResult = FacehuggerTickWorkflow.processSpentState(
                Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(this)), spentTimer, new FacehuggerTickWorkflow.SpentCallbacks(
                        () -> this.die(Objects.requireNonNull(this.damageSources().generic())),
                        () -> {
                            if (!this.level().isClientSide) {
                                this.discard();
                            }
                        }));
        if (spentResult >= 0) {
            this.spentTimer = spentResult;
            return;
        }

        if (this.pendingTargetUUID != null && !AttachmentRules.isSpentState(this.attachmentState)) {
            FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence.restoreTargetFromUUID(this);
        }

        LivingEntity target = this.getTarget();
        FacehuggerRotationLock.apply(target, this);

        if (target != null && FacehuggerTickWorkflow.shouldDieWithHost(
                Objects.requireNonNull(this.getAttachmentState()), target.isAlive())) {
            FacehuggerTickWorkflow.applyHostDeathReset(this);
            this.die(Objects.requireNonNull(this.damageSources().generic()));
            return;
        }

        if (target != null && target.isAlive()) {
            FacehuggerTickWorkflow.processAttachmentTick(
                    Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(this)),
                    Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(target)));
        }
    }

    @Override
    public void remove(@Nonnull Entity.RemovalReason reason) {
        if (!this.level().isClientSide) {
            AISignalSystem.clearSignalsForEntity(this.getUUID());
        }
        super.remove(reason);
    }

    @Override
    public void addAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.addAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence.writeSaveData(this, compound);
    }

    @Override
    public void readAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.readAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        FacehuggerAttachmentPersistence.readSaveData(this, compound);
        if (!this.level().isClientSide && AttachmentRules.isSpentState(this.attachmentState)) {
            if (FacehuggerSpentTransitionServices.isInitialized()) {
                FacehuggerSpentTransitionServices.spentTransition().resumeSpentWandering(
                        Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(this)));
            } else {
                FacehuggerSpentGoals.registerWanderGoals(this);
            }
        }
    }
}

FILE: OvomorphHatchEffects.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.spawn.SpawnContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ovomorph.OvomorphHatchExecutor;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.config.SoundHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.api.XenomorphTyped;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.hatch.OvomorphHatchConfigAccess;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity.XenomorphSoundRegistry;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.AABB;

/**
 * Hatch spawn side effects for ovomorphs (spawn, sound, removal).
 */
public final class OvomorphHatchEffects {

    private OvomorphHatchEffects() {
    }

    public static void executeHatch(Mob ovomorph, LivingEntity nearestHost) {
        try {
            XenomorphType spawnForm = OvomorphHatchConfigAccess.resolveSpawnForm();
            if (!OvomorphHatchExecutor.canExecuteHatch(spawnForm)) {
                ModLogger.error("OvomorphHatchEffects", "Cannot hatch - no spawn entity configured");
                return;
            }

            double spawnX = ovomorph.getX() + OvomorphHatchConfigAccess.spawnOffsetX();
            double spawnY = ovomorph.getY() + OvomorphHatchConfigAccess.spawnOffsetY();
            double spawnZ = ovomorph.getZ() + OvomorphHatchConfigAccess.spawnOffsetZ();
            float spawnYRot = ovomorph.getYRot();

            boolean spawned = spawnHatchedForm(ovomorph, spawnForm, spawnX, spawnY, spawnZ, spawnYRot);
            if (!spawned) {
                ModLogger.error("OvomorphHatchEffects",
                        "Cannot hatch - failed to spawn form: " + spawnForm.getConfigKey());
                return;
            }

            if (OvomorphHatchExecutor.shouldBindSpawnedHostTarget(
                    spawnForm,
                    nearestHost != null ? BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(nearestHost) : null)) {
                assignFacehuggerTarget(ovomorph.level(), spawnX, spawnY, spawnZ, nearestHost);
            }

            playHatchSound(ovomorph);
            ovomorph.remove(Entity.RemovalReason.DISCARDED);

            ModLogger.info("OvomorphHatchEffects",
                    "Ovomorph hatched into " + spawnForm.getConfigKey() + " at " + ovomorph.blockPosition());
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("OvomorphHatchEffects", "Failed to hatch ovomorph: " + e.getMessage(), e);
        }
    }

    private static boolean spawnHatchedForm(
            Mob ovomorph,
            XenomorphType spawnForm,
            double x,
            double y,
            double z,
            float yRot) {
        Level level = ovomorph.level();
        if (level == null || level.isClientSide()) {
            return false;
        }

        if (!BoundaryServices.isInitialized()) {
            ModLogger.error("OvomorphHatchEffects", "Cannot hatch - BoundaryServices not initialized");
            return false;
        }

        SpawnContext context = SpawnContext.at(
                BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(level),
                x,
                y,
                z,
                yRot,
                0f,
                0f);
        return BoundaryServices.spawn().spawnForm(spawnForm, context);
    }

    private static void assignFacehuggerTarget(
            Level level,
            double spawnX,
            double spawnY,
            double spawnZ,
            LivingEntity nearestHost) {
        if (level == null) {
            return;
        }

        AABB spawnBox = new AABB(
                spawnX - 0.5, spawnY - 0.5, spawnZ - 0.5,
                spawnX + 0.5, spawnY + 0.5, spawnZ + 0.5);
        for (Mob mob : level.getEntitiesOfClass(Mob.class, spawnBox, mob -> mob.isAlive())) {
            if (mob instanceof XenomorphTyped typed
                    && typed.getXenomorphType() == XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER) {
                mob.setTarget(nearestHost);
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    private static void playHatchSound(Mob ovomorph) {
        if (OvomorphHatchConfigAccess.hasHatchSound()) {
            SoundHelper.playAmbientSound(
                    ovomorph,
                    XenomorphType.OVOMORPH,
                    XenomorphSoundRegistry.getAmbientSound(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH));
        }
    }
}

FILE: OvomorphHatchPortAdapter.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ovomorph.OvomorphHatchPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.hatch.OvomorphHatchConfigAccess;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.hatch.OvomorphHatchHost;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.hatch.OvomorphHostQuery;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * NeoForge adapter for {@link OvomorphHatchPort}.
 */
public final class OvomorphHatchPortAdapter implements OvomorphHatchPort {

    private final OvomorphHatchHost host;

    public OvomorphHatchPortAdapter(OvomorphHatchHost host) {
        this.host = host;
    }

    @Override
    public BlockPosRef position() {
        return BoundaryRefs.from(host.mob().blockPosition());
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isProximityRequired() {
        return OvomorphHatchConfigAccess.isProximityRequired();
    }

    @Override
    public int hatchTime() {
        return OvomorphHatchConfigAccess.hatchTime();
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isViableHostNearby() {
        return OvomorphHostQuery.findNearestViableHost(Objects.requireNonNull(host.mob())) != null;
    }

    @Override
    public void cancelHatching() {
        host.setHatching(false);
        host.stopOpeningAnimation();
    }

    @Override
    public void executeHatch() {
        LivingEntity nearestHost = OvomorphHostQuery.findNearestViableHost(Objects.requireNonNull(host.mob()));
        OvomorphHatchEffects.executeHatch(Objects.requireNonNull(host.mob()), nearestHost);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.QueenNestProgress;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity.BaseXenomorphEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity.XenomorphSoundRegistry;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.attributes.AttributeSupplier;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

/**
 * Queen entity — final xenomorph lifecycle stage.
 *
 * <p>NDE: lifecycle is {@link QueenLifecycleAccess} → L4 {@code QueenEmbeddedLifecycle} via reflection.
 * Nest progress is {@link QueenNestProgress} (L5 NestBuildingAI) persisted via {@link QueenNestPersistence}.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 */
public class QueenEntity extends BaseXenomorphEntity {

    private final Object lifecycle;
    private QueenNestProgress nestProgress;

    public final AnimationState movingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState idleAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState standingToCrawlingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState crawlingToStandingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState jumpingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState fallingAnimationState = new AnimationState();

    public int standingToCrawlingStartTick = -1;
    public int crawlingToStandingStartTick = -1;

    public QueenEntity(EntityType<? extends QueenEntity> entityType, Level level) {
        super(entityType, level);
        this.lifecycle = QueenLifecycleAccess.create(this);
    }

    public static AttributeSupplier.Builder createAttributes() {
        return createAttributesForType(XenomorphType.QUEEN);
    }

    @Override
    public XenomorphType getXenomorphType() {
        return XenomorphType.QUEEN;
    }

    @Override
    protected void registerGoals() {
        XenomorphGoalRegistration.registerGoals(this, XenomorphType.QUEEN);
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getAmbientSound() {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getAmbientSound(XenomorphType.QUEEN);
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getHurtSound(@Nonnull DamageSource damageSource) {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getHurtSound(XenomorphType.QUEEN);
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getDeathSound() {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getDeathSound(XenomorphType.QUEEN);
    }

    @Override
    protected void playStepSound(@Nonnull BlockPos pos, @Nonnull BlockState state) {
        XenomorphSoundRegistry.playStepSound(this, XenomorphType.QUEEN);
    }

    @Override
    public void addAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.addAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        QueenNestPersistence.writeSaveData(compound, lifecycle, nestProgress);
    }

    @Override
    public void readAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.readAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        QueenNestPersistence.readSaveData(compound, lifecycle, nestProgress);
    }

    @Override
    public void tick() {
        super.tick();
        QueenLifecycleAccess.tick(lifecycle);
    }

    public boolean hasNest() {
        return QueenNestRegistry.hasNest(getUUID());
    }

    public BlockPos getNestPosition() {
        BlockPosRef ref = QueenNestRegistry.getNestCenter(getUUID());
        return ref != null ? BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(ref) : null;
    }

    public Object getAvoidanceAI() {
        return QueenLifecycleAccess.invokeObject(lifecycle, "getAvoidanceAI");
    }

    public QueenNestProgress getNestProgress() {
        return nestProgress;
    }

    public void setNestProgress(QueenNestProgress nestProgress) {
        this.nestProgress = nestProgress;
    }
}
