package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.specimen_pod;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import java.util.Objects;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.spawn.SpawnContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodSpawnPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodVariant;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.blocks.SpecimenPodBlockEntity;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.network.chat.Component;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;

/**
 * Minecraft-bound specimen pod behavior using {@link SpecimenPodVariant} policy from L2.
 */
public class AbstractSpecimenPodBehavior implements SpecimenPodBehavior {

    private final SpecimenPodVariant variant;

    protected AbstractSpecimenPodBehavior(@Nonnull SpecimenPodVariant variant) {
        this.variant = variant;
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public String getSpecimenType() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(variant.specimenType());
    }

    @Nonnull
    protected String getTranslationPrefix() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(variant.translationPrefix());
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public String getLogPrefix() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(variant.logPrefix());
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public Component getStructureFormedMessage() {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(Component.translatable(getTranslationPrefix() + ".structure_formed"));
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public Component getStatusMessage(@Nonnull SpecimenPodBlockEntity entity) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(Component.translatable(
                getTranslationPrefix() + ".status",
                entity.getStructureSize(), entity.getStructureSize(), entity.getStructureSize(),
                Component.translatable("message.weylandyutani.specimen_pod.contains", entity.getSpecimenType())));
    }

    @Override
    @Nonnull
    public Component getEmptyMessage(@Nonnull SpecimenPodBlockEntity entity) {
        return Objects.requireNonNull(Component.translatable(
                getTranslationPrefix() + ".status",
                entity.getStructureSize(), entity.getStructureSize(), entity.getStructureSize(),
                Component.translatable(getTranslationPrefix() + ".empty")));
    }

    protected boolean spawnSpecimen(@Nonnull SpecimenPodBlockEntity entity, @Nonnull ServerLevel level, @Nonnull BlockPos spawnPos) {
        SpecimenPodSpawnPolicy.SpawnRequest request = new SpecimenPodSpawnPolicy.SpawnRequest(
                getSpecimenType(),
                entity.isFormed(),
                entity.hasSpecimen(),
                SpawnContext.at(
                        BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(level),
                        spawnPos.getX() + 0.5,
                        spawnPos.getY() + 1.0,
                        spawnPos.getZ() + 0.5,
                        0f,
                        0f,
                        -1f));

        if (!BoundaryServices.isInitialized()) {
            return false;
        }
        return SpecimenPodSpawnPolicy.spawnSpecimen(BoundaryServices.spawn(), request);
    }
}

FILE: SpecimenPodPortAdapter.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.specimen_pod;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.lab.SpecimenPodState;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.lab.SpecimenPodBlueprint;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodWorkflow;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.blocks.SpecimenPodBlockEntity;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

/**
 * NeoForge adapter for {@link SpecimenPodPort} — block scans and structure mutation only.
 */
public final class SpecimenPodPortAdapter implements SpecimenPodPort {

    private final SpecimenPodBlockEntity entity;

    public SpecimenPodPortAdapter(SpecimenPodBlockEntity entity) {
        this.entity = entity;
    }

    @Override
    public BlockPosRef controllerPosition() {
        return BoundaryRefs.from(entity.getBlockPos());
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isControllerBlock() {
        return entity.getLevel() != null;
    }

    @Override
    public SpecimenPodState structureState() {
        return entity.getStructureState();
    }

    @Override
    public void setStructureState(SpecimenPodState state) {
        entity.setStructureStateInternal(state);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isFormed() {
        return entity.isFormed();
    }

    @Override
    public int structureSize() {
        return entity.getStructureSize();
    }

    @Override
    public void setStructureSize(int size) {
        entity.setStructureSizeInternal(size);
    }

    @Override
    public List<BlockPosRef> structureBlocks() {
        List<BlockPosRef> refs = new ArrayList<>();
        for (BlockPos pos : entity.getStructureBlocksInternal()) {
            refs.add(BoundaryRefs.from(pos));
        }
        return refs;
    }

    @Override
    public void setStructureBlocks(List<BlockPosRef> blocks) {
        List<BlockPos> positions = new ArrayList<>(blocks.size());
        for (BlockPosRef ref : blocks) {
            positions.add(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(ref));
        }
        entity.setStructureBlocksInternal(positions);
    }

    @Override
    public void clearSpecimenData() {
        entity.clearSpecimenDataInternal();
    }

    @Override
    public void markDirty() {
        entity.setChanged();
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isOccupied(int offsetX, int offsetY, int offsetZ) {
        var level = entity.getLevel();
        if (level == null) {
            return false;
        }
        BlockState state = level.getBlockState(
                Objects.requireNonNull(entity.getBlockPos().offset(offsetX, offsetY, offsetZ)));
        return !state.isAir();
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isControllerAt(BlockPosRef worldPos) {
        var level = entity.getLevel();
        if (level == null) {
            return false;
        }
        return level.getBlockEntity(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(worldPos)))
                instanceof SpecimenPodBlockEntity;
    }

    @Override
    public void destroyBlock(BlockPosRef worldPos) {
        var level = entity.getLevel();
        if (level == null || worldPos == null) {
            return;
        }
        if (BoundaryServices.isInitialized()) {
            boolean broken = BoundaryServices.mutation().breakBlock(
                    BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(level),
                    worldPos,
                    true);
            if (broken) {
                return;
            }
        }
        level.destroyBlock(Objects.requireNonNull(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(worldPos)), true);
    }

    @Override
    public void logDebug(String message) {
        ModLogger.debug("SpecimenPodBlockEntity", message);
    }

    @Override
    public void logInfo(String message) {
        ModLogger.info("SpecimenPod", message);
    }

    @Override
    public void applyValidationResult(SpecimenPodBlueprint.PodValidationResult result) {
        BlockPosRef center = controllerPosition();
        entity.setStructureBlocksInternal(
                toBlockPosList(SpecimenPodWorkflow.offsetsToWorld(center, result.occupiedOffsets())));
        entity.setStructureStateInternal(entity.getStructureState().transitionOnValidate(result.isValid()));
        if (result.isValid()) {
            entity.setStructureCenterInternal(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(center));
            entity.setStructureSizeInternal(result.structureHeight());
            logInfo(result.variant() + " structure formed at " + center);
        }
        markDirty();
    }

    private static List<BlockPos> toBlockPosList(List<BlockPosRef> refs) {
        List<BlockPos> positions = new ArrayList<>(refs.size());
        for (BlockPosRef ref : refs) {
            positions.add(BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(ref));
        }
        return positions;
    }
}

FILE: SurvivalAIGoal.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.ai.shared;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.ai.SurvivalBehaviorRules;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.ai.SurvivalAIConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.ai.SurvivalAIConfigStorage;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NeoForgeEscapeNavigationAdapter;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai.BlockDamageBridge;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.boundary.NeoForgeSuffocationProbe;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.Goal;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;


/**
 * Minecraft implementation of xenomorph survival behavior.
 *
 * Bridges Minecraft entity state into domain survival rules
 * and performs Minecraft-specific escape actions.
 *
 * Responsibilities:
 * - Detect Minecraft suffocation state
 * - Track Minecraft tick state
 * - Execute escape actions
 *
 * Does not contain survival decision rules.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: REFACTORED
 *
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class SurvivalAIGoal extends Goal {

    private static final String AI_NAME = "SurvivalAI";

    private final PathfinderMob entity;
    private final Level level;
    private final SurvivalAIConfig config;

    private int stuckTimer = 0;
    private int escapeCooldown = 0;


    public SurvivalAIGoal(PathfinderMob entity) {
        this.entity = entity;
        this.level = entity.level();
        this.config = SurvivalAIConfigStorage.getConfig();
    }


    @Override
    public boolean canUse() {

        if (!NeoForgeSuffocationProbe.isSuffocating(entity)) {
            return false;
        }

        return SurvivalBehaviorRules.shouldEscapeSuffocation(
                getAirRatio(),
                isStuck(),
                config.suffocationCriticalThreshold,
                config.suffocationLowThreshold);
    }


    @Override
    public boolean canContinueToUse() {

        return NeoForgeSuffocationProbe.isSuffocating(entity)
                && !SurvivalBehaviorRules.isStuck(
                        stuckTimer,
                        config.stuckThresholdTicks);
    }


    @Override
    public void start() {

        ModLogger.info(
                AI_NAME,
                "🚨 Entity suffocating, attempting to move to safety");

        stuckTimer = 0;
    }


    @Override
    public void tick() {

        stuckTimer++;
        escapeCooldown--;

        if (SurvivalBehaviorRules.canAttemptEscape(escapeCooldown)) {

            escapeCooldown =
                    config.escapeAttemptIntervalTicks;

            attemptEscape();
        }
    }


    private void attemptEscape() {

        BlockPos feet = entity.blockPosition();

        BlockDamageBridge.attemptBlockDamage(
                entity,
                level,
                feet);

        BlockDamageBridge.attemptBlockDamage(
                entity,
                level,
                feet.above());

        NeoForgeEscapeNavigationAdapter
                .attemptEscape(entity, level);
    }


    private boolean isStuck() {

        return SurvivalBehaviorRules.isStuck(
                stuckTimer,
                config.stuckThresholdTicks);
    }


    private double getAirRatio() {

        int maxAir = entity.getMaxAirSupply();

        if (maxAir <= 0) {
            return 1.0;
        }

        return (double) entity.getAirSupply() / maxAir;
    }


    @Override
    public void stop() {

        if (!NeoForgeSuffocationProbe.isSuffocating(entity)) {

            ModLogger.info(
                    AI_NAME,
                    "✅ Entity successfully moved to safety");
        }

        stuckTimer = 0;
        escapeCooldown = 0;
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.init;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.core.registries.Registries;
import net.minecraft.world.item.Item;
import net.neoforged.bus.api.IEventBus;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredBlock;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredHolder;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredRegister;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init.BlockGameplayHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init.RegistrationHelper;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.blocks.LabMachineBlock;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.blocks.ResinBlock;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.blocks.SpecimenGlassBlock;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.blocks.SpinyBlock;

/**
 * Registry for all blocks in the mod. Hardness/resistance from block JSON via {@link BlockGameplayHelper}.
 */
public class BlockInit {
    
    public static final DeferredRegister.Blocks BLOCKS = 
        DeferredRegister.createBlocks(ModContext.MOD_ID);
    
    public static final DeferredRegister<Item> ITEMS = 
        DeferredRegister.create(Objects.requireNonNull(Registries.ITEM), ModContext.MOD_ID);
    
    public static final DeferredBlock<LabMachineBlock> LAB_MACHINE = 
        BLOCKS.register("lab_machine",
            () -> new LabMachineBlock(BlockGameplayHelper.labEquipmentProperties("lab_machine")));
    
    public static final DeferredBlock<SpecimenGlassBlock> SPECIMEN_GLASS = 
        BLOCKS.register("specimen_glass",
            () -> new SpecimenGlassBlock(BlockGameplayHelper.glassProperties("specimen_glass")));
    
    public static final DeferredBlock<SpecimenPodControllerBlock> SPECIMEN_POD_CONTROLLER = 
        BLOCKS.register("specimen_pod_controller",
            () -> new SpecimenPodControllerBlock(
                    BlockGameplayHelper.labEquipmentProperties("specimen_pod_controller")));
    
    public static final DeferredBlock<ResinBlock> RESIN_BLOCK = 
        BLOCKS.register("resin_block", () -> new ResinBlock(BlockGameplayHelper.resinProperties()));
    
    public static final DeferredBlock<SpinyBlock> SPINY_BLOCK = 
        BLOCKS.register("spiny_block", () -> new SpinyBlock(BlockGameplayHelper.spinyProperties()));
    
    public static final DeferredBlock<CocoonBlock> COCOON_BLOCK = 
        BLOCKS.register("cocoon_block", () -> new CocoonBlock(BlockGameplayHelper.cocoonProperties()));
    
    public static final DeferredHolder<Item, Item> LAB_MACHINE_ITEM = 
        RegistrationHelper.registerBlockItem(Objects.requireNonNull(ITEMS), "lab_machine", Objects.requireNonNull(LAB_MACHINE));
    
    public static final DeferredHolder<Item, Item> SPECIMEN_GLASS_ITEM = 
        RegistrationHelper.registerBlockItem(Objects.requireNonNull(ITEMS), "specimen_glass", Objects.requireNonNull(SPECIMEN_GLASS));
    
    public static final DeferredHolder<Item, Item> SPECIMEN_POD_CONTROLLER_ITEM = 
        RegistrationHelper.registerBlockItem(Objects.requireNonNull(ITEMS), "specimen_pod_controller", Objects.requireNonNull(SPECIMEN_POD_CONTROLLER));
    
    public static final DeferredHolder<Item, Item> RESIN_BLOCK_ITEM = 
        RegistrationHelper.registerBlockItem(Objects.requireNonNull(ITEMS), "resin_block", Objects.requireNonNull(RESIN_BLOCK));
    
    public static final DeferredHolder<Item, Item> SPINY_BLOCK_ITEM = 
        RegistrationHelper.registerBlockItem(Objects.requireNonNull(ITEMS), "spiny_block", Objects.requireNonNull(SPINY_BLOCK));
    
    public static final DeferredHolder<Item, Item> COCOON_BLOCK_ITEM = 
        RegistrationHelper.registerBlockItem(Objects.requireNonNull(ITEMS), "cocoon_block", Objects.requireNonNull(COCOON_BLOCK));
    
    public static void register(@Nonnull IEventBus modEventBus) {
        BLOCKS.register(modEventBus);
        ITEMS.register(modEventBus);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.init;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.core.registries.Registries;

import net.minecraft.world.item.alchemy.Potion;
import net.neoforged.bus.api.IEventBus;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredHolder;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredRegister;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.init.EffectInit;

/**
 * Registry for custom potions.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class PotionInit {
    
    public static final DeferredRegister<Potion> POTIONS = 
        DeferredRegister.create(Objects.requireNonNull(Registries.POTION), ModContext.MOD_ID);
    
    /**
     * Gestation potion - applies gestation effect to the consumer.
     * Duration is 1200 ticks (60 seconds) for non-players, 3600 ticks (180 seconds) for players.
     * The actual duration is handled by GestationManager which applies the effect with appropriate duration.
     * We use 1200 ticks as the base duration here.
     */
    public static final DeferredHolder<Potion, Potion> GESTATION = 
        POTIONS.register("gestation", registryName -> new Potion(
            new MobEffectInstance(
                Objects.requireNonNull(EffectInit.GESTATION),
                1200,
                0,
                false,
                false,
                true
            )
        ));
    
    /**
     * Registers all potions with the mod event bus.
     * 
     * @param eventBus The mod event bus
     */
    public static void register(@Nonnull IEventBus eventBus) {
        POTIONS.register(eventBus);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.lifecycle;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.host.MobHostRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.registry.ConfigLoaderPriorities;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.registry.ConfigLoaderRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.block.BlockConfigLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.combat.CombatConfigLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.effects.HostEffectConfigLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.host.HostConfigLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.items.MotionTrackerConfigLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.lifecycle.LifecycleConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.lifecycle.MobEntityConfigLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.registry.EffectConfigLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.territory.TerritoryConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_4.entity.EntityConfigLoaderAdapter;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.parasite.SpecializedXenomorphManager;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.config.AIBehaviorConfigLoader;

/**
 * Registers and loads static configuration loaders at mod construction.
 */
public final class ConfigLoaderBootstrap {

    private ConfigLoaderBootstrap() {
    }

    public static void registerConfigLoaders() {
        ModLogger.info("ConfigLoaderBootstrap", "Registering configuration loaders...");
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "EntityConfigLoader",
                EntityConfigLoaderAdapter.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_ENTITY_CONFIG);
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "EffectConfigLoader",
                EffectConfigLoader.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_EFFECT_CONFIG);
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "HostConfigLoader",
                HostConfigLoader.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_HOST_CONFIG);
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "MobEntityConfigLoader",
                MobEntityConfigLoader.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_MOB_ENTITY_CONFIG);
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "BlockConfigLoader",
                BlockConfigLoader.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_BLOCK_CONFIG);
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "HostEffectConfigLoader",
                HostEffectConfigLoader.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_HOST_CONFIG);
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "LifecycleConfig",
                LifecycleConfig.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_DEFAULT);
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "TerritoryConfig",
                TerritoryConfig.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_DEFAULT);
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "CombatConfigLoader",
                CombatConfigLoader.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_DEFAULT);
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "AIBehaviorConfigLoader",
                AIBehaviorConfigLoader.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_AI_BEHAVIOR_CONFIG);
        ConfigLoaderRegistry.registerLoader(
                "MotionTrackerConfigLoader",
                MotionTrackerConfigLoader.getInstance(),
                ConfigLoaderPriorities.PRIORITY_DEFAULT);
        ModLogger.info("ConfigLoaderBootstrap", "All configuration loaders registered");
    }

    public static void loadStaticConfigLoaders() {
        ModLogger.info("ConfigLoaderBootstrap", "Loading static configuration loaders...");
        LifecycleConfig.getInstance().loadConfigs();
        EntityConfigLoaderAdapter.getInstance().loadConfigs();
        EffectConfigLoader.getInstance().loadConfigs();
        HostConfigLoader.getInstance().loadConfigs();
        HostEffectConfigLoader.getInstance().loadConfigs();
        TerritoryConfig.getInstance().loadConfigs();
        CombatConfigLoader.getInstance().loadConfigs();
        MobHostRegistry.initialize();
        MobEntityConfigLoader.getInstance().loadConfigs();
        SpecializedXenomorphManager.initializeFromConfig();
        BlockConfigLoader.getInstance().loadConfigs();
        MotionTrackerConfigLoader.getInstance().loadConfigs();
        ModLogger.info("ConfigLoaderBootstrap", "Static configuration loaders loaded");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.lifecycle;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.registry.SystemLoader;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.config.ConfigLoaderResourceReload;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.config.AIBehaviorConfigLoader;
import net.minecraft.server.packs.resources.ResourceManager;

/**
 * Triggers infrastructure config registry reload via Minecraft ResourceManager.
 */
public final class ConfigReloadAdapter {

    private ConfigReloadAdapter() {
    }

    public static void loadAll(ResourceManager resourceManager) {
        ModLogger.loading("ConfigReloadAdapter: initial load");
        ConfigLoaderResourceReload.loadAllConfigs(resourceManager);
        AIBehaviorConfigLoader.loadBehaviorConfigs(resourceManager);
        SystemLoader.loadSystems();
    }

    public static void reloadAll(ResourceManager resourceManager) {
        ModLogger.loading("ConfigReloadAdapter: reload");
        ConfigLoaderResourceReload.reloadAllConfigs(resourceManager);
        AIBehaviorConfigLoader.reloadBehaviorConfigs(resourceManager);
        SystemLoader.reloadSystems();
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.lifecycle;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.signals.AISignalSystem;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.boundary.BoundaryBootstrap;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.config.AIBehaviorConfigLoader;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.event.server.ServerStartingEvent;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.event.tick.ServerTickEvent;

/**
 * Server lifecycle: boundary ports, periodic systems enablement.
 */
public final class ModServerBootstrap {

    private ModServerBootstrap() {
    }

    public static void onServerStarting(ServerStartingEvent event) {
        BoundaryBootstrap.onServerStarting(event);
        AIBehaviorConfigLoader.loadBehaviorConfigs(event.getServer().getResourceManager());
        ModLogger.info("ModServerBootstrap", "Server starting - xenomorph systems ready");
    }

    public static void onServerTick(ServerTickEvent.Post event) {
        if (event.getServer().getTickCount() % 100 == 0) {
            AISignalSystem.cleanupExpiredSignals(event.getServer().getTickCount());
        }
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.nest;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.territory.QueenTerritory;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.territory.TerritoryManager;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.territory.NestTerritoryFactory;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import java.util.UUID;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;

/**
 * Territory restore / register binding for nest building port.
 */
public final class NestPortTerritoryBinding {

    private NestPortTerritoryBinding() {
    }

    public static BlockPos restoreNestState(
            QueenEntity queen,
            BlockPosRef nestCenter,
            boolean expandingToHive) {
        BlockPos nestPosition = BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(nestCenter);
        UUID queenUUID = queen.getUUID();
        if (NestTerritoryFactory.shouldRegisterMissingTerritory(
                TerritoryManager.getTerritory(queenUUID) != null)) {
            TerritoryManager.registerTerritory(
                    queenUUID,
                    NestTerritoryFactory.createTerritory(
                            nestCenter,
                            expandingToHive,
                            queenUUID,
                            queen.level().getGameTime()));
        }
        return nestPosition;
    }

    public static BlockPos registerTerritory(
            QueenEntity queen,
            BlockPosRef nestPos,
            boolean hiveStage,
            Consumer<BlockPos> nestPositionSink) {
        QueenTerritory territory = NestTerritoryFactory.createTerritory(
                nestPos,
                hiveStage,
                queen.getUUID(),
                queen.level().getGameTime());
        TerritoryManager.registerTerritory(queen.getUUID(), territory);
        BlockPos resolved = BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(nestPos);
        nestPositionSink.accept(resolved);
        return resolved;
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.human;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import com.mojang.blaze3d.vertex.PoseStack;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.human.HumanEntity;

import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.client.model.HumanoidModel;
import net.minecraft.client.model.geom.ModelLayers;
import net.minecraft.client.renderer.entity.EntityRendererProvider;
import net.minecraft.client.renderer.entity.MobRenderer;
import net.minecraft.resources.ResourceLocation;

/**
 * Data-driven renderer for Human entities.
 * Reads model and texture from v1 config.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class HumanRenderer extends MobRenderer<HumanEntity, HumanoidModel<HumanEntity>> {
    
    private final ResourceLocation texture;
    
    public HumanRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context) {
        super(context, new HumanoidModel<>(
                Objects.requireNonNull(context.bakeLayer(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayers.PLAYER)))), 0.5f);
        
        // Read texture from v1 config
        // TODO: Refactor EntityConfigStorage to use EntityType interface instead of XenomorphType
        // For now, bridge to XenomorphType.HUMAN for config access
        var config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(XenomorphType.HUMAN);
        this.texture = ResourceLocation.parse(Objects.requireNonNull(config.texture));
    }
    
    @Override
    public ResourceLocation getTextureLocation(@Nonnull HumanEntity entity) {
        return texture;
    }
    
    @Override
    protected void scale(@Nonnull HumanEntity entity, @Nonnull PoseStack poseStack, float partialTick) {
        // Read scale from v1 config
        // TODO: Refactor EntityConfigStorage to use EntityType interface instead of XenomorphType
        var config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(XenomorphType.HUMAN);
        float scale = config.entitySize.scale;
        poseStack.scale(scale, scale, scale);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.chestburster;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.CommonGoalRegistrar;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai.chestburster.HuntSmallAnimalsGoal;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.ai.chestburster.FleeFromThreatsGoal;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.ai.chestburster.HideInDarkPlacesGoal;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;

/**
 * Registers escape-and-hide goals for chestburster entities from JSON config.
 */
public final class ChestbursterEscapeGoalRegistrar {

    private ChestbursterEscapeGoalRegistrar() {
    }

    public static void registerGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerFloatGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER, "float"));
        double movementSpeedMultiplier = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromMovement(
                aiGoals, "movement_speed_multiplier");
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerStrollGoal(
                entity,
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER, "stroll"),
                aiGoals.strollSpeed * movementSpeedMultiplier);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerRandomLookAroundGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER, "random_look"));

        if (AIConfigHelper.getBoolean(aiGoals.targetSelection, "avoid_all_threats", false)) {
            entity.goalSelector.addGoal(
                    GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER, "flee"),
                    new FleeFromThreatsGoal(entity, aiGoals));
        }
        if (AIConfigHelper.getBoolean(aiGoals.specialAbilities, "eat_small_animals", false)) {
            entity.goalSelector.addGoal(
                    GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER, "hunt"),
                    new HuntSmallAnimalsGoal(entity, aiGoals));
        }
        if (AIConfigHelper.getBoolean(aiGoals.movement, "hide_in_dark_places", false)) {
            entity.goalSelector.addGoal(
                    GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER, "hide"),
                    new HideInDarkPlacesGoal(entity, aiGoals));
        }
    }
}

FILE: PatrolNestGoal.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.drone;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.ConfigCacheHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.territory.DroneTerritoryHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.territory.QueenTerritory;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.NestPatrolHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.DroneEntity;

import java.util.EnumSet;
import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.Goal;

/**
 * AI goal for drone nest patrol behavior.
 * Drones wander within nest territory boundary.
 * Low priority goal (allows other behaviors).
 * Foundation for future host-capturing behavior.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * TODO: Complete nest territory system, add territory validation, improve patrol behavior
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
public class PatrolNestGoal extends Goal {
    
    private final DroneEntity drone;
    private BlockPos nestCenter;
    private int patrolRadius;
    private int patrolTimer = 0;
    private EntityConfig config; // Cached config for data-driven values
    
    public PatrolNestGoal(DroneEntity drone) {
        this.drone = drone;
        this.setFlags(Objects.requireNonNull(EnumSet.of(Flag.MOVE)));
        // Load config once in constructor using centralized cache helper (DRY)
        this.config = ConfigCacheHelper.getConfig(XenomorphType.DRONE);
    }
    
    /**
     * Gets patrol interval from config (data-driven).
     * Uses centralized helper to eliminate repetitive null-check pattern (DRY).
     */
    private int getPatrolInterval() {
        return AIConfigHelper.requireIntFromSpecialAbilities(config, "patrol_interval");
    }
    
    @Override
    public boolean canUse() {
        // Only use this goal if drone can find a nest
        return findNearestNest();
    }
    
    @Override
    public boolean canContinueToUse() {
        // Continue if still near a nest
        return findNearestNest();
    }
    
    @Override
    public void start() {
        // Goal started - begin patrol behavior
        findNearestNest();
        patrolTimer = 0;
    }
    
    @Override
    public void tick() {
        if (nestCenter == null) {
            return;
        }
        
        patrolTimer++;
        
        // Move to a random position within patrol radius every interval (data-driven)
        int interval = getPatrolInterval();
        if (patrolTimer >= interval) {
            // Use centralized helper for random position generation and movement (DRY)
            NestPatrolHelper.moveToRandomPosition(drone, nestCenter, patrolRadius, 1.0);
            ModLogger.debug("PatrolNestGoal", "🔄 Drone moving to random patrol position within radius: " + patrolRadius);
            patrolTimer = 0;
        }
        
        // Check if drone is still within territory bounds using centralized helper (DRY)
        if (!NestPatrolHelper.isWithinRadius(drone, nestCenter, patrolRadius)) {
            // Move back towards nest center using centralized helper (DRY)
            NestPatrolHelper.moveTowardsNest(drone, nestCenter);
            ModLogger.debug("PatrolNestGoal", "🏠 Drone returning to nest center");
        }
    }
    
    @Override
    public void stop() {
        // Goal stopped - patrol behavior ends
        nestCenter = null;
    }
    
    /**
     * Find the nearest nest to patrol.
     * Uses DroneTerritoryHelper for territory queries.
     * 
     * @return true if nest was found
     */
    private boolean findNearestNest() {
        QueenTerritory nearestTerritory = DroneTerritoryHelper.findNearestTerritory(
                BoundaryRefs.from(drone.blockPosition()), 64);

        if (nearestTerritory != null) {
            this.nestCenter = BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(nearestTerritory.getCenterPos());
            this.patrolRadius = nearestTerritory.getRadius();
            return true;
        }
        
        return false;
    }
    
    @Override
    public boolean requiresUpdateEveryTick() {
        return false; // Update every few ticks for performance
    }
}

FILE: FacehuggerAttachmentGoal.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.facehugger;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.ai.AISignalType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.parasite.AttachmentRules;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.ConfigCacheHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.entity.EntityValidationHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.parasite.FacehuggerAttachmentPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.signals.AISignalData;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.signals.AISignalSystem;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_3.parasite.FacehuggerTickWorkflow;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai.SignalAwareGoal;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.HostValidationHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.FacehuggerEntity;

import java.util.EnumSet;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.UUID;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.attributes.Attributes;

/**
 * Thin MC Goal for facehugger approach / attachment: navigation, look, and signal I/O.
 * Activation, claim, and approach FSM decisions live in {@link FacehuggerAttachmentPolicy}.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 */
public class FacehuggerAttachmentGoal extends SignalAwareGoal {

    private final FacehuggerEntity facehugger;
    private AISignalData activeSignal;
    private final EntityConfig config;

    public FacehuggerAttachmentGoal(FacehuggerEntity facehugger) {
        super(facehugger);
        this.facehugger = facehugger;
        this.setFlags(Objects.requireNonNull(EnumSet.of(Flag.MOVE, Flag.LOOK)));
        this.config = ConfigCacheHelper.getConfig(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean canUse() {
        LivingEntity target = this.facehugger.getTarget();

        boolean validTarget = !EntityValidationHelper.isInvalid(
                BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(target), BoundaryServices.entityQuery());
        boolean validHost = validTarget && HostValidationHelper.isValidHostForFacehugger(target);

        if (validTarget && !validHost) {
            ModLogger.info("FacehuggerAttachmentGoal",
                    String.format("🦾 Target %s is not a valid host for facehugging - skipping",
                            Objects.requireNonNull(target).getDisplayName().getString()));
        }

        UUID targetId = validTarget ? Objects.requireNonNull(target).getUUID() : null;
        boolean hostClaimedBySignal = targetId != null && FacehuggerAttachmentPolicy.isHostClaimedBySignal(
                hasSignalForEntity(AISignalType.HOST_TARGETED, targetId),
                hasSignalForEntity(AISignalType.HOST_RESERVED, targetId),
                hasSignalForEntity(AISignalType.HOST_ATTACHED, targetId));

        if (validTarget && hostClaimedBySignal) {
            ModLogger.info("FacehuggerAttachmentGoal",
                    String.format("🦾 Target %s is already targeted/reserved by another facehugger - skipping",
                            Objects.requireNonNull(target).getDisplayName().getString()));
        }

        double configFollowRange = config != null ? config.followRange : 0.0;
        double attributeFollowRange = this.facehugger.getAttribute(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.FOLLOW_RANGE)) != null
                ? this.facehugger.getAttributeValue(Objects.requireNonNull(Attributes.FOLLOW_RANGE))
                : 0.0;
        double followRange = FacehuggerAttachmentPolicy.resolveFollowRange(configFollowRange, attributeFollowRange);
        double distance = validTarget ? this.facehugger.distanceTo(Objects.requireNonNull(target)) : Double.MAX_VALUE;

        return FacehuggerAttachmentPolicy.canActivateAttachment(
                this.facehugger.isSpent(),
                validHost,
                hostClaimedBySignal,
                distance,
                followRange);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean canContinueToUse() {
        LivingEntity target = this.facehugger.getTarget();
        boolean hostInvalid = EntityValidationHelper.isInvalid(
                BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(target), BoundaryServices.entityQuery());

        boolean hostAttachedByOther = false;
        if (!hostInvalid) {
            UUID targetId = Objects.requireNonNull(target).getUUID();
            boolean ownsActive = activeSignal != null
                    && activeSignal.getSourceEntityId().equals(facehugger.getUUID());
            hostAttachedByOther = FacehuggerAttachmentPolicy.isHostAttachedByOther(
                    hasSignalForEntity(AISignalType.HOST_ATTACHED, targetId),
                    ownsActive);
        }

        boolean attachmentInProgress = false;
        if (config != null) {
            int totalDuration = config.attachmentDuration + config.implantationDelay;
            attachmentInProgress = AttachmentRules.isAttachmentInProgress(
                    this.facehugger.getAttachmentTicks(), totalDuration);
        }

        return FacehuggerAttachmentPolicy.shouldContinueAttachment(
                hostInvalid, hostAttachedByOther, attachmentInProgress);
    }

    @Override
    public void start() {
        this.facehugger.setAttachmentTicks(0);
        this.facehugger.getNavigation().stop();

        LivingEntity target = this.facehugger.getTarget();
        if (FacehuggerAttachmentPolicy.shouldBroadcastHostTargeted(
                !EntityValidationHelper.isInvalid(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(target), BoundaryServices.entityQuery()))) {
            LivingEntity broadcastTarget = Objects.requireNonNull(target);
            BlockPos targetPos = broadcastTarget.blockPosition();
            double signalRadius = AIConfigHelper.getDoubleFromMovement(config, "signal_radius", 16.0);
            int signalDuration = AIConfigHelper.getIntFromMovement(config, "signal_duration", 200);

            activeSignal = broadcastSignal(
                    AISignalType.HOST_TARGETED,
                    targetPos,
                    signalRadius,
                    signalDuration);

            if (activeSignal != null) {
                activeSignal.getMetadata().put("targetEntityId", broadcastTarget.getUUID());
                ModLogger.info("FacehuggerAttachmentGoal",
                        String.format("📡 Facehugger %s broadcast HOST_TARGETED signal for %s",
                                this.facehugger.getDisplayName().getString(),
                                broadcastTarget.getDisplayName().getString()));
            }
        }

        ModLogger.info("FacehuggerAttachmentGoal",
                String.format("🦾 Facehugger %s starting attachment goal with target %s",
                        this.facehugger.getDisplayName().getString(),
                        target != null ? target.getDisplayName().getString() : "null"));
    }

    @Override
    public void tick() {
        LivingEntity target = this.facehugger.getTarget();
        if (EntityValidationHelper.isInvalid(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(target), BoundaryServices.entityQuery())) {
            return;
        }
        if (config == null || config.attachmentParameters == null) {
            return;
        }

        LivingEntity attachmentTarget = Objects.requireNonNull(target);
        this.facehugger.getLookControl().setLookAt(
                attachmentTarget, config.attachmentParameters.lookAngle, config.attachmentParameters.lookAngle);

        FacehuggerAttachmentPolicy.ApproachTickDecision decision =
                FacehuggerAttachmentPolicy.resolveApproachTick(
                        Objects.requireNonNull(this.facehugger.getAttachmentState()),
                        this.facehugger.distanceTo(attachmentTarget),
                        config.attachmentParameters.minDistance);

        if (decision.shouldMoveTowardHost()) {
            this.facehugger.getNavigation().moveTo(attachmentTarget, config.attachmentParameters.moveSpeed);
            this.facehugger.setAttachmentState(decision.nextState());
        } else if (decision.shouldStopNavigation()) {
            this.facehugger.getNavigation().stop();
            this.facehugger.setAttachmentState(decision.nextState());
        }
    }

    @Override
    public void stop() {
        if (activeSignal != null) {
            AISignalSystem.clearSignal(activeSignal);
            activeSignal = null;
        }
        FacehuggerTickWorkflow.applyAttachmentGoalCancelled(Objects.requireNonNull(this.facehugger));
    }

    @Override
    public boolean requiresUpdateEveryTick() {
        return true;
    }
}

FILE: HostTargetingGoal.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.facehugger;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.entity.EntityValidationHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.HostValidationHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.FacehuggerEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.target.NearestAttackableTargetGoal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;

/**
 * Host targeting goal for facehuggers that uses the host logic system.
 * Targets entities based on their host type and DNA configuration.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.2
 */
public class HostTargetingGoal extends NearestAttackableTargetGoal<LivingEntity> {
    
    private final FacehuggerEntity facehugger;
    
    public HostTargetingGoal(FacehuggerEntity facehugger) {
        super(facehugger, LivingEntity.class, true);
        this.facehugger = facehugger;
    }
    
    protected boolean canAttack(LivingEntity target) {
        // CRITICAL: Spent facehuggers cannot target new hosts
        if (this.facehugger.isSpent()) {
            ModLogger.debug("HostTargetingGoal", "🦾 HostTargetingGoal: Facehugger is spent - cannot target new hosts");
            return false;
        }
        
        if (EntityValidationHelper.isInvalid(BoundaryRefs.entityFrom(target), BoundaryServices.entityQuery())) {
            ModLogger.debug("HostTargetingGoal", "🦾 HostTargetingGoal: Target is null or dead");
            return false;
        }
        
        // CRITICAL: Creative mode players cannot be targeted
        if (target instanceof Player player && player.getAbilities().instabuild) {
            ModLogger.debug("HostTargetingGoal", 
                String.format("🦾 HostTargetingGoal: Target %s is in creative mode - cannot be targeted", 
                    target.getDisplayName().getString()));
            return false;
        }
        
        // CRITICAL: Use centralized host validation helper
        boolean isValid = HostValidationHelper.isValidHostForFacehugger(target);
        ModLogger.debug("HostTargetingGoal", 
            String.format("🦾 HostTargetingGoal: Target %s is valid host: %s", target.getDisplayName().getString(), isValid));
        return isValid;
    }
    
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.queen;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.EggLayingWorkflow;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.queen.EggLayingConfigAccess;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.ai.queen.EggLayingAreaValidator;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

/**
 * Thin MC wrapper for queen egg laying. Orchestration: {@link EggLayingWorkflow}.
 */
public class EggLayingAI {

    private final QueenEntity queen;
    private final EggLayingConfigAccess configAccess;
    private final EggLayingAreaValidator areaValidator;
    private int eggLayingTimer = 0;

    public EggLayingAI(QueenEntity queen) {
        this.queen = queen;
        this.configAccess = EggLayingConfigAccess.forQueen();
        this.areaValidator = new EggLayingAreaValidator(configAccess);
    }

    public void tick() {
        if (queen.level().isClientSide() || !queen.hasNest()) {
            return;
        }

        EggLayingWorkflow.TickResult result =
                EggLayingWorkflow.advanceTimer(eggLayingTimer, configAccess.getEggLayingInterval());
        eggLayingTimer = result.nextTimer();
        if (result.shouldAttemptLay()) {
            ModLogger.debug("EggLayingAI", "Egg laying timer reached, attempting to lay egg");
            attemptEggLaying();
        }
    }

    private void attemptEggLaying() {
        Level level = queen.level();
        if (!(level instanceof ServerLevel serverLevel)) {
            return;
        }

        BlockPos queenPos = queen.blockPosition();
        if (!areaValidator.canLayEggInArea(serverLevel, queenPos)) {
            ModLogger.info("EggLayingAI", "Cannot lay egg - area too crowded or chunk limit reached");
            return;
        }

        BlockPosRef centerRef = BoundaryRefs.from(queenPos);
        BlockPosRef eggRef = EggLayingWorkflow.findCandidateLocation(
                centerRef, configAccess.limits(), ref -> areaValidator.isSuitableEggLocation(serverLevel, ref));
        if (eggRef == null) {
            ModLogger.info("EggLayingAI", "No suitable location found for egg laying");
            return;
        }

        BlockPos eggPos = new BlockPos(eggRef.x(), eggRef.y(), eggRef.z());
        ModLogger.debug("EggLayingAI", "Laying egg at position: " + eggPos);
        OvomorphSpawnBinding.layEgg(serverLevel, eggPos, queen);
    }
}

FILE: OvomorphSpawnBinding.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.queen;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.spawn.SpawnContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;

/**
 * Spawns ovomorph entities when the queen lays eggs.
 */
public final class OvomorphSpawnBinding {

    private OvomorphSpawnBinding() {
    }

    public static void layEgg(ServerLevel level, BlockPos pos, QueenEntity queen) {
        if (!BoundaryServices.isInitialized()) {
            ModLogger.error("OvomorphSpawnBinding", "Cannot lay egg - BoundaryServices not initialized");
            return;
        }

        SpawnContext context = SpawnContext.at(
                BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(level),
                pos.getX() + 0.5,
                pos.getY(),
                pos.getZ() + 0.5,
                queen.getYRot(),
                queen.getXRot(),
                0f);

        boolean spawned = BoundaryServices.spawn().spawnForm(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH, context);
        if (spawned) {
            ModLogger.info("OvomorphSpawnBinding", "Queen laid an egg at: " + pos);
        } else {
            ModLogger.error("OvomorphSpawnBinding", "Failed to lay egg - spawn port rejected spawn");
        }
    }
}

FILE: QueenAvoidanceAI.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.queen;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.Vec3Ref;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.spatial.QueenAvoidancePolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.ConfigCacheHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.territory.TerritoryConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.queen.QueenProximityQuery;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.boundary.NeoForgePositionSearchAdapter;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;

import java.util.EnumSet;
import java.util.Objects;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.Goal;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.Vec3;

/**
 * Per-queen avoidance state and goal factory. Detection and math delegate to focused types.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: FLUX
 */
public class QueenAvoidanceAI {

    private final QueenEntity queen;
    private QueenEntity nearestOtherQueen;
    private double avoidanceStrength;

    public QueenAvoidanceAI(QueenEntity queen) {
        this.queen = queen;
    }

    public void tick() {
        if (queen.level().isClientSide()) {
            return;
        }
        if (!(queen.level() instanceof ServerLevel serverLevel)) {
            return;
        }

        int minDistance = TerritoryConfig.getMinQueenDistance();
        EntityType<?> queenType = queen.getType();
        var nearest = QueenProximityQuery.findNearest(serverLevel, queen, minDistance, queenType);
        nearestOtherQueen = nearest instanceof QueenEntity queenEntity ? queenEntity : null;

        if (nearestOtherQueen == null) {
            avoidanceStrength = 0.0;
            return;
        }

        double distance = queen.distanceTo(nearestOtherQueen);
        avoidanceStrength = QueenAvoidancePolicy.computeAvoidanceStrength(distance, minDistance);

        if (QueenAvoidancePolicy.shouldLogStrongAvoidance(avoidanceStrength)) {
            ModLogger.info("QueenAvoidanceAI",
                    "Queen avoiding other queen - Distance: " + String.format("%.1f", distance)
                            + " blocks, Strength: " + String.format("%.2f", avoidanceStrength));
        }
    }

    public Goal createGoal() {
        return new QueenAvoidanceGoal();
    }

    public Vec3 getAvoidanceDirection() {
        if (nearestOtherQueen == null || avoidanceStrength <= 0.0) {
            return null;
        }

        Vec3Ref flee = QueenAvoidancePolicy.fleeDirection(
                toRef(queen.position()),
                toRef(nearestOtherQueen.position()),
                avoidanceStrength);
        return toVec3(flee);
    }

    public boolean shouldAvoid() {
        return nearestOtherQueen != null && QueenAvoidancePolicy.shouldFlee(avoidanceStrength);
    }

    public QueenEntity getNearestOtherQueen() {
        return nearestOtherQueen;
    }

    public double getAvoidanceStrength() {
        return avoidanceStrength;
    }

    private static Vec3Ref toRef(Vec3 position) {
        return new Vec3Ref(position.x, position.y, position.z);
    }

    private static Vec3 toVec3(Vec3Ref ref) {
        return new Vec3(ref.x(), ref.y(), ref.z());
    }

    private final class QueenAvoidanceGoal extends Goal {

        private final EntityConfig config = ConfigCacheHelper.getConfig(XenomorphType.QUEEN);

        QueenAvoidanceGoal() {
            setFlags(Objects.requireNonNull(EnumSet.of(Flag.MOVE)));
        }

        @Override
        public boolean canUse() {
            return shouldAvoid();
        }

        @Override
        public boolean canContinueToUse() {
            return shouldAvoid();
        }

        @Override
        public boolean requiresUpdateEveryTick() {
            return true;
        }

        @Override
        public void tick() {
            QueenAvoidanceAI.this.tick();
            Vec3 direction = getAvoidanceDirection();
            if (direction == null) {
                return;
            }

            double distanceMultiplier = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromSpecialAbilities(
                    config, "avoidance_distance_multiplier");
            double speedMultiplier = AIConfigHelper.requireDoubleFromSpecialAbilities(
                    config, "avoidance_speed_multiplier");

            Vec3 fleePos = NeoForgePositionSearchAdapter.searchVec3InRadius(
                    queen,
                    direction,
                    8.0 * distanceMultiplier,
                    10,
                    pos -> queen.level().getBlockState(
                            Objects.requireNonNull(BlockPos.containing(Objects.requireNonNull(pos)))).isAir());

            if (fleePos != null) {
                queen.getNavigation().moveTo(fleePos.x, fleePos.y, fleePos.z, speedMultiplier);
            } else {
                queen.getNavigation().moveTo(
                        queen.getX() + direction.x * distanceMultiplier,
                        queen.getY(),
                        queen.getZ() + direction.z * distanceMultiplier,
                        speedMultiplier);
            }
        }
    }
}

FILE: WanderNearNestGoal.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.queen;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_3.territory.TerritoryConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.territory.QueenNestRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.Goal;
import net.minecraft.world.level.levelgen.Heightmap;
import net.minecraft.world.phys.Vec3;

/**
 * Random stroll constrained to the queen's nest radius.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: FUNCTIONAL
 */
public final class WanderNearNestGoal extends Goal {

    private final QueenEntity queen;
    private int repathCooldown;

    public WanderNearNestGoal(QueenEntity queen) {
        this.queen = queen;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean canUse() {
        return queen.hasNest() && queen.getRandom().nextInt(10) == 0;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean canContinueToUse() {
        return queen.hasNest() && !queen.getNavigation().isDone();
    }

    @Override
    public void start() {
        pickNestWanderTarget();
    }

    @Override
    public void tick() {
        if (--repathCooldown <= 0 && queen.getNavigation().isDone()) {
            pickNestWanderTarget();
        }
    }

    private void pickNestWanderTarget() {
        BlockPosRef centerRef = QueenNestRegistry.getNestCenter(queen.getUUID());
        if (centerRef == null) {
            return;
        }

        BlockPos center = BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(centerRef);
        int radius = TerritoryConfig.getNestRadius();
        double angle = queen.getRandom().nextDouble() * Math.PI * 2.0;
        double distance = queen.getRandom().nextDouble() * radius;
        int targetX = center.getX() + (int) Math.round(Math.cos(angle) * distance);
        int targetZ = center.getZ() + (int) Math.round(Math.sin(angle) * distance);
        int targetY = queen.level().getHeight(
                Heightmap.Types.MOTION_BLOCKING_NO_LEAVES,
                targetX,
                targetZ);

        Vec3 target = new Vec3(targetX + 0.5, targetY, targetZ + 0.5);
        if (queen.getNavigation().moveTo(target.x, target.y, target.z, 0.6D)) {
            repathCooldown = 40;
        }
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.shared;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.XenomorphTargetRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.ChestbursterEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.DroneEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.FacehuggerEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.GrowthEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.PraetorEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * Registers xenomorph entity types as targets for human entities.
 * This bridges the gap between human AI (which needs to target xenomorphs)
 * and xenomorph entities (which are in a different package).
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: NEW
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8
 */
public class XenomorphTargetRegistration {
    
    /**
     * Registers all xenomorph entity types as targets.
     * Should be called during mod initialization.
     */
    public static void registerXenomorphTargets() {
        // Register xenomorph entities as targets for humans
        // Priority order: facehuggers first (most dangerous), then others
        XenomorphTargetRegistry.registerTarget(new XenomorphTargetRegistry.XenomorphTargetProvider() {
            @Override
            @Nonnull
            public Class<? extends LivingEntity> getTargetClass() {
                return FacehuggerEntity.class;
            }
            
            @Override
            public int getPriority() {
                return 2; // High priority - facehuggers are most dangerous
            }
        });
        
        XenomorphTargetRegistry.registerTarget(new XenomorphTargetRegistry.XenomorphTargetProvider() {
            @Override
            @Nonnull
            public Class<? extends LivingEntity> getTargetClass() {
                return ChestbursterEntity.class;
            }
            
            @Override
            public int getPriority() {
                return 3;
            }
        });
        
        XenomorphTargetRegistry.registerTarget(new XenomorphTargetRegistry.XenomorphTargetProvider() {
            @Override
            @Nonnull
            public Class<? extends LivingEntity> getTargetClass() {
                return DroneEntity.class;
            }
            
            @Override
            public int getPriority() {
                return 4;
            }
        });
        
        XenomorphTargetRegistry.registerTarget(new XenomorphTargetRegistry.XenomorphTargetProvider() {
            @Override
            @Nonnull
            public Class<? extends LivingEntity> getTargetClass() {
                return PraetorEntity.class;
            }
            
            @Override
            public int getPriority() {
                return 5;
            }
        });
        
        XenomorphTargetRegistry.registerTarget(new XenomorphTargetRegistry.XenomorphTargetProvider() {
            @Override
            @Nonnull
            public Class<? extends LivingEntity> getTargetClass() {
                return QueenEntity.class;
            }
            
            @Override
            public int getPriority() {
                return 6;
            }
        });
        
        XenomorphTargetRegistry.registerTarget(new XenomorphTargetRegistry.XenomorphTargetProvider() {
            @Override
            @Nonnull
            public Class<? extends LivingEntity> getTargetClass() {
                return GrowthEntity.class;
            }
            
            @Override
            public int getPriority() {
                return 7;
            }
        });
    }
}

/**
 * Render-time animation binding for chestburster geo models.
 */
public final class ChestbursterModelAnimationSetup implements XenomorphModelAnimationSetup {

    public static final ChestbursterModelAnimationSetup INSTANCE = new ChestbursterModelAnimationSetup();

    private ChestbursterModelAnimationSetup() {
    }

    @Override
    public <T extends LivingEntity> void setupAnimations(
            @Nonnull T entity,
            @Nonnull HierarchicalModel<T> model,
            @Nonnull AnimationCaller animator,
            float ageInTicks) {
        if (!(entity instanceof ChestbursterEntity chestburster)) {
            return;
        }

        resetPose(model);

        if (chestburster.serpentineAnimationState.isStarted()) {
            animator.animate(chestburster.serpentineAnimationState, ChestbursterModelAnimation.serpentine, ageInTicks);
        }
    }
}

    public static final DroneModelAnimationSetup INSTANCE = new DroneModelAnimationSetup();

    private DroneModelAnimationSetup() {
    }

    public <T extends LivingEntity> void setupAnimations(

            @Nonnull HierarchicalModel<T> model,
            @Nonnull AnimationCaller animator,

                XenomorphType.DRONE,
                5.0F,

                        DroneModelAnimation.crawling_to_standing,
                        DroneModelAnimation.crawl_pose,
                        DroneModelAnimation.idle_standing));
    }

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.client.animation.state;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.ChestbursterEntity;

/**
 * Handles all animation state updates for Chestburster entities.
 * Triggers serpentine animation when chestburster is moving.
 *
 * <p>FILE STATUS: PLANNED — serpentine/jump/fall wired; polish deferred to client slice.
 */
public final class ChestbursterAnimationStateHandler {
    
    // TODO: CRITICAL - Missing transition animations. Entities instant-switch between standing (idle) and crawling (movement) poses. Need smooth transition animations between states (stand-to-crawl, crawl-to-stand).
    // TODO: Create hiding animation (curled up, defensive) - needed for hiding behavior
    // TODO: Create maturation animation (growing, transforming) - needed for maturation visual feedback
    // TODO: Create hunting animation (stalking, attacking) - needed for hunting behavior
    
    public static void updateAnimationState(ChestbursterEntity entity) {
        // Detect jump/fall states (highest priority)
        boolean isJumping = !entity.onGround() && entity.getDeltaMovement().y > 0.0D;
        boolean isFalling = !entity.onGround() && entity.getDeltaMovement().y <= 0.0D;
        boolean isMoving = entity.getDeltaMovement().horizontalDistanceSqr() > 1.0E-6D;
        
        // Priority: jumping/falling > movement > idle
        if (isJumping) {
            // Entity is jumping - play jump animation (will use default pose if animation doesn't exist)
            if (!entity.jumpingAnimationState.isStarted()) {
                entity.jumpingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
            entity.fallingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.serpentineAnimationState.stop();
            return;
        }
        
        if (isFalling) {
            // Entity is falling - play fall animation (will use default pose if animation doesn't exist)
            if (!entity.fallingAnimationState.isStarted()) {
                entity.fallingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
            entity.jumpingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.serpentineAnimationState.stop();
            return;
        }
        
        // Not jumping or falling - stop jump/fall animations
        entity.jumpingAnimationState.stop();
        entity.fallingAnimationState.stop();
        
        // Trigger serpentine animation based on horizontal movement
        if (isMoving) {
            // Start serpentine animation if not already running
            if (!entity.serpentineAnimationState.isStarted()) {
                entity.serpentineAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
        } else {
            // Stop serpentine animation if standing still
            entity.serpentineAnimationState.stop();
        }
    }
}

FILE: DroneAnimationStateHandler.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.client.animation.state;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.client.animation.AnimationTransitionHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.DroneEntity;

/**
 * Handles all animation state updates for Drone entities.
 *
 * <p>FILE STATUS: PLANNED — deferred client slice; wire from entity client tick when animation stack is enabled.
 */
public final class DroneAnimationStateHandler {
    
    // TODO: Create running animation (fast, aggressive) - needed for chase/combat behavior
    // TODO: Create attacking animation (claw swipes, tail strikes) - needed for melee attack behavior
    // TODO: Create nesting animation (curled up, resting) - needed for rest/patrol behavior
    
    public static void updateAnimationState(DroneEntity entity) {
        boolean isMoving = entity.getDeltaMovement().horizontalDistanceSqr() > 1.0E-6D;
        boolean isTransitioningToCrawl = entity.standingToCrawlingAnimationState.isStarted();
        boolean isTransitioningToStand = entity.crawlingToStandingAnimationState.isStarted();
        boolean isWalking = entity.walkingAnimationState.isStarted();
        boolean isIdle = entity.idleAnimationState.isStarted();
        
        // Detect jump/fall states (highest priority)
        boolean isJumping = !entity.onGround() && entity.getDeltaMovement().y > 0.0D;
        boolean isFalling = !entity.onGround() && entity.getDeltaMovement().y <= 0.0D;
        
        // Get transition duration from config (per-entity configurable)
        int transitionDuration = AnimationTransitionHelper.getTransitionDuration(entity, XenomorphType.DRONE);
        
        // Priority: jumping/falling > transitions > movement > idle
        if (isJumping) {
            // Entity is jumping - play jump animation (will use default pose if animation doesn't exist)
            if (!entity.jumpingAnimationState.isStarted()) {
                entity.jumpingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
            // Stop other animations
            entity.fallingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.walkingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
            entity.standingToCrawlingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.crawlingToStandingAnimationState.stop();
            return;
        }
        
        if (isFalling) {
            // Entity is falling - play fall animation (will use default pose if animation doesn't exist)
            if (!entity.fallingAnimationState.isStarted()) {
                entity.fallingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
            // Stop other animations
            entity.jumpingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.walkingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
            entity.standingToCrawlingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.crawlingToStandingAnimationState.stop();
            return;
        }
        
        // Not jumping or falling - stop jump/fall animations
        entity.jumpingAnimationState.stop();
        entity.fallingAnimationState.stop();
        
        // CRITICAL: Let transitions complete even if movement state changes
        // Check if a transition is in progress and let it finish
        if (isTransitioningToCrawl) {
            // Transition to crawl is in progress - let it complete
            if (entity.standingToCrawlingStartTick >= 0 && 
                entity.tickCount - entity.standingToCrawlingStartTick >= transitionDuration) {
                // Transition complete
                entity.standingToCrawlingAnimationState.stop();
                entity.standingToCrawlingStartTick = -1;
                // Start appropriate animation based on current movement state
                if (isMoving) {
                    entity.walkingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
                } else {
                    // Movement stopped during transition - go to idle in crawl pose
                    entity.idleAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
                }
            }
            // Keep other animations stopped while transitioning
            entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
            entity.crawlingToStandingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.crawlingToStandingStartTick = -1;
            return; // Don't process other logic while transition is in progress
        }
        
        if (isTransitioningToStand) {
            // Transition to stand is in progress - let it complete
            if (entity.crawlingToStandingStartTick >= 0 && 
                entity.tickCount - entity.crawlingToStandingStartTick >= transitionDuration) {
                // Transition complete
                entity.crawlingToStandingAnimationState.stop();
                entity.crawlingToStandingStartTick = -1;
                // Always go to idle when transition to stand completes
                entity.idleAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
            // Keep other animations stopped while transitioning
            entity.walkingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.standingToCrawlingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.standingToCrawlingStartTick = -1;
            return; // Don't process other logic while transition is in progress
        }
        
        // No transitions in progress - handle normal state
        if (isMoving) {
            // Entity is moving - should be in crawl pose
            if (!isWalking) {
                // Not walking yet - start transition to crawl if currently in stand pose (idle)
                if (isIdle) {
                    // Currently idle (standing) - need to transition to crawl
                    entity.standingToCrawlingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
                    entity.standingToCrawlingStartTick = entity.tickCount;
                    entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
                    entity.walkingAnimationState.stop();
                } else {
                    // Not idle and not walking - just start walking animation (already in crawl pose)
                    entity.walkingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
                    entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
                }
            }
        } else {
            // Entity is not moving - should be in stand pose with idle animation
            if (!isIdle) {
                // Not idle yet - start transition to stand if currently in crawl pose (walking)
                if (isWalking) {
                    // Currently walking (in crawl pose) - need to transition to stand
                    entity.crawlingToStandingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
                    entity.crawlingToStandingStartTick = entity.tickCount;
                    entity.walkingAnimationState.stop();
                } else {
                    // Not walking and not idle - just start idle animation (already in stand pose)
                    entity.idleAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
