FILE: FacehuggerAnimationStateHandler.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.client.animation.state;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.parasite.AttachmentState;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.FacehuggerEntity;

/**
 * Handles all animation state updates for Facehugger entities.
 * Triggers animations based on state: attachment (highest priority) > walking > idle.
 *
 * <p>FILE STATUS: PLANNED — idle/walk/attach wired; transition/leap/implantation animations deferred (L3-CARRY-03).
 */
public final class FacehuggerAnimationStateHandler {
    
    // TODO: CRITICAL - Missing transition animations. Entities instant-switch between standing (idle) and crawling (movement) poses. Need smooth transition animations between states (stand-to-crawl, crawl-to-stand).
    // TODO: Create jumping/leaping animation - needed for FacehuggerLeapGoal behavior
    // TODO: Create attachment animation (wrapping around face) - animation handler exists but attachmentState not set in startAttachment()
    // TODO: Create implantation animation (tail insertion) - needed for implantation phase
    
    public static void updateAnimationState(FacehuggerEntity entity) {
        AttachmentState attachmentState = entity.getAttachmentState();
        boolean isAttaching = attachmentState == AttachmentState.ATTACHING || attachmentState == AttachmentState.ATTACHED;
        boolean isMoving = entity.getDeltaMovement().horizontalDistanceSqr() > 1.0E-6D;
        
        // Detect jump/fall states (highest priority after attachment)
        boolean isJumping = !entity.onGround() && entity.getDeltaMovement().y > 0.0D;
        boolean isFalling = !entity.onGround() && entity.getDeltaMovement().y <= 0.0D;
        
        // Priority: attachment > jumping/falling > walking > idle
        if (isAttaching) {
            // Play attachment animation
            if (!entity.attachmentAnimationState.isStarted()) {
                entity.attachmentAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
            entity.jumpingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.fallingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.walkAnimationState.stop();
            entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
        } else if (isJumping) {
            // Entity is jumping - play jump animation (will use default pose if animation doesn't exist)
            if (!entity.jumpingAnimationState.isStarted()) {
                entity.jumpingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
            entity.fallingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.attachmentAnimationState.stop();
            entity.walkAnimationState.stop();
            entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
        } else if (isFalling) {
            // Entity is falling - play fall animation (will use default pose if animation doesn't exist)
            if (!entity.fallingAnimationState.isStarted()) {
                entity.fallingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
            entity.jumpingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.attachmentAnimationState.stop();
            entity.walkAnimationState.stop();
            entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
        } else if (isMoving) {
            // Not jumping or falling - stop jump/fall animations
            entity.jumpingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.fallingAnimationState.stop();
            // Play walking animation
            if (!entity.walkAnimationState.isStarted()) {
                entity.walkAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
            entity.attachmentAnimationState.stop();
            entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
        } else {
            // Not jumping or falling - stop jump/fall animations
            entity.jumpingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.fallingAnimationState.stop();
            // Play idle animation
            if (!entity.idleAnimationState.isStarted()) {
                entity.idleAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
            entity.attachmentAnimationState.stop();
            entity.walkAnimationState.stop();
        }
    }
}

    // TODO: Create enrage animation (crown extension, roaring) - needed for enrage mode

    public static void updateAnimationState(QueenEntity entity) {

        boolean isTransitioningToCrawl = entity.standingToCrawlingAnimationState.isStarted();
        boolean isTransitioningToStand = entity.crawlingToStandingAnimationState.isStarted();

        boolean isIdle = entity.idleAnimationState.isStarted();

            entity.movingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
            entity.standingToCrawlingAnimationState.stop();

            // Entity is falling - play fall animation (will use default pose if animation doesn't exist)

            entity.jumpingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.movingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
            entity.standingToCrawlingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.crawlingToStandingAnimationState.stop();
            return;

                entity.tickCount - entity.standingToCrawlingStartTick >= transitionDuration) {
                // Transition complete
                entity.standingToCrawlingAnimationState.stop();
                entity.standingToCrawlingStartTick = -1;

                    entity.movingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);

                }

            entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
            entity.crawlingToStandingAnimationState.stop();
            entity.crawlingToStandingStartTick = -1;

                entity.crawlingToStandingStartTick = -1;

        if (isMoving) {
            // Entity is moving - should be in crawl pose
            if (!isMovingAnim) {
                // Not moving yet - start transition to crawl if currently in stand pose (idle)
                if (isIdle) {

                    entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
                    entity.movingAnimationState.stop();
                } else {

                }
            }
        } else {

FILE: OvomorphHatchSession.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ovomorph.OvomorphHatchPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ovomorph.OvomorphHatchWorkflow;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.hatch.OvomorphHatchHost;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphHatchPortAdapter;

/**
 * Per-egg hatch workflow session: timer state + port-driven tick progression.
 */
public final class OvomorphHatchSession {

    private final OvomorphHatchHost host;
    private final OvomorphHatchPort hatchPort;
    private final OvomorphHatchWorkflow.State workflowState = new OvomorphHatchWorkflow.State();

    public OvomorphHatchSession(OvomorphHatchHost host) {
        this.host = host;
        this.hatchPort = new OvomorphHatchPortAdapter(host);
    }

    public OvomorphHatchWorkflow.State workflowState() {
        return workflowState;
    }

    public void startHatching(int tickCount) {
        if (!host.isHatching()) {
            host.setHatching(true);
            OvomorphHatchWorkflow.onHatchingStarted(hatchPort, workflowState);
            host.startOpeningAnimation(tickCount);
            ModLogger.info("OvomorphHatchSession",
                    "Ovomorph started hatching at " + host.mob().blockPosition());
        }
    }

    public void processTick(int tickCount) {
        if (host.isHatching()) {
            OvomorphHatchWorkflow.processTick(hatchPort, workflowState, tickCount);
        }
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.blocks;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.core.registries.Registries;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntityType;
import net.neoforged.bus.api.IEventBus;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredHolder;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.registries.DeferredRegister;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks.BlockEntityTypeHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.blocks.SpecimenPodBlockEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.blocks.entity.SpecimenPodBlockEntityTypeRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.init.BlockInit;

/**
 * Registry for all block entities in the mod.
 *
 * <p>Specimen pod factory wiring is invoked from {@code DeferredRegisterBootstrap} before
 * {@link #register(IEventBus)} so {@link SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration} is ready.
 */
public class ModBlockEntities {

    public static final DeferredRegister<BlockEntityType<?>> BLOCK_ENTITIES =
        DeferredRegister.create(Objects.requireNonNull(Registries.BLOCK_ENTITY_TYPE), ModContext.MOD_ID);

    public static final DeferredHolder<BlockEntityType<?>, BlockEntityType<SpecimenPodBlockEntity>> SPECIMEN_POD_CONTROLLER =
        BLOCK_ENTITIES.register("specimen_pod_controller",
            registryName -> createSpecimenPodControllerType());

    private static BlockEntityType<SpecimenPodBlockEntity> createSpecimenPodControllerType() {
        BlockEntityType.Builder<SpecimenPodBlockEntity> builder = Objects.requireNonNull(BlockEntityType.Builder.of(
                (pos, state) -> (SpecimenPodBlockEntity) SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration.create(pos, state),
                Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.SPECIMEN_POD_CONTROLLER.get(), "specimen_pod_controller")
        ));
        BlockEntityType<SpecimenPodBlockEntity> type = BlockEntityTypeHelper.buildWithoutDatafixer(builder);
        SpecimenPodBlockEntityTypeRegistry.register(() -> type);
        return type;
    }

    public static void register(@Nonnull IEventBus modEventBus) {
        BLOCK_ENTITIES.register(Objects.requireNonNull(modEventBus));
    }
}

     * Registers all items with the mod event bus.
     * 
     * @param eventBus The mod event bus
     */
    public static void register(@Nonnull IEventBus eventBus) {
        ITEMS.register(Objects.requireNonNull(eventBus));
        
        // Xenomorph spawn eggs are now registered directly through ItemInit.ITEMS
        // No separate registration needed
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.lifecycle;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.lifecycle.ConfigReloadAdapter;
import java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture;
import java.util.concurrent.Executor;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.minecraft.server.packs.resources.PreparableReloadListener;
import net.minecraft.server.packs.resources.ResourceManager;
import net.minecraft.util.profiling.ProfilerFiller;

/**
 * Minecraft reload listener that refreshes mod configuration and systems.
 */
public final class ConfigReloadListener implements PreparableReloadListener {

    private static final @Nonnull Object NO_PREP_DATA = new Object();

    public static final @Nonnull ConfigReloadListener INSTANCE = new ConfigReloadListener();

    private ConfigReloadListener() {
    }

    @Override
    public CompletableFuture<Void> reload(
            @Nonnull PreparationBarrier barrier,
            @Nonnull ResourceManager resourceManager,
            @Nonnull ProfilerFiller preparationsProfiler,
            @Nonnull ProfilerFiller reloadProfiler,
            @Nonnull Executor backgroundExecutor,
            @Nonnull Executor gameExecutor) {
        return barrier.wait(NO_PREP_DATA).thenRunAsync(
                () -> ConfigReloadAdapter.reloadAll(resourceManager),
                gameExecutor);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.nest;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.NestingConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.NestBlockScanHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.init.BlockInit;

import java.util.Objects;

/**
 * Structure presence / progress probes for nest building port.
 */
public final class NestPortStructureProbe {

    private NestPortStructureProbe() {
    }

    public static boolean hasNestStructureNearby(QueenEntity queen) {
        int scanRadius = NestingConfigHelper.resolveScanRadius(XenomorphType.QUEEN);
        return NestBlockScanHelper.hasNestBlocksNearby(
                Objects.requireNonNull(queen.level()),
                Objects.requireNonNull(queen.blockPosition()),
                Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.RESIN_BLOCK.get()),
                Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.SPINY_BLOCK.get()),
                Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.COCOON_BLOCK.get()),
                scanRadius);
    }

    public static int detectedNestStructureProgress(QueenEntity queen) {
        int scanRadius = NestingConfigHelper.resolveScanRadius(XenomorphType.QUEEN);
        return NestBlockScanHelper.detectNestProgress(
                Objects.requireNonNull(queen.level()),
                Objects.requireNonNull(queen.blockPosition()),
                Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.RESIN_BLOCK.get()),
                Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.SPINY_BLOCK.get()),
                scanRadius);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.human;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.init.EntityInitRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.renderer.RendererRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.human.HumanEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.human.HumanRenderer;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.client.event.EntityRenderersEvent;

/**
 * Human-specific renderer registry.
 * Registers all human entity renderers.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: NEW
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.8
 */
public class HumanRendererRegistry implements RendererRegistry {
    
    @Override
    public void registerRenderers(EntityRenderersEvent.RegisterRenderers event) {
        ModLogger.info("HumanRendererRegistry", "Loading human renderers...");
        
        int registeredCount = 0;
        int failedCount = 0;
        
        // Register human renderers
        try {
            @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
            EntityType<HumanEntity> humanType = (EntityType<HumanEntity>) EntityInitRefs.holder("HUMAN").get();
            event.registerEntityRenderer(Objects.requireNonNull(humanType), HumanRenderer::new);
            ModLogger.debug("HumanRendererRegistry", "✅ Registered Human renderer");
            registeredCount++;
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("HumanRendererRegistry", "Failed to register Human renderer: " + e.getMessage());
            failedCount++;
        }
        
        if (failedCount > 0) {
            ModLogger.warn("HumanRendererRegistry", 
                String.format("⚠️ Human renderer registration completed with %d successful and %d failed registrations", 
                    registeredCount, failedCount));
        } else {
            ModLogger.info("HumanRendererRegistry", 
                String.format("✅ All human renderers loaded successfully (%d renderers)", registeredCount));
        }
    }
    
    @Override
    public String getSpeciesName() {
        return "human";
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.ai.chestburster;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.AIGoalConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.AICompositionStrategy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.ChestbursterEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.ai.shared.SurvivalAIGoal;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.chestburster.ChestbursterEscapeGoalRegistrar;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Chestburster goal composition via {@link AICompositionStrategy}.
 */
public final class ChestbursterCompositionStrategy implements AICompositionStrategy {

    private static final ChestbursterCompositionStrategy INSTANCE = new ChestbursterCompositionStrategy();

    public static void registerGoals(ChestbursterEntity chestburster) {
        INSTANCE.applyGoals(chestburster);
    }

    public static int getMaturationTime() {
        return AIGoalConfigHelper.getMaturationTime(XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER);
    }

    @Override
    public void applyGoals(Mob mob) {
        if (!(mob instanceof ChestbursterEntity chestburster)) {
            return;
        }
        EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER);
        if (config != null && config.aiGoals != null) {
            ChestbursterEscapeGoalRegistrar.registerGoals(chestburster, config.aiGoals);
        }
        chestburster.goalSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER, "survival"),
                new SurvivalAIGoal(chestburster));
    }

    @Override
    public String strategyName() {
        return "chestburster";
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.ai.drone;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.AIGoalConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.ConfigCacheHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.AICompositionStrategy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.StandardTargetingHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.ai.drone.DroneSwarmGoalRegistrar;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.DroneEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.ai.shared.SurvivalAIGoal;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.drone.PatrolNestGoal;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Drone goal composition via {@link AICompositionStrategy}.
 * Owns swarm + targeting registration for drone (no parallel BehaviorFactory path).
 */
public final class DroneCompositionStrategy implements AICompositionStrategy {

    private static final DroneCompositionStrategy INSTANCE = new DroneCompositionStrategy();

    public static void registerGoals(DroneEntity drone) {
        INSTANCE.applyGoals(drone);
    }

    public static int getMaturationTime() {
        return AIGoalConfigHelper.getMaturationTime(XenomorphType.DRONE);
    }

    @Override
    public void applyGoals(Mob mob) {
        if (!(mob instanceof DroneEntity drone)) {
            return;
        }
        drone.goalSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.DRONE, "survival"), new SurvivalAIGoal(drone));
        drone.goalSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.DRONE, "patrol"), new PatrolNestGoal(drone));

        EntityConfig config = ConfigCacheHelper.getConfig(XenomorphType.DRONE);
        if (config != null && config.aiGoals != null) {
            DroneSwarmGoalRegistrar.registerGoals(drone, config.aiGoals);
        }

        StandardTargetingHelper.registerStandardTargetingGoals(drone, XenomorphType.DRONE);
    }

    @Override
    public String strategyName() {
        return "drone";
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.ai.facehugger;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.AIGoalConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.ConfigCacheHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.AICompositionStrategy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.CommonGoalRegistrar;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.FacehuggerEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.facehugger.FacehuggerAttachmentGoal;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.facehugger.HostTargetingGoal;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Facehugger goal composition via {@link AICompositionStrategy}.
 */
public final class FacehuggerCompositionStrategy implements AICompositionStrategy {

    private static final FacehuggerCompositionStrategy INSTANCE = new FacehuggerCompositionStrategy();

    public static void registerGoals(FacehuggerEntity facehugger) {
        INSTANCE.applyGoals(facehugger);
    }

    public static int getAttachmentDuration() {
        return AIGoalConfigHelper.getAttachmentDuration(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);
    }

    @Override
    public void applyGoals(Mob mob) {
        if (!(mob instanceof FacehuggerEntity facehugger)) {
            return;
        }
        ModLogger.info("FacehuggerCompositionStrategy",
                "🤖 Applying facehugger composition for " + facehugger.getDisplayName().getString());

        EntityConfig config = ConfigCacheHelper.getConfig(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);

        double strollSpeed = config.aiGoals.basicMovement != null && config.aiGoals.basicMovement.strollSpeed != null
                ? config.aiGoals.basicMovement.strollSpeed : 1.0;
        float lookRange = config.aiGoals.basicMovement != null && config.aiGoals.basicMovement.lookAtPlayerRange != null
                ? config.aiGoals.basicMovement.lookAtPlayerRange.floatValue() : 32.0f;

        int floatPriority = GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER, "float");
        int attachmentPriority = GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER, "attachment");
        int strollPriority = GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER, "stroll");
        int lookPriority = GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER, "look_at_player");
        int randomLookPriority = GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER, "random_look");

        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerFloatGoal(facehugger, floatPriority);
        facehugger.goalSelector.addGoal(attachmentPriority, new FacehuggerAttachmentGoal(facehugger));
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerStrollGoal(facehugger, strollPriority, strollSpeed);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerLookAtPlayerGoal(facehugger, lookPriority, lookRange);
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerRandomLookAroundGoal(facehugger, randomLookPriority);

        facehugger.targetSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER, "host_target"),
                new HostTargetingGoal(facehugger));
    }

    @Override
    public String strategyName() {
        return "facehugger";
    }
}

	@Override
	public ModelPart root() {
		return this.facehugger;
	}

	@Override
	public void setupAnim(@Nonnull T entity, float limbSwing, float limbSwingAmount, float ageInTicks, float netHeadYaw, float headPitch) {
		// Delegate to entity-specific animation helper for all animation logic
		// Pass this::animate to allow helper to call the protected animate method
		FacehuggerModelAnimationSetup.INSTANCE.setupAnimations(entity, this, this::animate, ageInTicks);
	}

	@Override
	public void renderToBuffer(@Nonnull PoseStack poseStack, @Nonnull VertexConsumer vertexConsumer, int packedLight, int packedOverlay, int color) {
		facehugger.render(poseStack, vertexConsumer, packedLight, packedOverlay);
	}
}

		PartDefinition left_foot_base = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(left_foot, "left_foot_base", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(0, 0).addBox(-1.0F, -0.25F, -2.5F, 2.0F, 0.5F, 2.5F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, 0.0F, 0.0F));

		PartDefinition left_toes = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(left_foot, "left_toes", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(0, 0).addBox(-1.0F, -0.25F, -2.0F, 2.0F, 0.5F, 2.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, 0.0F, -2.5F));

		PartDefinition right_leg = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(legs, "right_leg", ModelDefinitionHelper.cube(), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(-2.0F, 0.0F, 0.0F));

		PartDefinition right_thigh = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(right_leg, "right_thigh", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(0, 0).mirror().addBox(-1.0F, 0.0F, -1.0F, 2.0F, 6.0F, 2.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F)).mirror(false)), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, 0.0F, 0.0F));

		PartDefinition right_lower_leg = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(right_leg, "right_lower_leg", ModelDefinitionHelper.cube(), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, 6.0F, 0.0F));

		PartDefinition right_calf = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(right_lower_leg, "right_calf", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(1, 1).addBox(-1.0F, 0.0F, -0.75F, 2.0F, 6.0F, 1.5F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, 0.0F, 0.0F));

		PartDefinition right_foot = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(right_lower_leg, "right_foot", ModelDefinitionHelper.cube(), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, 5.75F, -0.5F));

		PartDefinition right_foot_base = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(right_foot, "right_foot_base", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(0, 0).mirror().addBox(-1.0F, -0.25F, -2.5F, 2.0F, 0.5F, 2.5F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F)).mirror(false)), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, 0.0F, 0.0F));

		PartDefinition right_toes = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(right_foot, "right_toes", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(0, 0).mirror().addBox(-1.0F, -0.25F, -2.0F, 2.0F, 0.5F, 2.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F)).mirror(false)), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, 0.0F, -2.5F));

		return ModelDefinitionHelper.layer(meshdefinition, 16, 16);
	}

	@Override
	public ModelPart root() {
		return this.root;
	}

	@Override
	public void setupAnim(@Nonnull T entity, float limbSwing, float limbSwingAmount, float ageInTicks, float netHeadYaw, float headPitch) {
		// Delegate to entity-specific animation helper for all animation logic
		// Pass this::animate to allow helper to call the protected animate method
		QueenModelAnimationSetup.INSTANCE.setupAnimations(entity, this, this::animate, ageInTicks);
	}

	@Override
	public void renderToBuffer(@Nonnull PoseStack poseStack, @Nonnull VertexConsumer vertexConsumer, int packedLight, int packedOverlay, int color) {
		xenomorph_queen.render(poseStack, vertexConsumer, packedLight, packedOverlay);
	}
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.entity;

import java.util.Objects;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.nbt.CompoundTag;
import net.minecraft.network.syncher.EntityDataAccessor;
import net.minecraft.network.syncher.EntityDataSerializers;
import net.minecraft.network.syncher.SynchedEntityData;
import net.minecraft.sounds.SoundEvent;
import net.minecraft.world.damagesource.DamageSource;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.AnimationState;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.EntityType;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.attributes.AttributeSupplier;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ovomorph.OvomorphDamageHatchPolicy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.XenomorphGoalRegistration;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.entity.EntityAttributeHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.api.XenomorphTyped;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphFixedRotation;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphGroundSnap;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphHatchPersistence;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.hatch.OvomorphHatchHost;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.entity.XenomorphSoundRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphHatchPortAdapter;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphHatchSession;

/**
 * Ovomorph entity — stationary egg that hatches when disturbed.
 *
 * <p>Hatch: {@link OvomorphHatchHost} + {@link OvomorphHatchSession} + {@link OvomorphHatchPortAdapter}.
 */
public class OvomorphEntity extends PathfinderMob implements XenomorphTyped, OvomorphHatchHost {

    private static final EntityDataAccessor<Boolean> DATA_IS_HATCHING = Objects.requireNonNull(
            SynchedEntityData.defineId(
                    OvomorphEntity.class,
                    Objects.requireNonNull(EntityDataSerializers.BOOLEAN)));

    private final OvomorphHatchSession hatchSession = new OvomorphHatchSession(this);
    private final OvomorphFixedRotation fixedRotation = new OvomorphFixedRotation();

    public final AnimationState openingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState closingAnimationState = new AnimationState();
    public final AnimationState idleAnimationState = new AnimationState();

    public OvomorphEntity(EntityType<? extends OvomorphEntity> entityType, Level level) {
        super(entityType, level);
        this.setNoGravity(true);
        this.setInvulnerable(true);
        this.setPersistenceRequired();
    }

    public static AttributeSupplier.Builder createAttributes() {
        return EntityAttributeHelper.createXenomorphAttributes(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH);
    }

    @Override
    protected void defineSynchedData(@Nonnull SynchedEntityData.Builder builder) {
        super.defineSynchedData(builder);
        builder.define(Objects.requireNonNull(DATA_IS_HATCHING), false);
    }

    @Override
    public XenomorphType getXenomorphType() {
        return XenomorphType.OVOMORPH;
    }

    @Override
    protected void registerGoals() {
        XenomorphGoalRegistration.registerGoals(this, XenomorphType.OVOMORPH);
    }

    @Override
    public void tick() {
        super.tick();

        if (!fixedRotation.isInitialized()) {
            fixedRotation.captureInitialRotation(this.getYRot(), this.getXRot());
        }

        if (!this.isPersistenceRequired()) {
            this.setPersistenceRequired();
        }

        OvomorphGroundSnap.apply(this);
        hatchSession.processTick(this.tickCount);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean removeWhenFarAway(double distanceToClosestPlayer) {
        return false;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean requiresCustomPersistence() {
        return true;
    }

    @Override
    public PathfinderMob mob() {
        return this;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isHatching() {
        return getEntityData().get(Objects.requireNonNull(DATA_IS_HATCHING));
    }

    @Override
    public void setHatching(boolean hatching) {
        getEntityData().set(Objects.requireNonNull(DATA_IS_HATCHING), hatching);
    }

    @Override
    public void startOpeningAnimation(int tickCount) {
        openingAnimationState.startIfStopped(tickCount);
    }

    @Override
    public void stopOpeningAnimation() {
        openingAnimationState.stop();
    }

    public AnimationState getOpeningAnimationState() {
        return openingAnimationState;
    }

    public void startHatching() {
        hatchSession.startHatching(this.tickCount);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean hurt(@Nonnull DamageSource source, float amount) {
        if (OvomorphDamageHatchPolicy.shouldStartHatch(source)) {
            if (!isHatching()) {
                startHatching();
            }
        } else {
            ModLogger.debug("OvomorphEntity",
                    "Ignoring indirect damage from " + source.getMsgId() + " - not starting hatching");
        }
        return true;
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getAmbientSound() {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getAmbientSound(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH);
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getHurtSound(@Nonnull DamageSource damageSource) {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getHurtSound(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH);
    }

    @Override
    protected SoundEvent getDeathSound() {
        return XenomorphSoundRegistry.getDeathSound(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH);
    }

    @Override
    public void setYRot(float yRot) {
        if (!fixedRotation.isInitialized()) {
            super.setYRot(yRot);
            fixedRotation.seedYRot(yRot);
        } else {
            super.setYRot(fixedRotation.resolveYRot(yRot));
        }
    }

    @Override
    public void setXRot(float xRot) {
        if (!fixedRotation.isInitialized()) {
            super.setXRot(xRot);
            fixedRotation.seedXRot(xRot);
        } else {
            super.setXRot(fixedRotation.resolveXRot(xRot));
        }
    }

    @Override
    public void lookAt(@Nonnull Entity entity, float maxYawIncrement, float maxPitchIncrement) {
        fixedRotation.lookAt(entity, maxYawIncrement, maxPitchIncrement);
    }

    @Override
    public void push(@Nonnull Entity entity) {
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isPushable() {
        return false;
    }

    @Override
    protected void playStepSound(@Nonnull BlockPos pos, @Nonnull BlockState state) {
    }

    @Override
    public void addAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.addAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        OvomorphHatchPersistence.writeSaveData(
                compound,
                Objects.requireNonNull(hatchSession.workflowState()),
                isHatching());
    }

    @Override
    public void readAdditionalSaveData(@Nonnull CompoundTag compound) {
        super.readAdditionalSaveData(compound);
        setHatching(OvomorphHatchPersistence.readSaveData(
                compound,
                Objects.requireNonNull(hatchSession.workflowState())));
    }
}

FILE: QueenEmbeddedLifecycle.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.entity;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.territory.QueenNestRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.queen.EggLayingAI;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.queen.QueenAvoidanceAI;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;

/**
 * Server-side queen lifecycle at L4 so L3 AI types remain importable without same-tier edges.
 *
 * <p><b>Lifecycle split (Option A):</b>
 * <ul>
 *   <li>This object owns {@link QueenAvoidanceAI} and {@link EggLayingAI} (ticked from {@link #tick()}).</li>
 *   <li>Nest building is owned by L7 {@code NestBuildingAI} on {@code QueenEntity#setNestProgress}
 *       ({@link com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.QueenNestProgress});
 *       {@link #getNestBuildingAI()} on lifecycle remains unused.</li>
 *   <li>{@link #restoreNestState} restores {@code QueenNestRegistry} only; workflow progress is
 *       restored via {@code QueenNestPersistence} into the typed nest progress port.</li>
 * </ul>
 *
 * <p>Stub progress accessors ({@link #getBuildingProgress}, {@link #getHiveBuildingProgress},
 * {@link #isExpandingToHive}) are legacy; {@code QueenEntity} NBT now reads live values from
 * {@code QueenNestProgress} when present.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: FLUX
 */
public final class QueenEmbeddedLifecycle {

    private final QueenEntity queen;
    private final QueenAvoidanceAI avoidanceAI;
    private final EggLayingAI eggLayingAI;

    public QueenEmbeddedLifecycle(QueenEntity queen) {
        this.queen = queen;
        this.avoidanceAI = new QueenAvoidanceAI(queen);
        this.eggLayingAI = new EggLayingAI(queen);
    }

    public void tick() {
        avoidanceAI.tick();
        eggLayingAI.tick();
    }

    public QueenAvoidanceAI getAvoidanceAI() {
        return avoidanceAI;
    }

    public Object getNestBuildingAI() {
        return null;
    }

    public boolean hasNest() {
        return QueenNestRegistry.hasNest(queen.getUUID());
    }

    public BlockPos getNestPosition() {
        BlockPosRef ref = QueenNestRegistry.getNestCenter(queen.getUUID());
        return ref != null ? BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(ref) : null;
    }

    public int getBuildingProgress() {
        return 0;
    }

    public int getHiveBuildingProgress() {
        return 0;
    }

    public boolean isExpandingToHive() {
        return false;
    }

    public void restoreNestState(
            BlockPos nestPos,
            int buildingProgress,
            int hiveBuildingProgress,
            boolean isExpandingToHive) {
        if (nestPos == null) {
            return;
        }
        QueenNestRegistry.registerNest(queen.getUUID(), BoundaryRefs.from(nestPos));
    }
}

PACKAGE: level_4/species/xenomorph/structure

FILE: NestStructureGenerator.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.structure;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.queen.NestBlueprint;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.WorldRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.NestLayoutPlanner;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.init.BlockInit;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Random;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.core.registries.BuiltInRegistries;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.Blocks;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

/**
 * MC executor for nest structure placement.
 * Layout planning: {@link NestLayoutPlanner}; rules: {@link NestBlueprint} (domain).
 */
public class NestStructureGenerator {

    public static boolean buildNestPhase(ServerLevel level, BlockPos centerPos, int phase) {
        try {
            List<NestLayoutPlanner.PlacementIntent> intents =
                    NestLayoutPlanner.planPhase(phase, NestLayoutPlanner.getHiveStructureSize(), new Random());
            if (intents.isEmpty()) {
                ModLogger.warn("NestStructureGenerator", "Unknown building phase: " + phase);
                return false;
            }
            return executePlan(level, centerPos, intents);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("NestStructureGenerator", "Failed to build nest phase " + phase + ": " + e.getMessage());
            return false;
        }
    }

    private static boolean executePlan(
            ServerLevel level,
            BlockPos centerPos,
            List<NestLayoutPlanner.PlacementIntent> intents) {
        Map<NestLayoutPlanner.BlockKind, List<BlockPos>> grouped = new EnumMap<>(NestLayoutPlanner.BlockKind.class);

        for (NestLayoutPlanner.PlacementIntent intent : intents) {
            NestLayoutPlanner.BlockOffset offset = intent.offset();
            BlockPos pos = Objects.requireNonNull(centerPos.offset(offset.x(), offset.y(), offset.z()));

            if (intent.blockKind() == NestLayoutPlanner.BlockKind.AIR_ENTRANCE) {
                if (level.getBlockState(pos).getBlock() == Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.RESIN_BLOCK.get())) {
                    grouped.computeIfAbsent(NestLayoutPlanner.BlockKind.AIR_ENTRANCE, k -> new ArrayList<>()).add(pos);
                }
                continue;
            }

            if (canPlaceBlockAt(level, pos)) {
                grouped.computeIfAbsent(intent.blockKind(), k -> new ArrayList<>()).add(pos);
            }
        }

        boolean anyPlaced = false;
        for (var entry : grouped.entrySet()) {
            if (!entry.getValue().isEmpty()) {
                anyPlaced |= placeBlocks(level, entry.getValue(), blockStateForKind(entry.getKey()));
            }
        }
        return anyPlaced;
    }

    private static BlockState blockStateForKind(NestLayoutPlanner.BlockKind kind) {
        return switch (kind) {
            case RESIN -> Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.RESIN_BLOCK.get()).defaultBlockState();
            case SPINY -> Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.SPINY_BLOCK.get()).defaultBlockState();
            case COCOON -> Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.COCOON_BLOCK.get()).defaultBlockState();
            case AIR_ENTRANCE -> Blocks.AIR.defaultBlockState();
        };
    }

    private static boolean placeBlocks(ServerLevel level, List<BlockPos> positions, BlockState blockState) {
        boolean success = true;
        WorldRef worldRef = BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(level);
        String blockId = Objects.requireNonNull(
                BuiltInRegistries.BLOCK.getKey(Objects.requireNonNull(blockState.getBlock()))).toString();
        boolean usePort = BoundaryServices.isInitialized();

        for (BlockPos pos : positions) {
            try {
                BlockPosRef posRef = BoundaryRefs.from(pos);
                if (usePort) {
                    if (!BoundaryServices.mutation().placeBlock(worldRef, posRef, blockId)) {
                        success = false;
                    }
                } else {
                    level.setBlock(Objects.requireNonNull(pos), Objects.requireNonNull(blockState), 3);
                }
            } catch (Exception e) {
                ModLogger.warn("NestStructureGenerator", "Failed to place block at " + pos + ": " + e.getMessage());
                success = false;
            }
        }

        if (success) {
            ModLogger.info("NestStructureGenerator", "Placed " + positions.size() + " blocks");
        }

        return success;
    }

    public static int getTotalPhases() {
        return NestLayoutPlanner.getTotalPhases();
    }

    public static int getHiveStructureSize() {
        return NestLayoutPlanner.getHiveStructureSize();
    }

    private static boolean canPlaceBlockAt(ServerLevel level, BlockPos pos) {
        BlockPos checkPos = Objects.requireNonNull(pos);
        if (!level.isInWorldBounds(checkPos)) {
            return false;
        }

        BlockState currentState = level.getBlockState(checkPos);

        if (currentState.getBlock() == Blocks.BEDROCK || currentState.getBlock() == Blocks.BARRIER) {
            return false;
        }

        return true;
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.specimen_pod;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodVariant;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.blocks.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodBlockView;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.blocks.SpecimenPodBlockEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.blocks.entity.SpecimenPodBlockEntityTypeRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodPortAdapter;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.specimen_pod.SpecimenPodBehaviors;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.entity.BlockEntity;
import net.minecraft.world.level.block.state.BlockState;

/**
 * Wires L2 block entity construction and L3 port adapter from L5 registration tier.
 */
public final class SpecimenPodBlockEntityBootstrap {

    private SpecimenPodBlockEntityBootstrap() {
    }

    public static void wire() {
        SpecimenPodBehaviors.forVariant(Objects.requireNonNull(SpecimenPodVariant.GENERIC));
        ModLogger.info("SpecimenPodBlockEntityBootstrap", "Specimen pod behavior factory verified");
        SpecimenPodBlockEntityRegistration.register(
                SpecimenPodBlockEntityBootstrap::createEntity,
                SpecimenPodBlockEntityBootstrap::tick);
    }

    public static SpecimenPodBlockEntity createEntity(BlockPos pos, BlockState state) {
        SpecimenPodBlockEntity entity = new SpecimenPodBlockEntity(
                SpecimenPodBlockEntityTypeRegistry.get(), pos, state);
        SpecimenPodPort port = new SpecimenPodPortAdapter(entity);
        entity.bindPort(port);
        return entity;
    }

    private static void tick(Level level, BlockPos pos, BlockState state, BlockEntity be) {
        if (be instanceof SpecimenPodBlockView view) {
            SpecimenPodBlockEntity.tick(level, pos, state, view);
        }
    }
}

PACKAGE: level_5/ai

FILE: HatchWhenPlayerNearbyGoal.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_5.ai;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.GlassLineOfSightHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.PlayerValidationHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphEntity;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.ai.goal.Goal;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

/**
 * Triggers ovomorph hatching when a survival-mode player is detected with line of sight.
 */
public final class HatchWhenPlayerNearbyGoal extends Goal {

    private final PathfinderMob entity;
    private final double detectionRange;

    public HatchWhenPlayerNearbyGoal(PathfinderMob entity, double range) {
        this.entity = entity;
        this.detectionRange = range;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean canUse() {
        if (entity instanceof OvomorphEntity ovomorph) {
            return !ovomorph.isHatching() && hasPlayerInDirectSight();
        }
        return false;
    }

    private boolean hasPlayerInDirectSight() {
        Level level = entity.level();
        if (level == null) {
            return false;
        }
        Player nearestPlayer = level.getNearestPlayer(Objects.requireNonNull(entity), detectionRange);
        if (nearestPlayer == null) {
            return false;
        }
        if (PlayerValidationHelper.isCreativeMode(nearestPlayer)) {
            return false;
        }
        if (!entity.hasLineOfSight(nearestPlayer)) {
            return false;
        }
        return GlassLineOfSightHelper.hasClearPathWithoutGlass(entity, nearestPlayer);
    }

    @Override
    public void start() {
        if (entity instanceof OvomorphEntity ovomorph) {
            ovomorph.startHatching();
            ModLogger.debug("HatchWhenPlayerNearbyGoal", "Player detected! Starting hatching process...");
        }
    }

    @Override
    public boolean canContinueToUse() {
        return false;
    }

FILE: OvomorphAnimationStateHandler.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_5.client;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphEntity;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.network.chat.Component;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.player.Player;
import net.minecraft.world.level.Level;

/**
 * Handles all animation state updates for Ovomorph entities.
 *
 * <p>FILE STATUS: PLANNED — hatch open/close wired; polish deferred to client slice.
 */
public final class OvomorphAnimationStateHandler {

    private OvomorphAnimationStateHandler() {
    }

    public static void updateAnimationState(OvomorphEntity entity) {
        boolean isHatching = entity.isHatching();
        boolean isOpeningStarted = entity.openingAnimationState.isStarted();
        boolean isClosingStarted = entity.closingAnimationState.isStarted();
        boolean isIdleStarted = entity.idleAnimationState.isStarted();

        if (isHatching) {
            if (!isOpeningStarted) {
                ModLogger.info("OvomorphAnimationStateHandler",
                    String.format("🥚 Starting ovomorph opening animation (tick: %d, hatching: true)", entity.tickCount));
                entity.openingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
                if (isClosingStarted) {
                    entity.closingAnimationState.stop();
                }
                if (isIdleStarted) {
                    entity.idleAnimationState.stop();
                }

                Level level = entity.level();
                if (level != null && !level.isClientSide()) {
                    level.getEntitiesOfClass(Player.class, Objects.requireNonNull(entity.getBoundingBox().inflate(32)))
                            .forEach(player ->
                                    player.displayClientMessage(
                                            Objects.requireNonNull(Component.literal("🥚 Ovomorph animation started!")), true));
                }
            }
        } else {
            if (isOpeningStarted) {
                ModLogger.info("OvomorphAnimationStateHandler", "🥚 Stopping ovomorph opening animation, starting closing animation");
                entity.openingAnimationState.stop();
                entity.closingAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            } else if (!isClosingStarted && !isIdleStarted) {
                entity.idleAnimationState.start(entity.tickCount);
            }
        }
    }
}

import com.mojang.blaze3d.vertex.PoseStack;

/**
 * Model class for ovomorph entity.
 * Fully functional with animations.
 * 
 * FILE STATUS: STABLE
 * 
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.3
 */
@SuppressWarnings("unused")
public class OvomorphModel<T extends OvomorphEntity> extends HierarchicalModel<T> {
	// This layer location should be baked with EntityRendererProvider.Context in the entity renderer and passed into this model's constructor
	public static final ModelLayerLocation LAYER_LOCATION = ModelDefinitionHelper.layerLocation(ModContext.MOD_ID, "ovomorphmodel");
	private final ModelPart root;
	private final ModelPart ovomorph;
	private final ModelPart flaps;
	private final ModelPart flap1;
	private final ModelPart flap2;
	private final ModelPart flap3;
	private final ModelPart flap4;
	private final ModelPart main_body;

	public OvomorphModel(ModelPart root) {
		this.root = root;
		this.ovomorph = root.getChild("ovomorph");
		this.flaps = this.ovomorph.getChild("flaps");
		this.flap1 = this.flaps.getChild("flap1");
		this.flap2 = this.flaps.getChild("flap2");
		this.flap3 = this.flaps.getChild("flap3");
		this.flap4 = this.flaps.getChild("flap4");
		this.main_body = this.ovomorph.getChild("main_body");
	}

	public static LayerDefinition createBodyLayer() {
		MeshDefinition meshdefinition = new MeshDefinition();
		PartDefinition partdefinition = ModelDefinitionHelper.root(meshdefinition);

		PartDefinition ovomorph = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(partdefinition, "ovomorph", ModelDefinitionHelper.cube(), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, 19.375F, 0.0F));

		PartDefinition flaps = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(ovomorph, "flaps", ModelDefinitionHelper.cube(), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, 3.625F, 0.0F));

		PartDefinition flap1 = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(flaps, "flap1", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(0, 0).addBox(0.0F, -2.0F, -5.0F, 5.0F, 2.0F, 5.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(-5.0F, -17.0F, 5.0F));

		PartDefinition flap2 = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(flaps, "flap2", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(0, 0).mirror().addBox(-5.0F, -2.0F, -5.0F, 5.0F, 2.0F, 5.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F)).mirror(false)), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(5.0F, -17.0F, 5.0F));

		PartDefinition flap3 = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(flaps, "flap3", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(0, 0).mirror().addBox(-5.0F, -2.0F, 0.0F, 5.0F, 2.0F, 5.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F)).mirror(false)), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(5.0F, -17.0F, -5.0F));

		PartDefinition flap4 = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(flaps, "flap4", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(0, 0).addBox(0.0F, -2.0F, 0.0F, 5.0F, 2.0F, 5.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(-5.0F, -17.0F, -5.0F));

		PartDefinition main_body = ModelDefinitionHelper.child(ovomorph, "main_body", ModelDefinitionHelper.boxed(ModelDefinitionHelper.cube().texOffs(0, 0).addBox(-5.0F, -9.75F, -5.0F, 10.0F, 2.0F, 10.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))
		.texOffs(0, 0).addBox(-6.0F, -5.75F, -6.0F, 12.0F, 2.0F, 12.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))
		.texOffs(0, 0).addBox(-6.0F, -7.75F, -6.0F, 12.0F, 2.0F, 12.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))
		.texOffs(0, 0).addBox(-7.0F, 0.25F, -7.0F, 14.0F, 4.0F, 14.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))
		.texOffs(0, 0).addBox(-7.0F, -3.75F, -7.0F, 14.0F, 4.0F, 14.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))
		.texOffs(0, 0).addBox(-6.0F, 4.25F, -6.0F, 12.0F, 2.0F, 12.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))
		.texOffs(0, 0).addBox(-5.0F, 7.25F, -5.0F, 10.0F, 1.0F, 10.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))
		.texOffs(0, 0).addBox(-5.0F, 6.25F, -5.0F, 10.0F, 1.0F, 10.0F, ModelDefinitionHelper.deformation(0.0F))), ModelDefinitionHelper.offset(0.0F, -3.625F, 0.0F));

		return ModelDefinitionHelper.layer(meshdefinition, 16, 16);
	}

	@Override
	public ModelPart root() {
		return this.root;
	}

	@Override
	public void setupAnim(@Nonnull T entity, float limbSwing, float limbSwingAmount, float ageInTicks, float netHeadYaw, float headPitch) {
		OvomorphModelAnimationSetup.INSTANCE.setupAnimations(entity, this, this::animate, ageInTicks);
	}

	@Override
	public void renderToBuffer(@Nonnull PoseStack poseStack, @Nonnull VertexConsumer vertexConsumer, int packedLight, int packedOverlay, int color) {
		ovomorph.render(poseStack, vertexConsumer, packedLight, packedOverlay, color);
	}
}

FILE: OvomorphModelAnimationSetup.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_5.client;

import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.model.AnimationCaller;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.model.OvomorphModelAnimation;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.xenomorph.client.model.XenomorphModelAnimationSetup;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphEntity;
import net.minecraft.client.model.HierarchicalModel;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.LivingEntity;

/**
 * Render-time animation binding for ovomorph geo models.
 */
public final class OvomorphModelAnimationSetup implements XenomorphModelAnimationSetup {

    public static final OvomorphModelAnimationSetup INSTANCE = new OvomorphModelAnimationSetup();

    private OvomorphModelAnimationSetup() {
    }

    @Override
    public <T extends LivingEntity> void setupAnimations(
            @Nonnull T entity,
            @Nonnull HierarchicalModel<T> model,
            @Nonnull AnimationCaller animator,
            float ageInTicks) {
        if (!(entity instanceof OvomorphEntity ovomorph)) {
            return;
        }

        resetPose(model);

        if (ovomorph.openingAnimationState.isStarted()) {
            animator.animate(ovomorph.openingAnimationState, OvomorphModelAnimation.opening, ageInTicks);
        } else if (ovomorph.closingAnimationState.isStarted()) {
            animator.animate(ovomorph.closingAnimationState, OvomorphModelAnimation.closing, ageInTicks);
        } else if (ovomorph.idleAnimationState.isStarted()) {
            animator.animate(ovomorph.idleAnimationState, OvomorphModelAnimation.idle, ageInTicks);
        }
    }
}

FILE: RendererLoader.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_5.client;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;

import net.neoforged.api.distmarker.Dist;
import net.neoforged.bus.api.SubscribeEvent;
import net.neoforged.fml.common.EventBusSubscriber;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.client.event.EntityRenderersEvent;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.species.common.renderer.RendererRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.client.XenomorphRendererRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.human.HumanRendererRegistry;

/**
 * Centralized renderer loading system.
 * Uses registry pattern to allow species-specific renderers to register themselves.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: FLUX
 * This file coordinates multiple renderer registries and will change as new species are added.
 *
 * Renderer registries are registered via static initialization to ensure they're available
 * before EntityRenderersEvent.RegisterRenderers fires (which can occur during resource reload).
 *
 * @author WeylandYutaniCorp
 * @since 0.1.0
 */
@EventBusSubscriber(modid = ModContext.MOD_ID, value = Dist.CLIENT)
public class RendererLoader {

    private static final List<RendererRegistry> REGISTRIES = new ArrayList<>();

    static {
        try {
            registerRegistry(new XenomorphRendererRegistry());
            registerRegistry(new HumanRendererRegistry());
            ModLogger.debug("RendererLoader", "Renderer registries initialized via static block");
        } catch (Exception e) {
            ModLogger.error("RendererLoader", "Failed to initialize renderer registries: " + e.getMessage(), e);
        }
    }

    public static void registerRegistry(@Nonnull RendererRegistry registry) {
        REGISTRIES.add(registry);
        ModLogger.debug("RendererLoader", "Registered renderer registry: " + registry.getSpeciesName());
    }

    @SubscribeEvent
    public static void registerRenderers(@Nonnull EntityRenderersEvent.RegisterRenderers event) {
        ModLogger.info("RendererLoader", "Loading renderers from " + REGISTRIES.size() + " registries...");

        int totalRegistered = 0;
        int totalFailed = 0;

        for (RendererRegistry registry : REGISTRIES) {
            try {
                ModLogger.debug("RendererLoader", "Registering renderers for: " + registry.getSpeciesName());
                registry.registerRenderers(event);
                totalRegistered++;
            } catch (Exception e) {
                ModLogger.error("RendererLoader",
                        "Failed to register renderers for " + registry.getSpeciesName() + ": " + e.getMessage());
                totalFailed++;
            }
        }

        if (totalFailed > 0) {
            ModLogger.warn("RendererLoader",
                    String.format("Renderer registration completed with %d successful and %d failed registries",
                            totalRegistered, totalFailed));
        } else {
            ModLogger.info("RendererLoader",
                    String.format("All renderer registries loaded successfully (%d registries)", totalRegistered));
        }
    }
}

                        Objects.requireNonNull(ItemInit.OVOMORPH_SPAWN_EGG)
                )));

        CreativeTabHelper.addItemsToTab(event, Objects.requireNonNull(event.getTabKey()), Objects.requireNonNull(CreativeModeTabs.FOOD_AND_DRINKS),
                Objects.requireNonNull(Arrays.asList(
                        Objects.requireNonNull(ItemInit.GESTATION_POTION),
                        Objects.requireNonNull(ItemInit.GESTATION_SPLASH_POTION)
                )));

        CreativeTabHelper.addItemToTab(event, Objects.requireNonNull(event.getTabKey()), Objects.requireNonNull(CreativeModeTabs.TOOLS_AND_UTILITIES),
                Objects.requireNonNull(ItemInit.MOTION_TRACKER));

        CreativeTabHelper.addItemsToTab(event, Objects.requireNonNull(event.getTabKey()), Objects.requireNonNull(CreativeModeTabs.BUILDING_BLOCKS),
                Objects.requireNonNull(Arrays.asList(
                        Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.LAB_MACHINE_ITEM),
                        Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.SPECIMEN_GLASS_ITEM),
                        Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.SPECIMEN_POD_CONTROLLER_ITEM),
                        Objects.requireNonNull(BlockInit.RESIN_BLOCK_ITEM),

import net.minecraft.client.renderer.entity.EntityRendererProvider;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Xenomorph-specific data-driven renderer.
 *
 * <p>NDE escape hatch: loaded by L4 {@code XenomorphRendererRegistry} via
 * {@code Class.forName} on inner classes ({@code XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer$*}) so the L4
 * registry stays at {@code level_4} without compile-time L3 imports.
 *
 * FILE STATUS: FLUX
 */
public class XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer<T extends Mob> extends BaseDataDrivenRenderer<T> {

    public XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context, XenomorphType entityType) {
        this(context, entityType,
                XenomorphModelRegistryFactory.create(),
                new XenomorphTextureRegistry(),
                new XenomorphEntityTypeResolver(),
                new XenomorphRenderConfigProvider());
    }

    protected XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context,
                                          EntityType entityType,
                                          ModelRegistry modelRegistry,
                                          TextureRegistry textureRegistry,
                                          EntityTypeResolver entityTypeResolver,
                                          RenderConfigProvider configProvider) {
        super(context, entityType, modelRegistry, textureRegistry, entityTypeResolver, configProvider);
    }

    public static final class FacehuggerRenderer extends XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer<FacehuggerEntity> {
        public FacehuggerRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context) {
            super(context, XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);
        }
    }

    public static final class ChestbursterRenderer extends XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer<ChestbursterEntity> {
        public ChestbursterRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context) {
            super(context, XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER);
        }
    }

    public static final class DroneRenderer extends XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer<DroneEntity> {
        public DroneRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context) {
            super(context, XenomorphType.DRONE);
        }
    }

    public static final class GrowthRenderer extends XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer<GrowthEntity> {
        public GrowthRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context) {
            super(context, XenomorphType.GROWTH);
        }
    }

    public static final class PraetorRenderer extends XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer<PraetorEntity> {
        public PraetorRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context) {
            super(context, XenomorphType.PRAETOR);
        }
    }

    public static final class QueenRenderer extends XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer<QueenEntity> {
        public QueenRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context) {
            super(context, XenomorphType.QUEEN);
        }
    }

    public static final class OvomorphRenderer extends XenomorphDataDrivenRenderer<OvomorphEntity> {
        public OvomorphRenderer(EntityRendererProvider.Context context) {
            super(context, XenomorphType.OVOMORPH);
        }
    }
}

    @SubscribeEvent
    public static void registerLayers(EntityRenderersEvent.RegisterLayerDefinitions event) {
        ModLogger.info("XenomorphModelLayerBootstrap", "Registering xenomorph model layers");

        event.registerLayerDefinition(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.OVOMORPH_CUSTOM), OvomorphModel::createBodyLayer);

        event.registerLayerDefinition(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.FACEHUGGER_CUSTOM), FacehuggerModel::createBodyLayer);
        event.registerLayerDefinition(Objects.requireNonNull(ModelLayerRegistry.CHESTBURSTER_CUSTOM), ChestbursterModel::createBodyLayer);
    }
}

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphEntity;

/**
 * Entity type registration for Xenomorph and Human entities.
 *
 * <p>Hitbox dimensions come from entity JSON via {@link EntityRegistrationHelper}.
 */
public final class EntityInit {

    @Nonnull
    public static final DeferredRegister<EntityType<?>> ENTITY_TYPES =
            Objects.requireNonNull(DeferredRegister.create(Objects.requireNonNull(Registries.ENTITY_TYPE), ModContext.MOD_ID));

    public static final DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<OvomorphEntity>> OVOMORPH =
            EntityRegistrationHelper.registerEntity(
                    ENTITY_TYPES, "ovomorph", OvomorphEntity::new, MobCategory.CREATURE, XenomorphType.OVOMORPH);

    public static final DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<FacehuggerEntity>> FACEHUGGER =
            EntityRegistrationHelper.registerEntity(
                    ENTITY_TYPES, "facehugger", FacehuggerEntity::new, MobCategory.CREATURE, XenomorphType.FACEHUGGER);

    public static final DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<ChestbursterEntity>> CHESTBURSTER =
            EntityRegistrationHelper.registerEntity(
                    ENTITY_TYPES, "chestburster", ChestbursterEntity::new, MobCategory.MONSTER, XenomorphType.CHESTBURSTER);

    public static final DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<DroneEntity>> DRONE =
            EntityRegistrationHelper.registerEntity(
                    ENTITY_TYPES, "drone", DroneEntity::new, MobCategory.MONSTER, XenomorphType.DRONE);

    public static final DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<GrowthEntity>> GROWTH =
            EntityRegistrationHelper.registerEntity(
                    ENTITY_TYPES, "growth", GrowthEntity::new, MobCategory.MONSTER, XenomorphType.GROWTH);

    public static final DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<QueenEntity>> QUEEN =
            EntityRegistrationHelper.registerEntity(
                    ENTITY_TYPES, "queen", QueenEntity::new, MobCategory.MONSTER, XenomorphType.QUEEN);

    public static final DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<PraetorEntity>> PRAETOR =
            EntityRegistrationHelper.registerEntity(
                    ENTITY_TYPES, "praetor", PraetorEntity::new, MobCategory.MONSTER, XenomorphType.PRAETOR);

    public static final DeferredHolder<EntityType<?>, EntityType<HumanEntity>> HUMAN =
            EntityRegistrationHelper.registerEntity(
                    ENTITY_TYPES, "human", HumanEntity::new, MobCategory.CREATURE, XenomorphType.HUMAN);

    private EntityInit() {
    }

    public static void register(@Nonnull IEventBus modEventBus) {
        ENTITY_TYPES.register(modEventBus);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_5.lifecycle;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.lifecycle.ModServerBootstrap;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.lifecycle.ConfigReloadListener;
import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.common.NeoForge;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.event.AddReloadListenerEvent;

/**
 * Registers NeoForge lifecycle and reload listeners at mod construction.
 */
public final class ReloadListenerBootstrap {

    private ReloadListenerBootstrap() {
    }

    public static void register() {
        NeoForge.EVENT_BUS.addListener(ReloadListenerBootstrap::onAddReloadListeners);
        NeoForge.EVENT_BUS.addListener(ModServerBootstrap::onServerStarting);
        NeoForge.EVENT_BUS.addListener(ModServerBootstrap::onServerTick);
    }

    private static void onAddReloadListeners(@Nonnull AddReloadListenerEvent event) {
        event.addListener(ConfigReloadListener.INSTANCE);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_5.nest;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.structure.NestStructureGenerator;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;
import net.minecraft.server.level.ServerLevel;

/**
 * Nest / hive structure phase placement via {@link NestStructureGenerator}.
 */
public final class NestPortBuildPhases {

    private NestPortBuildPhases() {
    }

    public static boolean buildNestStructurePhase(QueenEntity queen, BlockPos nestPosition, int phase) {
        if (!(queen.level() instanceof ServerLevel serverLevel) || nestPosition == null) {
            return false;
        }
        return NestStructureGenerator.buildNestPhase(serverLevel, nestPosition, phase);
    }

    public static boolean buildHiveStructurePhase(
            QueenEntity queen,
            BlockPos nestPosition,
            int hivePhaseIndex,
            int nestBuildingPhases) {
        if (!(queen.level() instanceof ServerLevel serverLevel) || nestPosition == null) {
            return false;
        }
        return NestStructureGenerator.buildNestPhase(
                serverLevel, nestPosition, hivePhaseIndex + nestBuildingPhases);
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_6.ai;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.CommonGoalRegistrar;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_5.ai.HatchWhenPlayerNearbyGoal;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;

/**
 * Patient Egg AI behavior - stationary, wait for hatching.
 */
public final class PatientEggAI {

    private PatientEggAI() {
    }

    public static void registerGoals(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig.AIGoalsConfig aiGoals) {
        ModLogger.debug("PatientEggAI", "Setting up data-driven egg AI");

        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerFloatGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH, "float"));

        double detectionRange = aiGoals.lookAtPlayerRange;
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerRandomLookAroundGoal(
                entity, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH, "random_look"));
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerLookAtPlayerGoal(
                entity,
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH, "look"),
                (float) detectionRange);

        if (AIConfigHelper.getBoolean(aiGoals.specialAbilities, "proximity_detection", false)) {
            entity.goalSelector.addGoal(
                    GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.OVOMORPH, "hatch"),
                    new HatchWhenPlayerNearbyGoal(entity, detectionRange));
        }

        ModLogger.debug("PatientEggAI", "Egg detection range: " + detectionRange + " blocks (data-driven)");
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_6.client;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModContext;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.ChestbursterEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.DroneEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.FacehuggerEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.client.animation.state.ChestbursterAnimationStateHandler;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.client.animation.state.DroneAnimationStateHandler;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.client.animation.state.FacehuggerAnimationStateHandler;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.client.animation.state.QueenAnimationStateHandler;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.entity.OvomorphEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_5.client.OvomorphAnimationStateHandler;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Entity;
import net.neoforged.api.distmarker.Dist;
import net.neoforged.bus.api.SubscribeEvent;
import net.neoforged.fml.common.EventBusSubscriber;
import net.neoforged.neoforge.event.tick.EntityTickEvent;

/**
 * Client-only animation tick wiring. State handlers live at {@code level_3/.../animation/state}.
 */
@EventBusSubscriber(modid = ModContext.MOD_ID, value = Dist.CLIENT)
public final class XenomorphAnimationClientHooks {

    private XenomorphAnimationClientHooks() {
    }

    @SubscribeEvent
    public static void onEntityTick(EntityTickEvent.Post event) {
        Entity entity = event.getEntity();
        if (!entity.level().isClientSide()) {
            return;
        }
        if (entity instanceof DroneEntity drone) {
            DroneAnimationStateHandler.updateAnimationState(drone);
        } else if (entity instanceof FacehuggerEntity facehugger) {
            FacehuggerAnimationStateHandler.updateAnimationState(facehugger);
        } else if (entity instanceof ChestbursterEntity chestburster) {
            ChestbursterAnimationStateHandler.updateAnimationState(chestburster);
        } else if (entity instanceof OvomorphEntity ovomorph) {
            OvomorphAnimationStateHandler.updateAnimationState(ovomorph);
        } else if (entity instanceof QueenEntity queen) {
            QueenAnimationStateHandler.updateAnimationState(queen);
        }
    }
}

FILE: NestBuildingPortAdapter.java
