package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_6.nest;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.validation.ValidationResult;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.ConfigCacheHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.NestBuildingPort;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.NestBuildingTiming;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.services.BoundaryServices;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.territory.TerritoryValidator;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.territory.TerritoryProgressionSystem;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.nest.NestPortTerritoryBinding;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.nest.NestPortStructureProbe;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_5.nest.NestPortBuildPhases;

import java.util.UUID;

import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;

/**
 * NeoForge adapter for {@link NestBuildingPort}.
 *
 * <p>Delegates structure probe, territory binding, and phase placement to focused helpers.
 * Workflow orchestration is owned by L7 {@code NestBuildingAI}.
 */
public class NestBuildingPortAdapter implements NestBuildingPort {

    private final QueenEntity queen;
    private final EntityConfig config;
    private BlockPos nestPosition;

    public NestBuildingPortAdapter(QueenEntity queen) {
        this.queen = queen;
        this.config = ConfigCacheHelper.getConfig(XenomorphType.QUEEN);
    }

    public NestBuildingTiming timing() {
        return new NestBuildingTiming(
                getNestBuildingPhases(),
                getHiveBuildingPhases(),
                getNestCreationCooldownTicks(),
                getPhaseBuildDelayTicks());
    }

    @Override
    public UUID queenId() {
        return queen.getUUID();
    }

    @Override
    public BlockPosRef queenPosition() {
        return BoundaryRefs.from(queen.blockPosition());
    }

    @Override
    public boolean checkForExistingNest() {
        return hasNestStructureNearby();
    }

    @Override
    public int detectNestProgress() {
        return detectedNestStructureProgress();
    }

    @Override
    public boolean hasNestStructureNearby() {
        return NestPortStructureProbe.hasNestStructureNearby(queen);
    }

    @Override
    public int detectedNestStructureProgress() {
        return NestPortStructureProbe.detectedNestStructureProgress(queen);
    }

    @Override
    public BlockPosRef currentNestCenter() {
        return nestPosition != null ? BoundaryRefs.from(nestPosition) : null;
    }

    @Override
    public void restoreNestState(
            BlockPosRef nestCenter,
            int buildingProgress,
            int hiveBuildingProgress,
            boolean expandingToHive) {
        this.nestPosition = NestPortTerritoryBinding.restoreNestState(queen, nestCenter, expandingToHive);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean validateNestLocation() {
        ValidationResult validation = TerritoryValidator.validateNestLocation(
                BoundaryServices.worldQuery(),
                BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(queen.level()),
                BoundaryRefs.from(queen.blockPosition()));
        return validation.isSuccess();
    }

    @Override
    public void registerTerritory(BlockPosRef nestPos, boolean hiveStage) {
        NestPortTerritoryBinding.registerTerritory(
                queen, nestPos, hiveStage, pos -> this.nestPosition = pos);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean buildNestStructurePhase(int phase) {
        return NestPortBuildPhases.buildNestStructurePhase(queen, nestPosition, phase);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean buildHiveStructurePhase(int hivePhaseIndex) {
        return NestPortBuildPhases.buildHiveStructurePhase(
                queen, nestPosition, hivePhaseIndex, getNestBuildingPhases());
    }

    @Override
    public boolean checkTerritoryProgression() {
        return TerritoryProgressionSystem.checkProgression(
                BoundaryRefs.worldFrom(queen.level()), queen.getUUID());
    }

    @Override
    public void onHiveStructureComplete() {
        TerritoryProgressionSystem.updateStructureToHive(queen.getUUID());
    }

    private int getNestBuildingPhases() {
        return AIConfigHelper.requireIntFromSpecialAbilities(config, "nest_building_phases");
    }

    private int getHiveBuildingPhases() {
        return AIConfigHelper.requireIntFromSpecialAbilities(config, "hive_building_phases");
    }

    private int getNestCreationCooldownTicks() {
        return AIConfigHelper.requireIntFromSpecialAbilities(config, "nest_creation_cooldown");
    }

    private int getPhaseBuildDelayTicks() {
        return AIConfigHelper.requireIntFromSpecialAbilities(config, "phase_build_delay");
    }
}

FILE: NestBuildingAI.java
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_7;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_0.spatial.BlockPosRef;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.hive.QueenNestProgress;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.territory.QueenNestRegistry;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_1.hive.NestBuildingWorkflow;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.boundary.BoundaryRefs;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_6.nest.NestBuildingPortAdapter;
import net.minecraft.core.BlockPos;

/**
 * Thin L7 shell over {@link NestBuildingWorkflow} + {@link NestBuildingPortAdapter}.
 * Implements {@link QueenNestProgress}; goal construction lives in composition (L8).
 */
public class NestBuildingAI implements QueenNestProgress {

    private final QueenEntity queen;
    private final NestBuildingPortAdapter portAdapter;
    private final NestBuildingWorkflow workflow;

    public NestBuildingAI(QueenEntity queen) {
        this.queen = queen;
        this.portAdapter = new NestBuildingPortAdapter(queen);
        this.workflow = new NestBuildingWorkflow(portAdapter, portAdapter.timing());
    }

    @Override
    public void tick() {
        if (queen.level().isClientSide()) {
            return;
        }
        workflow.tick();
    }

    @Override
    public void restoreNestState(
            BlockPosRef nestCenter,
            int buildingProgress,
            int hiveBuildingProgress,
            boolean expandingToHive) {
        workflow.restoreFromSave(nestCenter, buildingProgress, hiveBuildingProgress, expandingToHive);
    }

    public boolean hasNest() {
        return QueenNestRegistry.hasNest(queen.getUUID());
    }

    public BlockPos getNestPosition() {
        BlockPosRef ref = QueenNestRegistry.getNestCenter(queen.getUUID());
        return ref != null ? BoundaryRefs.toBlockPos(ref) : null;
    }

    @Override
    public int getBuildingProgress() {
        return workflow.getBuildingProgress();
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isNestComplete() {
        return workflow.isNestComplete();
    }

    @Override
    public int getHiveBuildingProgress() {
        return workflow.getHiveBuildingProgress();
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isExpandingToHive() {
        return workflow.isExpandingToHive();
    }

    public boolean isHiveExpansionComplete() {
        return workflow.isHiveExpansionComplete();
    }
}

FILE: QueenCompositionStrategy.java

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_8;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.AIConfigHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_1.entity.ConfigCacheHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_2_systems.level_0.ai.GoalPriorityResolver;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.AICompositionStrategy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.CommonGoalRegistrar;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_0.ai.NestBuildingGoal;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.StandardTargetingHelper;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.ai.shared.SurvivalAIGoal;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.queen.QueenAvoidanceAI;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.queen.WanderNearNestGoal;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_7.NestBuildingAI;
import java.util.Objects;
import net.minecraft.world.entity.Mob;

/**
 * Queen goal composition — survival, nest building, avoidance, and territory patrol.
 */
public final class QueenCompositionStrategy implements AICompositionStrategy {

    private static final QueenCompositionStrategy INSTANCE = new QueenCompositionStrategy();

    public static void registerGoals(QueenEntity queen) {
        INSTANCE.applyGoals(queen);
    }

    @Override
    public void applyGoals(Mob mob) {
        if (!(mob instanceof QueenEntity queen)) {
            return;
        }

        EntityConfig config = ConfigCacheHelper.getConfig(XenomorphType.QUEEN);

        queen.goalSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.QUEEN, "survival"), new SurvivalAIGoal(queen));

        NestBuildingAI nestBuildingAI = queen.getNestProgress() instanceof NestBuildingAI existing
                ? existing
                : null;
        if (nestBuildingAI == null) {
            nestBuildingAI = new NestBuildingAI(queen);
            queen.setNestProgress(nestBuildingAI);
        }
        queen.goalSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.QUEEN, "nest"), new NestBuildingGoal(nestBuildingAI));

        QueenAvoidanceAI avoidanceAI = queen.getAvoidanceAI() instanceof QueenAvoidanceAI existingAvoidance
                ? existingAvoidance
                : new QueenAvoidanceAI(queen);
        queen.goalSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.QUEEN, "avoidance"),
                Objects.requireNonNull(avoidanceAI.createGoal()));

        queen.goalSelector.addGoal(
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.QUEEN, "wander_near_nest"),
                new WanderNearNestGoal(queen));

        double strollSpeed = config.aiGoals.strollSpeed;
        int strollInterval = AIConfigHelper.requireIntFromSpecialAbilities(config, "stroll_interval");
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerRandomStrollGoal(
                queen,
                GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.QUEEN, "stroll"),
                strollSpeed,
                strollInterval);

        float lookRange = config.aiGoals.lookAtPlayerRange;
        CommonGoalRegistrar.registerLookAtPlayerGoal(
                queen, GoalPriorityResolver.priority(XenomorphType.QUEEN, "look"), lookRange);

        StandardTargetingHelper.registerStandardTargetingGoals(queen, XenomorphType.QUEEN);
    }

    @Override
    public String strategyName() {
        return "queen";
    }
}

package com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_9;

import com.weylandyutani.layer_0_domain.level_1.entity.XenomorphType;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfig;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.entity.EntityConfigStorage;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_1_infrastructure.level_0.platform.ModLogger;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai.growth_PLANNED.PassiveDevelopmentAI;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_1.ai.praetor_PLANNED.StrategicCommanderAI;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.ai.drone.DroneSwarmGoalRegistrar;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.ai.facehugger.FacehuggerStealthGoalRegistrar;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.ai.queen.HiveMotherAI;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.ai.shared.StandardAI;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.ChestbursterEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.DroneEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.FacehuggerEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_2.species.xenomorph.entity.QueenEntity;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_3.species.xenomorph.ai.chestburster.ChestbursterEscapeGoalRegistrar;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.ai.chestburster.ChestbursterCompositionStrategy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.ai.drone.DroneCompositionStrategy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_4.species.xenomorph.ai.facehugger.FacehuggerCompositionStrategy;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_6.ai.PatientEggAI;
import com.weylandyutani.layer_3_minecraft.level_8.QueenCompositionStrategy;

import net.minecraft.world.entity.PathfinderMob;

/**
 * Single owner for xenomorph AI goal registration.
 * Routes exclusively by entity JSON {@code ai_goals.behavior_type}; composition strategies are
 * leaf registrars invoked by that switch (no parallel {@link XenomorphType} router).
 */
public final class XenomorphCompositionDispatch {

    private XenomorphCompositionDispatch() {
    }

    public static void registerGoals(PathfinderMob entity, XenomorphType type) {
        BehaviorFactory.registerAIBehavior(entity, type);
    }

    /** Config-driven {@code behavior_type} routing — sole registration authority. */
    private static final class BehaviorFactory {

        private BehaviorFactory() {
        }

        static void registerAIBehavior(PathfinderMob entity, XenomorphType xenomorphType) {
            EntityConfig config = EntityConfigStorage.getConfig(xenomorphType);

            if (config == null || config.aiGoals == null) {
                ModLogger.warn("XenomorphCompositionDispatch", "No AI goals config found for " + xenomorphType);
                return;
            }

            String behaviorType = config.aiGoals.behaviorType;
            if (behaviorType == null || behaviorType.isBlank()) {
                ModLogger.warn("XenomorphCompositionDispatch",
                        "No behavior type specified for " + xenomorphType + " — contract should reject at load");
                return;
            }
            ModLogger.debug("XenomorphCompositionDispatch",
                    "Registering AI behavior: " + behaviorType + " for " + xenomorphType);

            switch (behaviorType) {
                case "stealthy_hunter" -> registerStealthyHunter(entity, config);
                case "escape_and_hide" -> registerEscapeAndHide(entity, config);
                case "passive_development" -> PassiveDevelopmentAI.registerGoals(entity, config.aiGoals);
                case "swarm_killer" -> registerSwarmKiller(entity, config);
                case "strategic_commander" -> StrategicCommanderAI.registerGoals(entity, config.aiGoals);
                case "hive_mother", "aggressive_queen" -> registerHiveMother(entity, config);
                case "patient_egg" -> PatientEggAI.registerGoals(entity, config.aiGoals);
                default -> {
                    ModLogger.warn("XenomorphCompositionDispatch",
                            "Unknown behavior type: " + behaviorType + " for " + xenomorphType);
                    StandardAI.registerGoals(entity, xenomorphType, config.aiGoals);
                }
            }
        }

        private static void registerStealthyHunter(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig config) {
            // Live facehugger product path is attachment composition; thin stealth registrar remains for non-FH.
            if (entity instanceof FacehuggerEntity facehugger) {
                FacehuggerCompositionStrategy.registerGoals(facehugger);
            } else {
                FacehuggerStealthGoalRegistrar.registerGoals(entity, config.aiGoals);
            }
        }

        private static void registerEscapeAndHide(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig config) {
            if (entity instanceof ChestbursterEntity chestburster) {
                ChestbursterCompositionStrategy.registerGoals(chestburster);
            } else {
                ChestbursterEscapeGoalRegistrar.registerGoals(entity, config.aiGoals);
            }
        }

        private static void registerSwarmKiller(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig config) {
            if (entity instanceof DroneEntity drone) {
                DroneCompositionStrategy.registerGoals(drone);
            } else {
                DroneSwarmGoalRegistrar.registerGoals(entity, config.aiGoals);
            }
        }

        private static void registerHiveMother(PathfinderMob entity, EntityConfig config) {
            if (entity instanceof QueenEntity queen) {
                QueenCompositionStrategy.registerGoals(queen);
            } else {
                HiveMotherAI.registerGoals(entity, config.aiGoals);
            }
        }
    }
}
